sanatkumāra saṃhitāyāṃ
śrīgaṇeśāyanamaḥ
prapadyedevamī śānaṃsarvajñamaparājitam
saṃbhavaṃsarvabhūtānāmanādiviśvatomukham
vedādauyaḥsvaraḥproktaoṃkārākhyomaheśvaraḥ
sṛjate sarvabhūtānipaṃcabhūtaiḥsadāśivaḥ
sāṃkhyānāṃparamaṃyogaṃvrataiḥpāśupataistathā
rakṣārtha sarvajaṃtūnāṃtridhātmānaṃ sṛjatyajaḥ
sasaṃjñayātubhagavānekaevama heśvaraḥ
prajvalaṃtaṃ mahāśūlaṃghorarūpaṃ mahāśanim
nānākrīḍanakairdevaḥ krīḍateyogamāyayā
dayitārdhavapuḥrutvānṛtyāraṃbhesthitoharaḥ
tadbhaktyāsaṃpravakṣyāmipurāṇaṃśivabhāṣitam
parāśarasyadāyādaḥśrīmānsatyavatīsutaḥ
brahmarṣiḥ sacadharmātmākālayogavidāṃvaraḥ
ṛṣisaṃdhaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śrutairivapitāmahaḥ
bhārateśatasāhakhyāṃsaṃhitāyāṃkavīśvaraḥ
caturdhāvyasyamatimāniiśaṣyāṃścā'dhyāpayatpṛthak
teṣāṃsukhopaviṣṭānāṃ kathāṃ kathayatāṃ parām
tatra cādhyātmadharmātmābrahmaṇastanayaḥ śubhaḥ
anugrahārthamṭaṣīṇāṃ darśanaṃ kṛtavānṛṣiḥ
sadadarśasukhāsīnān brahmarṣīnamitaujasaḥ
arghyamācamanīyaṃcateṣāṃdattaṃcadharmavit
tataḥ saṃpūjayāmāsavalapīnsaṃśi tavratān
anujñātaścataiḥ sarvairupaviṣṭaḥ kuśāsane
pṛṣṭastuṛṣibhistatratra hmaputromahāmuniḥ
prāsādasyacayatpuṇyaṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ
mūrtīnāṃtu vibhāgasya maṃtrasya paramaṃvidhim
sthānānityaṣṭāvasyāpirudrasyatumahātmanaḥ
upaviṣṭaistu bhagavān yogīśobrahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ
tapoveṣānurūpeṣu āsaneṣu yathāyatham
virājatyadhikaṃbrahmātaiśvavahmarṣibhiḥ sadā
satāṃmadhyeca dharmātmā bhagavāntsūkṣmayogavit
kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve ṛṣayastamathābruvan
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃ hitāyāṃprathamo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣayaūcuḥ
śaivaṃ purāṇaṃde vasyayadvṛttaṃtadbravīhinaḥ
śaivaṃ purāṇaṃbhavataḥ śṛṇudhvaṃdvijasattamāḥ
yacchrutvā nirmalāḥ saṃtastaccittāstatparāyaṇāḥ
bhavaṃtibhāvitātmānaḥ kṛtakṛtyāviśeṣataḥ
sva rgakāmapradaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇīyasanatkumārasaṃhitāvivṛtau prathamodhyāyaḥ
oṃoṃnamaḥ śivāya athadvitīyeṛṣibhiḥ pṛṣṭobrahmasutobravīt
pāvanaṃśraddadhānānāmihaloke paratraca
prakṛtyārthādhikāreṇapradhānapurupeśvara
kīrtayiṣyāmivoviprāḥ purāṇaṃśivabhāpitam
śrutaṃpurāmayāvyāsāddevadevasya dhīmataḥ
yadahaṃtatpravakṣyāmiyathā pūrvaśrutaṃ mayā
saṃkṣepāccaivavakṣyāmipṛthivyādiyathātathā
saptadvīpasyacākhyānaṃvarṣāṇāṃcatathaivaca
sana tkumāravikāṃtaṃrudrasyavihitaṃkṛtam
ārādhitaṃ mahādevaṃbrahmaṇastanayenatu
varadānenasaṃbaṃdhomuniśiṣyasamāgamaḥ
bhavanaṃmeruśṛṃgasyabrahmaviṣṇumaheśvarān
vibhīṣaṇasya saṃvādaṃ rudrasya ca mahātmanaḥ
sarvatīrthaphalaṃpuṇyaṃśiva liṃgasyapūjanam
liṃgārcanavidhiṃcaiva devasya pūjanaṃtathā
prāsādasya caya tpuṇyaṃmahādevasyadhīmataḥ
sthānādijyaiṣṭhyamasyāpirūpasya tu mahātmanaḥ
liṃgasaṃsthāpanepuṇyaṃ puṣpadānasya yatphalam
dhūpasyaca vidhiṃcaivamāsānāṃcaparaṃphalam
yathādvādaśajyotirligādīnām
caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyāṃ vidhāne vihitephalam
nāmāṣṭamīvidhānaṃ catathāvailakṣaṇāṣṭamīm
vibhūtiṃdevadevasyaīśvara syacadhīmataḥ
yoganāḍyāstathākhyānaṃmayāproktaṃ purātanam
avimu ktasyamāhātmyaṃtathācoṃkāravarṇanam
yajñeśvarasyamāhātmyaṃta thātīrthānuvarṇanam
bhagavadārādhanaṃnaṃdestathānaṃyabhiṣe canam
nīlakaṃṭhasya māhātmyaṃtripurasya tathāvadhaḥ
vāsudevasya māhātmyaṃvidhānaṃcaivatasyaca
jñānapraśaṃsanaṃcaiva mokṣaṃ paramasaṃpadam
idānīṃvi staraṃcitraṃvibhāgaṃrūpamaiśvaram
āsīttamomayaṃ sarvamaprajñātamalakṣaṇam
ātmanāsarvamātmānaṃsaṃciṃtyabhagavānharaḥ
manaḥsaṃsṛjate pūrva mahaṃkāraṃtupṛṣṭhataḥ
ahaṃkārātprajātānimahā bhūtānipaṃcaca
aṣṭauprakṛtayaḥ proktāvikārāścaiva ṣoḍaśa
śabdaḥsparśaśvarūpaṃcarasogaṃdhastathaiva ca
prāṇopānaḥ samā naśvaudānovyānaevaca
satvaṃrajastamaścaiva guṇāḥproktāstutetrayaḥ
tasmādbhagavato brahmātasmādviṣṇurajāyata
tasmātparataraṃnāsti nāstitasmātparaṃśivam
brahmāviṣṇuśrvadvāvetāvudbhūtauśaṃkarā ttutau
tapasāharatecaivanānābhūtānisarvaśaḥ
dinaikaṃbrahmaṇaḥ proktaṃniśākalpastathācyate
evaṃmāsaṃcavarṣacatathāvarṣaśataṃdvijāḥ
evamādiparārdhītoharasyani miṣaḥsmṛtaḥ
brahmādistaṃbaparyaṃtaṃnimiṣaśca maheśvaraḥ
nimiṣaṃjīvitaṃ sarva caṃdrādīnāṃ grahaiḥ saha
pātālaṃsutalaṃtālaṃvitalaṃtalamevaca
paṃcamaṃviddhipātālaṃrukmasauvarṇikaṃ smṛtam
saptamaṃśarkarābhūmiraṣṭamaṃvijayaṃsmṛtam
eteṣudharma prakhyātā aṣṭaupātālavāsinaḥ
eṣāmādaucama dhyeca aṃte rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
evaṃ prakurute lokānkrīḍārthaṃ tumaheśvaraḥ
brahmalokaparīmāṇagatirūrdhvavivarṇitā
pṛthi vīcāṃtarikṣaṃcadiśaśrvavidiśastathā
samuccayaṃgirīṇāṃca anukramaṇasaṃkhyayā
samudrāṇāṃcavistāraṃpramāṇaṃcata thāśṭaṇu
sthāvarāṇāṃcarāṇāṃ cadevānāṃca divaukasām
catuṣpādadvipādānāṃ dhārmikān karmamokṣakān
sa hasraguṇamākhyātaṃsthāvarāṇāṃprakīrtitam
sahasaṃpādahīnāśvaityāha bhagavāśivaḥ
maheśvaraḥ parasteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃdeva mānuṣāt
evaṃ saṃkhyā'trasaṃkhyātāsarvajñenasvayaṃbhuvā
eṣāṃmāheśvaraṃ jñānaṃbhaktimaṃtraiḥ prakīrtitam
ekaṃjñānaṃnamasyaṃtiabhūtaṃbhūtasaṃjñakam
nirguṇaṃnirmalaṃjñānaṃśaṃkareṇapracoditam
ṛṣīṇāṃ śrotukāmānāṃ bhaktā nāṃcadṛḍhavrata
śrāvitaṃjñāna sarvasvaṃ purāṇeṣucagīyate
tatojñānaṃparaṃ śreṣṭha proktamīśena dhīmatā
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya sarvavarṇeviśeṣataḥ
yathāsaṃbhavatijñānaṃtathāīśaḥpravartate
ahamādiśvamadhyaṃca ahaṃcatecasaṃsthitaḥ
krīḍā rthamīhatevyāsa utpannamatiravyayaḥ
tataḥkālohibhagavān sobhidhyāyaśivājñayā
sṛṣṭituprathamaṃ kurvanprakṛtināmanāmataḥ
tasmādbrahmāpraka tyāstu utpannaḥsahaviṣṇunā
pādahīnānkṣaciyāṃśvatasmāddhīnāṃstu vaiśya kān
caturthapādahīnāṃśva ācāraiśvavahiṣkṛtān
pṛthivīṃcāṃ tarikṣaṃcadiśaścaiva makalpayat
lokālokasya saṃkhyānaṃ dvipadāmuddhestathā
saritāṃsāgarāṇāṃcatīrthānyāyatanāni ca
ulkānipātaṃ ketuṃ ca jyotiṣāṃpatanānyapi
evaṃsarvārthasaṣṭāvai codyamānaḥ śivenavai
utpannaṃ caiva tatsarvaṃ bhūyaḥ kālena pīḍyate
vyāsauvā ca
kathaṃbrahmāsamutpannaḥkathaṃ sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate
āsīttamomayaṃcaitannaprājñāyata kiṃcana
tataḥ śivomahādevoyogadhṛksatusarvaśaḥ
tasmātpṛthvītvamāpannaṃtasmādāpa statobhuvaḥ
tattamodārayāmāsa āpobhūtvātuśaṃkaraḥ
tasmāttuteja sācaivavāyunācasadākṣipan
tasmādaṃḍa samutpattistatonārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
apāṃcāgneyvasaṃyogādagnistejaśvasaṃbhavaḥ
vāyorapivikurvāṇādākāśamabhavattadā
saṃghātaśvā'bhavatpṛthvīeṣāmāheśvarītanuḥ
atrapraviśyahijalaṃ nimiṣārdhapramāṇataḥ
tatobrahmāsamutpanno adbhirnārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
tasmi naṃḍesa bhagavānuṣitvāparivatsarān
tatovaibrāhmaṇojajñekālekālenacoditaḥ
athavyomadiśaśvā'ṣṭau apāṃsthānaṃ caśāśvataṃ
tataḥsakālamadhyetuso'thassṛṣṭimathā'karot
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyāṃ ddi tīyo'dhyāyaḥ
mahatastutatobrahmātasmādrahmāṃḍatāṃ gataḥ
samudrā stasyarudhiramākāśamudaraṃtathā
pavanaścaivaniḥśvāsastejonirnimnagārasaḥ
ākāśatamasīśrotre caṃdrārkaunayanausmṛ tau
pṛthivyaṃte samudrāśvasamudrāṃtetamaḥsmṛtam
rasātalāṃtesalilaṃtasyatipannagādhipāḥ
tadaṃtepunarākāśaṃtasyāpyaṃte punarjalam
tejasoṃtetadā pṛthvīpṛthvīsamabhirāṭatā
aṃḍasyadhāraṇātsadma mahataśvamahātmanaḥ
evaṃ brahmāṃḍamityuktaṃ mahādhāraṇamucyate
yoyathāyasya yonitvetaṃpravakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ
āponareṇavaissṛṣṭā āpovai narasū navaḥ
tāyadasyāyanaṃ pūrvatena nārāyaṇaḥsmṛtaḥ
tadālokāstatojīvāḥ satvāḥpaṃcātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ
jarāyujāṃḍajodbhijjāḥ svedajāścacaturvidhāḥ
ṣṭavidhādevayonirmānuṣāstvekavidhayā
mānuṣyaṃcaikavidhaṃtucāturvarṇyamanekadhā
pṛthivīcāṃtarikṣaṃcatridivaṃbhuvanaṃ smṛtam
pṛthivyāstuparīmāṇebhūyastulyovidhiḥsmṛtaḥ
ekaṃtukoṭyāvikhyātamevaṃtribhuvanaṃmataṃ
rudrāṇāṃ koṭirekātupure cāṃtarvyavasthitā
bahmā viṣṇuśrvadvāvetauupāsāte maheśvaram
pṛthivyādiprasaṃkhyānaṃ tapasāsamudāhṛtam
tadidaṃsaṃpravakṣyāmi puruṣāllokaviśrutān
śivakrīḍanasaṃsthānaṃśive naparikalpitam
kāmārādhanakaṃśaṃbhoḥ pūjanaṃdvīpavāsibhiḥ
sārdhapaṃcā śītiśatayojanādivisāriṣu
jaṃbūdvīpādidvīpeṣumayāvyāptamidaṃ dvija
jaṃbūddīpe mahādevogomedegirijeśvaraḥ
śālmalidvīpamadhyasthādevaḥ paśupatiḥ svayam
kuśadvīpeharo bhūtvā krauṃce proktovṛṣadhvajaḥ
śākeśaṃkaranāmā yaṃpuṣkarebhālalocanaḥ
tatratatra mahādevaṃ pūjayaṃtaḥ sthirānabahūn
bhogānmahauṣadhīstebhyaḥ prāpnuvaṃtiśivājñayā
jaṃbūddīpaścagomedaḥśālmaliścakuśastathā
krauṃcadvīpastathāśākaḥ puṣkaraḥ samamaḥ smṛtaḥ
ataḥparaṃpravakṣyāmiddīpā nāṃtupṛthakpṛthak
parimāṇaṃcasaṃkhyāṃcadvīpapravaramevaca
jaṃbūdvīpe jaṃbuvṛkṣoyojanai staṃnibodhata
sahasraṃśa tamekaṃcayojanānāṃsamucchritaḥ
tasyajaṃbūphalarasaścāmṛtasvādurucyate
pramāṇādā yatodvīpodviguṇaḥ pariṇāhataḥ
dviguṇena samudreṇalavaṇenasamāvṛtaḥ
tasyavarṣāṇi samehakāmagāścayathārhataḥ
bhāratasya varṣasyanavabhedāḥ prakī titāḥ
saptavargāḥprasaṃkhyātāḥ samaiva kulaparvatāḥ
dakṣiṇenavisaṃ khyātamilāvattaṃprakīrtitam
uttaraṃ dakṣiṇaṃcaiva iṃdradhanvākṛtiryathā
catvārodroṇa saṃsthānāṃvarṣāṇāṃcapramāṇataḥ
girivarṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣobhārataṃda kṣiṇenatu
pūrveṇamālyavāṃścaivapaścimegaṃdhamādanaḥ
nīlaḥ parvatarājaśvaśvetaḥ śuklomahāgiriḥ
śṛṃgāduttarataḥpārśvesamaṃtātsamupotthitau
sahasrāṇāṃ pramaṃkhyānaṃkālajñānaviśāradaiḥ
ta sminjaṃbūdaketyeva kanakaṃdevabhūṣaṇam
tasyajaṃbūttarepārśvamerurnāma mahāgiriḥ
meruṃpradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jaṃbūmūlaviśe spunaḥ
yojanānāṃsahasrāṇi caturaśītirucchrayaḥ
adhastāddaśasahasrāṇiṣa viṃśaścaivapārśvataḥ
meruṃpradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā kailāsākhyastatogiriḥ
caturaśītistatovyāsogirīṃdrasya mahātmanaḥ
tasyasānuṣucitreṣukaṃdareṣudarīṣuca
tatrāyatijitakrodhājitalobhājiteṃdriyāḥ
yegṛhasthāḥsvadharmajñāgo brāhmaṇahite ratāḥ
teyāṃtiparamaṃsthānaṃprasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
śataṃśatasahasrāṇiyojanānāṃsamaṃtataḥ
nīlava niṣadhaścaivahemakūṭaścaparvataḥ
himavāndakṣiṇepārśvetābatparamamucchritaḥ
paṃcaviṃśatsahasrāṇivistareṇasadocya te
tathaivavakṣasiṃdhuśvatisrastāvaipratīcyagāḥ
nalinīmha dinī caivaplāvanī caiva pūrvagāḥ
gaṃgāyātusamaṃtāsāṃ jaṃbūddī pasaridvarā
gaṃgāsamānarūpāśrvapuṇyatīryaśiloccayāḥ
devatīryāḥ supuṇyāśvapṛthivyāma nukīrtitāḥ
jaṃbūdvīpaḥprasaṃkhyātoyāthātathyenavaidvijāḥ
paṇṇāmitaradvīpānāṃśeṣaṃprāmāṇyataḥ śṛṇu
jaṃbūdvīpapramā ṇenadviguṇāṃtarataḥ smṛtaḥ
uttareṇa smṛtāḥ sarve aṃtare svargavāsinaḥ
dvīpādvīpa samānasyanāmadheyāni sarvaśaḥ
kṣāraikṣuḥ surāsarpirdadhyodānāmanāmataḥ
maṃḍodaśca prasaṃkhyātastataḥ svādakottaraḥ
dvīpānāṃ sahasrāṇi avijñā tānitāni tu
sataivatusamāsena vyākhyātānimayādvijāḥ
apivarṣaśatairviprānaśakyaṃ kathituṃmayā
lakṣadvīpekṣa saḥśālmaleśālmaliḥsmṛtaḥ
kuśadvīpe kuśastaṃ vaḥ krauṃcadvīpe mahāgiriḥ
śākadvīpeśākavṛkṣaḥ puṣkarapuṣkaraḥsmṛtaḥ
jaṃbūvṛkṣapramāṇena dviguṇottarataḥ smṛtāḥ
sarveṣāmevavṛkṣāṇāmamṛtasvādaucyate
taṃtupītvāmṭatarasaṃ dīrghāyuṣṭavaṃ cagacchati
nānyaṃpriyaṃvijānaṃtica kravākasadharmiṇaḥ
sarvāṃmaṇimayībhūmiḥ sūkṣmakāṃcanavālukā
sarvakālaphalāvṛkṣāḥ svasvagaṃdhaphalāśrayāḥ
sarve pāṃcaivadvīpānāṃ saptānāṃ kulaparvatāḥ
sanaiva nadyasteṣāṃtusamaiva kalpitāḥ śubhāḥ
tāsāṃnadyupanadyastuśataśotha sahasraśaḥ teṣāṃ parvatarājānaṃparivārya samaṃtataḥ
raṃjitāḥśṛṃgavaṃtaśvaśobhategirayastathā
tataḥsiddhāśvaṛṣayogaṃdharvādānavāḥ khagāḥ
mahākalpetudatyaṃteityāha bhagavānaśivaḥ
teṣāṃparvatajālānidīpyantiprabhayāsvayā
vṛtāḥ parvatarājā naṃparivārya samaṃtataḥ
ṣaṣṭiṃgirisahasrāṇiete tasya samaṃtadā
tatratepuruṣā divyāḥśukladaṃtāḥpriyaṃvadāḥ
teṣāṃnaduḥkhaṃnaglānirnakaścitparibādhate
teṣudvīpeṣujāyaṃtepuruṣāste tapodhanāḥ
dīrghāyuṣvaṃtaṃteṣāṃ vidyatekāmagāgatiḥ
jaṃbūdvīpasyaparyāyaṃkathayiṣyāmivaidvijāḥ
mānuṣāṇāṃcavarṣāṇayugānāṃcaivasaṃkhyayā
kīrtayiṣyāmivāviprāḥ purāṇaṃ yadvibhāvyate
aṣṭavarṣasahasrāṃtakālaṃkṛtayugaṃviduḥ
lakṣādvādaśavaiproktāḥ ṣaṭsahasrāṇivatsarāḥ
tretā yugasyaprāmāṇyaṃpurāṇe parikīrtitam
aṣṭavarṣasahasrāṃtālakṣāśvāṣṭauprakīrtitāḥ
lakṣāśvāṣṭaucala kṣaudyau ayutedvatayaivaca
aṣṭavarṣasahasratikālaḥ kaliyugesṭataḥ
evamādi cavarṣacatathāvarṣaśataṃdvijāḥ
evamāyurjiteṃdrasya harasyanimiṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
brahmādistaṃbaparyaṃtaṃnimiṣotpattirīśvaraḥ
nimeṣajīvinaḥ sarve caṃdrādityau gṛhaiḥ saha
mahākalpaṃcavikhyātaṃśivasya nimiṣastathā
dvīpānāṃcaivavarṣāṇāṃ kathayāmisamāsataḥ
anyeṣāṃ caivadvīpānāṃ vivi dhāvihitāgatiḥ
bhāratasya varṣasyanavabhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
iṃdradvīpaḥ kaśeruśvatāmraparṇogabhastimān
nāgaddīpasta thāsaumyogāṃdharvaśrvāraṇastathā
ayaṃtunavabhasteṣāṃdvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃgataḥ
svādūdakonāmanāmnāsāgarottaratomahān
tasyacādyāparāpṛthvīdviguṇena pramāṇataḥ
tasmātparaṃcavailokolokālokaścanāmataḥ
lokānviśatitallo kṛpramāṇaṃlokavistarāt
manasāsiddhisaṃpannānīrogāśvirajīvinaḥ
prākārasthitayaścaiva sauvarṇāśvasahārṇavāḥ
lokeśāścaiva catvārolokālokesthitāstathā
evaṃ sabhuvivistārastriguṇaḥ parimāṇataḥ
itiśrīśiva mahā purāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ saptadvīpavarṇanaṃnāmatṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ
pṛthivyāstumayākhyāto vistāro dīrghatātathā
adhastādyatpravakṣyāmipa tālatalavāsinām
tatra bhogavatīramyānānāratnopaśobhitā
sarve canāgarājānāṃviśramaṃtemudānvitāḥ
tatrasiddhāmunigaṇā bharatādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
kāliyaḥ pavanonāmanāgaḥ pūraṇaevaca
maṇimālaścaiva bhadronāgaścaivātha kauśikaḥ
vasuśvabaṃdhumāraśvakaṃ balāśvatarāvubhau
karavīra puṃḍarī kausaṃvato'thamahoragaḥ
yecā'nyenāgapata yo anaṃtāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
purībhogavatī ramyānānāratnopaśobhitā
vicitrābhiḥ patākābhirvimānaiśvasahasraśaḥ
dolālaṃbitavāsāśvamuktādāmairalaṃkṛtāḥ
hāsya nāṭya vicitrābhirgānavāditraniḥkhanaiḥ
sarvakāmaprasiddhārthāḥ striya śvāpsarasopamāḥ
naivateṣāṃ bhavedglānirnaśokonajarātathā
īrṣyāyāśca bhayaṃ nāsti sarva kāma hite ratāḥ
puṣṭidānasyara hitāḥ sarva kāmeṣu pūjitāḥ
tatra bhogavatī ramyāprabhālokā dviśiṣyate
tatrastaṃbha sahakhāṇi sauvarṇānisamaṃtataḥ
vajravaiḍūryakalpānimahāratnāniśobhitā
iṃdranīla mahānīlaiḥ sarvataśvābhimaṃḍitā
sarvakālaphalānayaḥ sarvapāyasa kardamāḥ
kulyāśvaghṛtasaṃpūrṇāḥ sadāvṛkṣopaśobhitāḥ
annaparvatakūṭāśca śaṃkha kuṃdeṃdu pāṃḍurāḥ
kalpitābrahmaṇā pūrṇāḥ śaṃkarasyājñayāpurā
payasānityapūrṇānibhājanāni samaṃtataḥ
madhukulyāca saṃnyastāraktadaṃtātiśobhitāḥ
priyaṃvadāstathācānyābhāryāyauvanasaṃpadaḥ
bhuktābhuktāḥ priyaistatrayonistāsāṃnacakṣatā
prasūtāyāstukanyāyāyau vanaṃnāpihīyate
parastriyonajānaṃ tisvadāraniratāḥ sadā
iṣṭabhuksvajanākīrṇānāgaloke prakīrtitāḥ
ūrdhvatirya ggatiḥkhyātātāsāṃtaṣāmanekaśaḥ
nāgalokasya vistāraṃ dviguṇaṃ parikīrtitam
ekadeśapramāṇenamayākhyātaṃyathāta thā
yojanaiḥ koṭire kātunāgalokaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
ūrdhvatiryakprasaṃkhyātaṃcaturasraṃtathā dvijāḥ
anaṃtaraṃpravakṣyā mihiraṇyapuravāsinām
tatrāpi koṭiḥ saṃkhyātāyojanaiḥ parimāṇataḥ
tatrāsansaphalāvaṃkṣāḥpuṣpaiścaiva sugaṃdhinaḥ
nānāvicitranirghoṣaniḥsvanaiḥ pūrṇakaṃdaraiḥ
yauvanasthāḥ striyastatrasukumā rāḥpriyaṃvadāḥ
puruṣārūpasaṃpannāḥsvadāranirateṃdriyāḥ
sauvarṇāśvagṛhāstatra mānaśuścairvibhūṣitāḥ
vimānacāriṇaḥ sarvesarve casthitayauvanāḥ
akṣatapratimāstatrastriyaṃśvāpsarasopamāḥ
śukladaṃtāṃbaradharā ścaṃdrāṃśuvimalaprabhāḥ
manoramāḥsusiddhārthāścakravākasadharmiṇaḥ
nodvegonaca kopastu īrṣyāsūyāvivarjitāḥ
varṣairanekaiḥsaṃkhyātāguṇāstasmimpurottame
daityāstatrava saṃtye teprahādādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
teṣāṃ prasādājjīvaṃtisarva lokāṃnasaṃśayaḥ
brahmādyādevatāḥ sarvādhāryatesamanaṃtaram
parāparāṇāṃlokānāṃdhāraṇairlokadhāraṇaiḥ
sarvānimāndhārayatisurabhirnāmanāmataḥ
pṛthvīṃdhārayatisarvāṃsudhanvā nāmanāmataḥ
sarvāgaśvasusarvāgaḥ sulabhācottarāṃ diśaṃ
dakṣiṇāṃ caṣakānāmadhārayaṃtidiśaṃsadā
teṣāṃ prasādājjī vaṃtibrahmādyāstridivaukasaḥ
tasminadivyāniveśmāni citrāṇicalaghūnica
patākādhvajacitrāṇiprāsādānāṃca paṃktayaḥ
sarvakāmaphalāvṛkṣāramyāśvitrāścapādapāḥ
svargādatitarāṃ ramyā sukhasparśājalāśayāḥ
kāmyānāmapurotyeṣāsadāsaṃpūrṇamānasā
brahmaṇāvihitāpūrva kāmarūpaguṇānvitā
pāyasenacapūrṇānibhājanā nisahasraśaḥ
sarvaicaivasukhasparśāśvāraṇasyāpiveśmani
prāsādapaṃ ktayobhāṃtiśaradīva nhṛdāḥ śubhāḥ
amṛtānicakuṃḍānidiśodivyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
pāyasena ca pūrṇāni bhājanānisaha sraśaḥ
saṃnyastānicadṛśyate aṃbudivyāmṛtopamam
bhaktānānāvidhāstatrabhūṣaṇāḥpūrṇa kalpitāḥ
naśakyānāmamātreṇa ākhyātuṃsusamāhitaiḥ
uddeśamātraṃ kathitāḥ pātāle' sminguṇāmayā
teṣāṃvakṣyāmivaiviprānāgapātālavāsināṃ
citrāvicitrāḥ kurvāṇāḥ sūkṣmāṇicagṛhāṇica
dṛ śyaṃtetāninityaṃhiavyaktāvyaktasaṃjñitāḥ
purīgulyā anaṃtasyapātāleparikīrtitā
guṇāḥsaṃkhyānarahitāstasmin puravaretadā
yathāvāhmīcaviṣṇośvapurīṃdrasya tu tattvataḥ
anaṃtasyāpyanaṃtasya sarvakāmasupūjitā
ataḥparaṃtu vipreṃdraśṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥkathām
pravātyadhomukhīcaiva nadīvaitariṇīyataḥ
asipatravanaṃcaivayamaśūlībhayāvahā
bhairavānicarūpāṇiekapāṣāṇamevaca
jalaṃśālmalīkarṣaṇaṃśālmalinaḥ kaṃṭakivṛkṣaviśeṣāt karṣaṇam
athapāpaviśeṣeṇanarakaviśeṣasaṃbaṃdhamāha rauravaiti
kūṭasākṣiṇāmanṛtasākṣyaṃkurva urdhva kaṃ catathāśūlaṃtathāvaitaraṇīnadī
karaṃbhavālukācaivaśṛṃgāṭakavanaṃtathā
aṃdhakāraṃtamoghoraṃnarakomakṣikāta thā
na rakāba huśaḥ proktāyamasya viṣaye smṛtāḥ
sarvādhārairanekaiśvakliśyaṃte capunaḥpunaḥ
āśībhistakṣaṇaiścaiva krakacaiścaivapāṭanam
vaitaraṇyāstathākṣāraṃśālmalīkarṣaṇaṃ tathā
ādānaṃ yaṃtrasūtrasya kuṃbhīpākecamardanam
raurave kūṭasākṣiṇāṃpātanaṃnātra saṃśayaḥ
parahiṃsāniviṣṭānāṃbodha ke patanaṃbhavet
brahmasvaharaṇāccaiva kuṃbhīpākecapātanam
varṣāṇāṃcasahasrāṇipīḍyatecanarādhamaḥ
varṣāṇāṃśatasāhasraṃpīḍyamānaḥ punaḥpunaḥ
strīghātīpūtimāṃsecaniḥ kṣiptaḥ pa cyatedhruvam
dhanadhānyasuvarṇānihiraṇyaṃvāviśeṣataḥ
hṛtvānarakamāpnotiyamaśūlaṃbhayāvaham
mātṛnaḥsūcimukhena śataṃvarṣāṇipīḍanam
pitṛhaṃtātyadhomukhepīḍyaṃtacasuduḥkhitaḥ
sarveṣuvaitariṇyāṃcadevadravyavināśakaḥ
pa cyatenarakeghārevarṣāṇāmekaviṃśatim
malāpahasyamūlānihiṃsya mānohimā navaḥ
bhairavāṇicarūpāṇighoraṃparamadāruṇam
adhomukhenapatativarṣāṇāṃcasahasraśaḥ
ekapāṣāṇanara ke mitrabhāryā bhilāṣiṇaḥ
tathācā'syābhayaṃdatvābhayamutpādyate punaḥ
etāvatāpāpipuruṣairanubhūyamānānnarakānabhidhāyedānīyamalokavartīniramyāṇipuṇyaśālijanagamyānisthānānyāha
eva parastrīgāminaścaiva paradravyābhilāṣukāḥ
sākṣībhūtastuyaḥ kaśvinmithyāsaṃ bhāṣatetadā
ūrdhvapādastathāśūle mahānarakapātane
jivhācotpāṭyatetasya ha laistīkṣṇaiśvapāṭyate
brāhmaṇānāṃcali gānāṃniṃdāṃyaśvakarotisaḥ
vaitaraṇyāṃmahānadyāṃpacyate sa narādhamaḥ
śṛṃgāṭakavanetībre karṣyateyamaśāsanaiḥ
hastacchedaṃcayaḥkuryātstriyāvāpuruṣasya vā
karaṃbhavālukāścaiva ghoraṃ paramadāruṇam
gṛhadāhaṃcakurvāṇaḥpacyatesanarā dhamaḥ
aṃdhakāremahāghorenara kemākṣiketathā
varṣāṇāṃcasahasrāṇi asibhiḥ kalpakoṭayaḥ
evaṃśubhapradaṃ caivanānārūpamavasthitam
pāpānāmatidūrasthaṃduvaidamapidāruṇam
janānāṃpu ṇyakarmaṇāṃ kṣaṇenagamanaṃprati
saṃkṣepānnarakāḥ khyātādustarāśvamahāmu ne
garbhavāsecayaḥkleśomriyamāṇepivaitathā
avidyābādhateduḥkhama jñānāṃvanavāsinām
yadduḥkhaṃyājñikānāṃtuyadduḥkhaṃsāṃkhyayoginām
yadduḥkhaṃmokṣakāṃkṣiṇāṃrāgādīnāmavarjanāt
siddhānnenayajet yajñaṃtasmādyajñaṃsamācaret
jñānamevāśrayedvidvān jātidoṣavināśakam
jātidoṣavināśena sarvakleśavināśanam
raurave kūṭasākṣiṇāṃpātanaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
āyughnaśvāpinippāto vaitaraṇyāmudīritaḥ
siddhenayajateyajñaṃhiṃsādoṣamavāpnuvan
ahiṃsādoṣamāpnotimahāpāśupatesthitaḥ
anyepidurvṛttāḥ proktā mohitāḥ śivamāyayā
yayāprāṇāhigacchaṃ tinarakaṃ svargamevaca
sarvebrahmāṃḍakādevāsthāvarāṇāṃcakārakāḥ
duḥkhāduḥkhaṃ viśaṃtyete avidyātamasākulāḥ
durjayaṃ kāmamokṣāṇāmavidyākarmasaṃbhavāḥ
kathaṃ mānuṣabhāvoyaṃkleśaḥ saṃsargavāsinām
tasmādevaṃpravṛttānāṃtrāhmaṇānāṃ hitaiṣiṇām
sukhā nāṃkhalu kartavyāḥ sarvajñānasamādvijāḥ
narakāccavināśāyajātiduḥkhavināśanam
saṃsāracakramārūḍhāśramaṃteyaṃ tracakravat
tasmāccakravināśāyaśivacakaṃsamāśrayet
śivacakaṃsamārūḍhojñānīdoṣairnalipyate
avi dyākarmajāndoṣānvaṃ cayāmāsamāyayā
evaṃ māheśvarejñānebhaktimānyaḥpriyobhavet
pāparāśidahedevaṃṭaṇarā śimivānalaḥ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ caturtho'dhyāyaḥ
pṛthivyāṃprākpratīcyāṃtudakṣiṇasyāṃtathaivaca
saptadvīpasamudrāśvavyākhyātāhimayāddija
ūrdhvaṃ tāvatpravakṣyāmiyāvadbrahmakulaṃbhavet
prathamaṃ bhavanaṃbhūyovyākhyātaṃtaddijanmanām
dvitīyaṃ bhavanaṃbhūmervyākhyāsyāmiya thābhavet
mahītalesahasrāṇāṃśatenordhvaṃ vibhāvyate
tatrabhānuścacaṃdraśvagrahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha
uparyuparisaṃsṛṣṭaṃyathoktaṃ grahatārakāḥ
ekamanvaṃtaraṃviprāyasya vaigrahatārakāḥ
yathāṃtarikṣe siṃcaṃtibhāṃtivāṃtiyathāgrahāḥ
sarve nānāvidhā statrameghānānāvidhāḥsmṛtāḥ
āgneyānavajānaṃtiparjanyāśvaprakīrtitāḥ
varuṇasyaghanāḥproktāvicaraṃtiyathāpure
eteṣāmupariṣṭāttubhānorlokovibhāvyate
tasmādbhānormahotsāhalokāḥ sura namaskṛtāḥ
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇiṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām
upāsateratha varaṃbhānorakliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
tatrateṣāṃmahātmānonāgagaṃdharvarākṣasāḥ
ṣaṣṭiścaivasahasrāṇi apsarāṇāṃprasaṃkhyayā
gī tagaṃdharvaghoṣaśvahāhāhūhūranekaśaḥ
nāvidhāitiślokārthayojanā
yenavaparjanyāsta āgneyāitijānaṃtividvāṃsaitiyojanā
mahotsāhalokāḥ
vāyurathāḥ vāyūrathogamanasādhanaṃyeṣāṃta meghāḥ
vāyavyāgaṇaviśeṣāḥ
saptaskaṃdheṣu saptasugaṇeṣuvibhaktāitiśeṣaḥ
śataśothavimānāniśataghaṃṭāyutānica
nānāratnavicitrāṇipatākaiḥ śobhitānica
kiṃkiṇījālacitrāṇi nānāratnojjvalānica
sarvakāmasamṛddhānikāvyaśabdānvitānica
ete vāyurathāramyāaṃtarikṣa carāḥ smṛtāḥ
vāyavyāḥ śataśasta śrasa taskaṃdheṣuvaitathā
evaṃgaṇāryāṃāṃtitānsvānbhāgānākāśamevaca
svargapaṃthānamāśrityacaraṃtivimalodakāḥ
devaiḥ sahāpsaro bhiśvasiddhaiśvāpsarasānvitaiḥ
tatradivyāniveśmānivicitrāṇibahūnica
puṇyakṛdbhirupetāni bhāsvarāṇisahasra śaḥ
tatradevāvimānasthāramaṃtekelikārakāḥ
yatragacchaṃti sukṛtaḥ sarva saṃgajitonarāḥ
etelokāmayākhyātā ādityasya mahātmanaḥ
ā dityasyopariṣṭāttu lokāvaivasvatāḥsmṛtāḥ
tatradivyāḥ śucimayāvimānaśataśobhitāḥ
kṣatriyāścaivayajvānomaṃtriṇaḥ somapāyinaḥ
tasmādūrdhvaṃ tatolokāṃ bhāsva raḥsamavasthitaḥ
viprāpbhavaṃtiyajvānovimānaśataśobhitāḥ
yāṃtilokāśrvatatrasthāṛṣīṇāṃ sumahātmanāṃ
divyāṃ baradharāḥsarveupariṣṭādvibhūṣitāḥ
ākāśagaṃgātatrasthāsarve caiva grahāstathā
tasmādūrdhvamṭaṣīṇāṃ vailokaḥ paramapūji taḥ
tatraśūrāraṇeprāṇān parityajya mahāhave
triviṣṭapecavikhyāteśakasyevāmarāvatī
upariṣṭādṛṣīṇāṃtuśa kalokaṃtutatsmṛtam
koṭiśatasahasreṇa sādhyānāṃparivāritam
caturguṇaṃtu vikhyātaṃdevalokapramāṇataḥ
ataḥ sanatkumāraśvakārtikeyaśvanaṃdanaḥ evaṃ bhavaṃti sukhinaḥśayyāvastra hiraṇyadāḥ
upariṣṭāttārakāṇāṃ brahmaloketitatsmṛtam
saptarṣayodhruvaścaivaviṣṇuścaiva mahāmatiḥ
tasyordhvaviṣṇuloka śvagolokaścapratiṣṭhitaḥ
ādyāditvātsārvavibhaktikastasiḥ
pṛthivīmaṃḍalādūrdhvayojanāvarṇitaṃtathā
ūrdhvamekaṃtuvai lokaṃkoṭīnāṃ śatayojanam
eṣo'dhvagapracārovaijñānaṃjñānaṃtathaiva ca
naśakyaṃprāpyate gaṃtuṃvarjayitvāśivānugān
anugrahādvāyo gādvānaiṣṭhikādvātathādvijāḥ
etasminnaṃtaredevāḥ sarvaiṃdrapurogamāḥ
pādayoḥ patitāḥ sarve brahmāṇamṛṣayastathā
brahmaṇācāpyanujñātāḥ sarve sukhamayāḥ sthitāḥ
svāgataṃvo mahā bhāgāḥśṛṇudhvaṃ kimihecchatha
yena kāryeṇa vāyātāstadurvaṃtusurottamāḥ
devāūcuḥ
kṛtaṃvareṇaparyāptaṃ sraṣṭātvaṃ paripṛ cchasi

mahānnaḥsaṃśayo'tyaṃtaṃbhagavānvaktumarhati

yadahaṃpṛṣṭavānpūrvaṃ rudrasyaparamātmanaḥ

naimiṣeyāstuṛṣayojitakrodhājiteṃdriyāḥ
icchādveṣavinirmuktādhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ
īśvarajñānasaṃpa nnāgatābrahmasabhāṃparāṃ
bhṛgvaṃgirasavṛddhau capurastātkṛtavānśuciḥ
paramabhāvinī paramaṃparamātmānaṃ bhāvayatītisā
yataḥ pāpasamācārāḥ sadācā
oṃnamaḥśivāya uktvāpuṇya tatrakāmamayānāmasabhāparamabhāvinī

sūtauvāca
vi nayādāgatovyāsaḥ sadbhāvaṃ bhaktimāśritaḥ
sanatkumāraṃ sarvajñaṃsaṃdehamathapṛṣṭavān
eṣamesaṃśayobrahmanbrūhi me tvaṃmahāmune
bhagavanbhūtabhavyeśaśaktyāśrāvayituṃkṣamaḥ
ākhyāhirudramāhātmyaṃśṛṇumaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ

nadevāsuragaṃdharvānapiśācānarākṣasāḥ
dṛṣṭvāhaṃmohamāpannoniśveṣṭaściramāsthitaḥ
lakṣa koṭisahasrāṇāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
kṛtvākarālaṃdaṃṣṭrānaṃ mukhapadmaṃ suśobhanam
samamāyāṃtisaṃmūḍhāḥ kimarthapariśuṣyatha

yathāvasthānibhūtānisthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
prājāpatyaṃ bhavedannamanneprāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
annādbhavaṃtibhū tāni annaṃvaiyajñasaṃbhavam
ṛcoyajūṃṣisāmāni kalpopaniṣadastathā

sāvitrīsaṃbhavotyeṣabrahmākṣaramayomahān
mayāśaktyāva hmaṇācaviṣṇunāpisaījyate
yajñalokastadāsāmnāṃpratipattiḥ svayaṃbhuvā
upadeśaṃtataḥ kṛtvā mahādevo maheśvaraḥ
uktvāvacanamīśānastatraivāṃtaradhīyata
ekā bhagavatomūrtirūrdhvaromābhayāvahā
dvitīyātasyavaimūrtiḥ sūryajyotiḥsamaprabhā
tṛtīyābhagavatomūrtiḥ śaśinaḥ paramātmanaḥ
tattupaśyaṃtividdadvāṃsaḥ sūkṣmadhyānaviciṃtakāḥ
loke vedecasaṃyuktāśaivīcaiva pṛthakpṛthak
krīḍateprathamāmṛrtirdvitīyātapyatetapaḥ
tṛtīyāharatelokāṃścaturthīssṛjateprajāḥ
paṃcamījñānasadbhāvaṃ sarva māhatya tiṣṭhati
saeṣasarvabhūtānāṃ gomāīśānaucyate
utpattiṃpralayaṃcaiva bhūtā nāṃsaṃgatiṃgatiṃ
mahāṃśca mahatoyasmānmahadbhiśvamahīyate
yasmā didaṃ mahannityaṃ mahādevaitismṛtaḥ
yasmānnāśayatepūrṇa trailokyaṃ sacarācaraṃ
paśūnāṃpāśanaṃcaivatasmātpaśupatiḥ smṛ taḥ
svayaṃmātāsvayaṃbhūtvāpriyolokairanuttamaḥ
itiṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ
lokeṣucasvayaṃbhūtvāsvayaṃbhūritihismṛtaḥ
yasmādekaṃśiraśchitvātatkapālamadhārayat
kapālītitataḥ proktobajhā yairṛṣibhistathā
yasmātkṣayāṃte trailokyaṃśaṃkareyātisaṃkṣayaṃ
tasmātsaṃvartakodhātāśaṃkaretyabhidhīyate
yasmā dimānibhūtāni paśyaṃtenādhikaṃtataḥ
sarvaṃviśveśvarodevastasmādīśānatobhavat
bṛhattvāhaṇa māvataṃbrahmayāvatprāṇamayodhuvaḥ
akṣarādvāparorudrākṣarāśvavayaṃpurā
asmākaṃdevatārudrova yaṃdeveṣudevatāḥ
devādevādvijātīnāṃ dvijāḥ śeṣasya devatāḥ
āpadbhāvaḥsamāpannomucyatenātra saṃśayaḥ
itiśrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃtrahmagītopākhyānaṃnāmaṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ
etatkāraṇasaṃjātaṃniścalaṃkevalaṃ dhruvam
viṣṇuḥpārśvāttusaṃbhūtoliṃgebhūtāḥ surāstathā
liṃgāyasavadharmeṇa jagatsthā varajaṃgamaṃ
liṃgamūrtiścabhagavānanādinidhanaḥśivaḥ
alpākṣaramidaṃgutyaṃ mamaikāṃteniśamyatām
ahaṃviṣṇuḥ purāśakroanyevāsurapuṃgavāḥ
virūpākṣasya netrābhyāṃnimiṣonmeṣaṇesthitāḥ
taccavakṣyāmi vipreṃdrāīśvaraṃ saṃpracakṣate
rudreṇasadṛśaṃdevaṃ nānyaṃ paśyāmahevayam
sarvathāvarttamānāśvayebhaktāḥ parameśvare
tevaśyavāsināṃtulyāmunīnāṃ bhāvitātmanāṃ
bhavapāpaṃnaviṃdaṃtiteryātiparamāṃ gatim
nadevāsuragaṃdharvānayakṣānacarākṣasāḥ
viṣṇutvaṃvāsavatvaṃcaamaratvaṃsuraiḥ saha
rudrabhaktāstuvipreṃdrāḥ prāpnuvaṃtiśivālayam
aśubhāḥ pāpakarmāṇoyena rāḥkalmaṣīkṛtāḥ
īśvaraṃpratipaśyaṃ dvijābhāvitabhāvanāḥ
ādidevaṃ mahādevaṃ prabhuṃ prabhavatāmapi
yesmaraṃtisadā rudrabhayaṃteṣāṃnavidyate
suraiḥ sahavāsamitiśeṣaḥ
śivālayaṃ śivakalyāṇaṃca tadālayasthānaṃ mokṣamityarthaḥ
prabhavatāṃ alaukikaśaktimatāṃ devānām
pāpayonayaḥ śvapacādayaḥ
nīlakaṃṭhasya nīlaḥ kaṃṭhoviṣabhakṣaṇena yaṃsyasaḥ
sarvalakṣaṇahīnaḥ sarvairnijavarṇāśramocitadharmehīṃnaḥ
śi yekīrtayaṃtisata taṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram
rudrarudretitrisaṃdhyaṃyaśvabūyādvicakṣaṇaḥ
kīrtanānnīlakaṃṭhasyasa rvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
sarvalakṣaṇahīnopiyuktovāsarvapātakaiḥ
sarvaṃtaratitatpāpaṃbhāvataḥ śivamāsthitaḥ
saṃsā reśbhramamāṇānāṃpāpa yoniṣuyadbhavet
mahādevaprapannānāṃbhayaṃteṣāṃnavidyate
manasāpiśirvadevaṃyeprapayaṃtimānavāḥ
vidhūtāḥ sarvapāpebhyodevaiḥ saharamaṃtite
agnihotraṃcayenityaṃyajñāṃścaiva sudakṣiṇān
rudrabhaktasya vipreṃdrāḥ kalāṃnā ītiṣoḍaśīm
sarveṣāṃ dhyānayogānāṃye cā'nyemokṣakāṃkṣiṇaḥ
mahādevaprasādenaprāpnuvaṃtiparāṃgatim
aprāpyacavirūpākṣaṃkaḥ pumānsiddhimarhati
tīrthānāṃcamahātīrthaṃ maṃgalā nāṃcamaṃgalam
yatpavicaṃpavitrāṇāṃ saṃprapadyetamīśvaram
eṣadevovirūpākṣaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ
thṛdisthaḥ sarvabhūtā nāmoṃkāramadhigacchati
niṣkalaṃpuruṣavaraṃsamahāliṃgalakṣaṇam
aśāmyaśamana karaṃkathaṃtatphalaṃvidmahe
yathāghṛtaṃcapayasiyayāgniścaivadāruṇi
yathāvayaṃtathācānye tathāsana tkumārādayaḥ
ādhyātmikaiḥ suravarairbrahmaṇaḥ svātmasaṃbhavaiḥ
tatkāraṇakāitibhāvaḥ
oṃnamaḥ prakṛtyajāpyaṃstutihomaliṃgaṃnatobravīmyatra mahāmaheśvaram
punastutatrāpidadarśaliṃgamanāmayaliṃgamalakṣaṇaṃca
nadevagaṃdharvanabhūtasaṃghānasiddhayakṣādhipapannagādhipāḥ
vibhuṃ prapaśyaṃti maheśvaraṃparaṃmahāviṣaṃyojarayatkṣaṇena
piṭa mānuṣanāgānāṃnabhayaṃ vidyatekvacit
kāmageṣuvimāneṣuvicaraṃti himānavāḥ
arcayaṃtivirūpākṣaliṃgamūrtimaheśvaram
itiśrī śivamahāpurāṇesa natkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ saptamodhyāyaḥ
ṛṣayaūcuḥ
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭivarṣaśatānica
thṛṣīkeśenavipreṃdrāvarṣa koṭiṃprasāditaḥ
ārādhito mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇirmaheśvaraḥ
tuṣṭena catathāviṣṇurvaraiḥśveṣṭhaistu yojitaḥ
sāmnācadvaṃdva śinnāmamahācakradharovalī
īśvarasyaprasādenaviṣṇuḥ paramataijasaḥ
rakṣate pṛthivīṃsarvāmajeyaśvabalītataḥ
prasāditovirūpākṣaḥ puṣkarākṣomaheśvaraḥ
iṣṭābhistutipūjābhirvividhaiḥ karmabhi stathā
ārādhito mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇirhiraṇmayaḥ
tuṣṭenacakṛtobrahmāsaṃhartāviśvatomukhaḥ
dātāhartāca goptā ca saṃhartācayugeyuge
pitāmahatvaṃcasurāsurāṇāṃ brahmādhipatyaṃ paramavyayaṃca
anāgataṃ vartamānaṃ cavi śvaṃ sarveṣu lokeṣucarācaratvam
sarvecavedāḥ sahaṣatiraṃgaiḥsāṃkhyaṃcayogaṃcasapāribhāṣam
śakreṇāpipurācīrṇedivyaṃ pāśupataṃ mahat
vāyubhakṣo'bukṣavadurvāsāśvarmasaṃvṛtaḥ
evamāsīdvirūpākṣorudraḥśṛṃgādṛhāsataḥ
kapardītasya tuṣṭo vai kṛttivāsāḥ pinākadhṛk
gaṇeśovaikṛtaḥ śakroma hāvajradharobalī
bhūyaścakraturājena dattaṃ caiva triviṣṭapaṃ
sanatkumāraḥputrome vyākhyātomānasoddijāḥ
sahasraṃca vimānānāṃ saptasaṃkhyāsuyatpurā
caṃdrasūryaprakāśeṣuvibhāneṣupratiṣṭhitaḥ
strīsahasrasamākīrṇodīpyamānaḥ sutejasā
gāyadbhirnṛtyamānaiśvavādayadbhiśvasarvaśaḥ
puruṣaiḥ sūryasaṃkāśairdīpyamānaiḥ svatejasā
upaviṣṭaḥ sthitastatragi riṃpādena pīḍayan
yajamānāśvayedṛṣṭālokayātrākarāśvaye
pārthivāstetaṃmāsādya sarvadhiṣṇyeṣvadhiṣṭhitāḥ
udyogināṃcatarjitvaṃ bhīruṇāṃcanivāraṇam
puṣpakāle capuṣyaṃtiphalakāle phalapradāḥ
pākakāle capacyatedvāreṣucasu saṃvṛtāḥ
śaileṣuniratāyecapātālecasamāśritāḥ
aṃtarikṣe carāye cacaraṃtiṃdivisaṃśritāḥ
yecanakṣatramārgeṣunakṣa trāṇisamāśritāḥ
hāsavṛddhikarāyeca caṃdrasūryaugrasaṃtiye
svasthāneprasthitāśvānyesāṃkhyayogamanuvratāḥ
asaṃkhyātātyanekāśvajaṃgamājaṃgamāḥ sthitāḥ
jvalaṃtamuṣṇaṃmuṃcatinabhayaṃ tesamāśritāḥ
divyāḥpārśvagatāḥ sarvegṛhāstupādapāstathā
kuṃdeṃdu kumudaprakhyāṃmālapadmasugaṃdhinīm
jighaṃticai vadhāvaṃtirudrapārśvagatāgaṇāḥ
teṣāṃvarṇaviśeṣo'sti pramāṇaṃcaiva dṛśyate
ekaikasya gaṇeśasyaśarīraṃpratitiṣṭhati
merumaṃdaraśailānāṃgaṇānāṃ parimāṇataḥ
teṣāṃ parivṛtodevograhāṇāmiva bhāskaraḥ
sanatkumārodeveśogaṇeśāyama hātmane
evaṃdṛṣṭaṃmayākhyātaṃ bhīmasyāmitatejasaḥ
śṛṇuyādgaṇasaṃkhyānaṃmanasāpisadāsmaret
prayatnamānasobhūtvā paṭhetparvaṇi parvaṇi
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti amṛtatvaṃcaviṃdati
śataṃśatasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate
ṛtu kālecanārīṇāṃ tathaiva samudāharet
āhārakāletupaṭhedrāhmaṇānāṃcasaṃni dhau
nityamevaṃ paṭhatiyaḥśraddhānojiteṃdriyaḥ
śatarudraphalaṃ tasya labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
paṭhatastutataḥpuṇyaṃgaṇasaṃkhyāṃcanityaśaḥ
śṛṇuyādvā piyobhaktyāsarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
prabhātasamayekāle samutthāyamahāmanāḥ
brahmāṇaṃdeva kartāraṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam
imāṃsiddhiprapaśyaṃtaḥ siddhāste garvitāḥ purā
sya śivasyavā
uktagaṇavarṇanasyapāṭhaśravaṇādiṣu phalaviśeṣamāhaṃ
śṛṇuyādityādi
śataśatasahasrāṇivarṣāṇāmitiśeṣaḥ
mogharetāḥ saphalaśukraḥ
anaṃtapāpayuktovā
ūrdhvacanayanaṃdṛṣṭvādeva tejomayaṃsthitam
pitācapitarome dyadṛṣṭvāpātramupāgatāḥ
evaṃ dṛṣṭvāsa māṃ putro vyājahārasasaṃbhramaḥ
nigṛhīto'smi bhadraṃ te bālenākṛtakarmaṇā
vi mānānicaratnāni ajasraṃcasusaṃskṛtam
tenāhaṃduḥkhasaṃtāpāddehaṃtyakṣye na saṃśayaḥ
ātmānaṃ gamayāmāsadhyānayogena dṛṣṭavān
sapāraititaṃ jñātvātatodṛṣṭanarobhavat
utthāyacāsa nābrahmāprāṃjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ
namaskṛtvā mahādeva mīśvaraṃ sarvatomukham
idamāhamahātejābrahmālokapitāmahaḥ
yogānāmadhikoyogīdevānāmaṃbikāpatiḥ
dṛṣṭvāpurānaṃdimukhadeva devenabhāṣitam
anugrahaṃmahādevaḥ kartukāmomaheśvaraḥ
sarvavaidarśayāmāsa ātmācaiva sudurlabhaḥ gāṇapatyaṃlabhaṃ tveteviṣṇunācaprakīrtitāḥ
nakiṃcidrahmacārīcapaśyatyakṛtabuddhyaḥ
aikāṃtena casaukhyevānāstitatravicāraṇā
vṛṇīṣvātmaṃmahādevaṃgāṇapatyaṃsudurlabham
gāṇapatyaṃcabhadraṃteviṣṇunāsāditaṃpurā
brahmaṇovacanaṃ śrutvāprayatāmānasaṃjapan
prasannaśvamahādevaḥ śūlapāṇirmaheśvaraḥ
tuṣṭaḥ prasannodeveśaḥ karmabhiśvāmitaujasaḥ
sthitaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃrutvā devadevasya dhīmataḥ
carācaraprīticārīdharmiṣṭhovaradovaraḥ
dhāraṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃdharādharapatiryamaḥ
bhūtasaṃsāra karaṇogopatistri daśeśvaraḥ
sāṃkhyayogeśvaraḥ karmakumāraḥ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
śatasūryāgninetraśvacārunetravibhūṣitaḥ
caturmukhaśvaturdaṃṣṭraścatu bahuśrcaturyugaḥ
vāyukālāgnirudraśvadigvāsāmeghavāhanaḥ
jalādhāro tyanaṃtaśvadharmādharmabhṛteśvaraḥ
kārtikaḥ śubhakatīca śrīkaṃṭhaḥ kalināśanaḥ
viṣṇuprasādadaścaiva samudrevaḍavāmukhaḥ
devā suravinirjetādevāsuraparāyaṇaḥ
kapardīśūlahastaśca ajātaḥ paramāgatiḥ
tāpasānāṃparaṃ tattvaṃ tathāca paramaṃ padaṃ
bhavanaṃyo parāvarajñolokānāṃ sarvadāharivāhanaḥ
asitāṃgaḥsitāṃgaśca asitāyatalocanaḥ
brahmaṇādhīyatebrahmāsaṃsthito nābhipaṃkaje
nīlograjaṭilaḥ śrīmānśaṃkhacakragadādharaḥ
ṛcoyajūṃṣi sāmāni kalpopaniṣadastathā
maṃtrāṇāṃ bhavanaṃ caiva parasyātharvaṇasyaca
sahasravāṭpaśupatiḥsahasraśatayojanaḥ
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃcabhagavāneva sarvaśaḥ
tvadgātrebhyaḥ prasūryaṃtetra yolokāḥ sa nātanāḥ
evaṃ saṃstūyamānaḥ sa vyaktī bhūtomaheśvaraḥ
upagamyamudāyuktastadādṛṣṭaḥ sadṛṣṭimān
kamaṃḍaludharodaṃḍīśaśāṃkakṛtaśekharaḥ
vyā ghracarmāṃbaradharaḥ siṃhacamaṃcaracchadaḥ
nāgayajñopavītīca akṣamālāvibhūṣitaḥ
jaṭīśikhaṃḍīkhadvāṃgīpaṭṭiśāśani śūladhṛk
puraḥ śaradharodevaḥśakticāpasamudgaraiḥ
śaṃkhacakragadāpāṇiḥpadmaśūkahalāyudhaḥ
śaśiruṣṇājinadharaḥka pālī ghoracāpadhṛk
vṛṣārūḍhorhīpyamānogaṇaiḥ parivatoharaḥ
naṃdināśūlahastenapurastāddarśitaḥ prabhuḥ
dadṛśe bhagavāndevaḥsūryāgniśaśinādṛśā
tathācasarvaprāṇirūpaitibhāvaḥ
brahmaṇākathitaṃ pūrvaṃ yathāgatyaṃyathodbhavam
manasaḥ kāmalobhaumelobhānmeharṣaṇaṃcayat
iṃdriyāṇāṃcasarveṣāmindriyāṇimanāṃsi ca
prāṇāyāmesa māneṣuudānodāname vaca
kālena sarvabhūtānāṃniṣpattiḥ samudāhṛtā
nāśnaṃtitarpitādevāḥ sadāviśadamānasaḥ
tvamevoragagaṃdharvapiśācayakṣarākṣasāḥ
tvadṛte nā'nyabhaktosmi manasā karmaṇāgirā
tasyaivaṃvacanaṃ śrutvā umāpatirmaheśvaraḥ
mamanāmāni sarvāṇigocarāṇibhavaṃtute
susaṃgrahāṇi sarvāṇināsti kācidvicāraṇā
pārāśaryaitikhyāta utpatsyati mahātapāḥ
vedavyā saḥ sadharmātmājñānavāndīrghadarśanaḥ
vyāsaḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥsateśiṣyobhaviṣyati
nirmalaṃvimalaṃ śuddhaṃ jñānaṃ caṃdrasama prabham
rathaṃkāmagamaṃ divyaṃsāraratnavibhūṣitam
muktājālaparicchanna hemajālasamāvṛtaṃ
patākairamaṇaṃtatrasevyamānaṃ surāsuraiḥ
vimānaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ sarvalokojva laṃśubham
tenayāsyasirtatenapūjyamānaṃ surāsuraiḥ
akṣaraṃtatraaiśvaryaṃ bhaviṣyatimamājñayā
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāryā aṣṭamodhyāyaḥ
sasaṃcacāra lokāṃstrīn brahmaputro'bikāsutaḥ
eṣarhātācakartācasaṃha rtācayugeyuge
etasya trividhaṃ sarvamīśānasya mahātmanaḥ
eṣayajñapatirdevaḥ kṛtāṃtaḥ saumāpatiḥ
eṣa hotācahomyaśva evaṃ yajñavidoviduḥ
iṃdriyāṇīṃdriyārtheṣusarva eva maheśvaraḥ
evaṃjñānaparaṃbrahmapraśāṃtaṃnirmalaṃśivam
avyaktaṃce vavyaktaṃcajñānaṃcājñānamevaca
sāṃkhyayogaṃparaṃ sāṃkhyayaḥ paśyatisapaśyati
tatojñānenaśuddhāstuprāṇāyāmajiteṃdriyāḥ
dhyāyaṃtiparamoṃkāraṃyogināṃparamaṃ padam
tapasāṃca prasādenalabhaṃteyogaci takāḥ
śrutiriyaṃ paramāśivasyagutyaṃśrutvāparamaina sānalipyate saḥ
evaṃ śrutvātataḥ sarve ṛṣayodharmavatsalāḥ
abhyanujñāpyatāṃdevagacchāmovigataiṣaṇāḥ
japyairdhūpairalaṃkāraiḥ stūyate vividhaiḥśivaḥ
oṃkārādinamaskāraiḥ sahitai gītavādanaiḥ
athasavyāpasavyaiśvavāmadevaṃ tu suvratāḥ
najñānenanatapa sāciṃtanātbhāvitātmanām
sāṃkhyādeva paraṃmokṣaṃyaccānyairvividhaistathā
ṛṣibhirviprayuktānvaiṛṣīṇāṃ pradadauva rān
teṣāmapiyathākāmaṃmanasāīpsitaṃdadet
sarvavarṇānukaṃpīcasarvatīrthamayovyayaḥ
yeṣāṃtu kalaṣābuddhirnarāṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām
tevaisūkṣmāṃyoga mūrtiviśaṃtividuṣo janāḥ
niṣkalāvirajāḥ khyātābhaviṣyaṃtiśivāśritāḥ
yatīnāṃ brahmagītāca brahmaṇāsamudāhṛtā
yaścaināṃ paṭhateni tyaṃyaścaināṃśṭaṇuyātsadā
devāgārepaṭhennityaṃsadābrāhmaṇasannidhau
dhyāyaphalaśrutiḥ
āsīdasti
viṣkaṃbheṇa argalarūpeṇa
āyāmataitiyāvat
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃbahmagītā nāmanavamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
tadahaṃ jñātumicchā mivistareṇamahāmune
āsīdgirivarovyāsayojanānāṃsamaṃtataḥ
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇinadīpra sravaṇairyutaḥ
viṣkaṃbheṇasthitobrahman tāvānevocchritaḥ smṛtaḥ
surasyasagi riśreṣṭhaśvāmīkarasamaprabhaḥ
tasyakuṃbhepukuṃbheṣukaṃdareṣudarīṣuca
nānākusumacitrepuśikhināṃ madhurāgiraḥ
bheruṃḍaiḥ svarṇayūthaiśvacakārairanviteṣuca
gajavaṃdā va kīrṇeṣu madenavāsitapuca
vyāghrāṇāṃ caiva kakṣāṇāṃkhagānāṃ bhavaneṣuca
harmya staṃbheṣu kīrṇe pusiṃhānāṃ rūpaśālināṃ
śobhitagirivaryeca devānāṃcasurāgaṇāḥ
kuberapramukhāyakṣāḥ krīḍaṃticasamaṃtataḥ
vicaraṃtimudāyuktāvidyādharagaṇānvitāḥ
hāhāhūhūśvagaṃdharvā staṃburupramukhāstathā
sametyaviśvāvasunāvicaraṃti mudānvitāḥ
yaṃtradhārānighāteṣuninadaṃtiśikhaṃḍinaḥ
tāstucaṃ drāṃśubhāḥ kāmaṃjyotsnāyāḥ sariduttamāḥ
yatrasāpatategaṃgādevatānāṃ kulānivai
teṣucātmanivābhāṃtiuditāṃnisamaṃ tataḥ
taṃprāpya sarvabhūtāni sauvarṇānimahāṃtivai
nacāpisamaṛṣayorvātivai mārutāḥ śubhāḥ
manasātanna paśyaṃtidevatā grāmaharṣayaḥ
bhuvanaṃkāṃcanaśrīmanvijayaṃvijayānadī
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇidaśacāṣṭauprakīrtitāḥ
tāpanīyena mahatāprākāreṇasamāvṛtāḥ
gṛhāstaṃtra suramyāśvapatākāśobhimāli kāḥ
divākarakarābhāścasuprabhā amitaujasaḥ
tatradvārasahasrāṇitāvaṃ taśvadvijottamāḥ
sarvāṇipuṇyakarmāṇitaru ṇārkasamaprabhāḥ
vinyastaiḥ pūrṇakuṃbhaiśca śobhitāniyathātathā
muktādāmaiḥsuvipulairbhūṣitānisamaṃtataḥ
puṣpopahārairvividhairdhūpaiśvāgarusaṃbhavaiḥ
rakṣibhiśvasamāguptaṃvipulaiśvarya śālibhiḥ
prākārapratisaṃchannaprāsādairgṛhapaṃktibhiḥ
kailāsaśikharaprakhyāvirājatasahasraśaḥ
anyājāṃbūnadama yāḥprāsādānāṃcapaṃktayaḥ
pāvakāiva dīpyatejvālāvipulamālinaḥ
kecinmaṇimayāstatraprāsādābhavanottamāḥ
prerayaṃnidiśaḥ sarvāḥ śaradīvoditā grahāḥ
bhūmikābhiḥ paricchinnaṃkānanaiścasamaṃtataḥ
gavākṣamālākalitaṃmuktādāmairvibhūṣitaṃ
vicitrairbhūṣitairnaddhaṃ śivenamana sākṛtaṃ
dvāraiḥ suvipulaiśvitraiḥ śobhitaṃsaparicchadaiḥ
nānāratnaśataiśvitraiḥ patākāśataśobhitaiḥ
vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalādyaiśva phalānāṃca suvarṇitaiḥ
pārijātakavarṇaiśvasauvarṇa kadalīvanaiḥ
nadībhiśvataḍāgaiśvapalvalaiśvasamaṃtataḥ
vāpī bhirdīrghikābhiśvanhadaiḥ kūpaiścaśobhitaiḥ
kadaṃba pallavaiśvāpi balākānāṃcapaṃ ktibhiḥ
mayūraiścakravākaiśvatathaivaśukasārikaiḥ
tasminadvārapurāṇyaṣṭaupuraśreṣṭhedvijottama
śrīdvāraṃ prathamaṃtatra mahāsi yovyavasthitaḥ
pūrvasyāṃ diśivaiśaivaḥ padmamālāvibhūṣitaḥ
la kṣmīdvāraṃtatastasya yatrāṃbudasamaprabhaḥ
mahākālomahākāyaḥ sthitaḥ śūlomahābalaḥ
śivaṃnāmapuraṃtatradakṣiṇenavya vasthitam
gaṃḍakarṇaḥsthitastatra mahāvīryaḥśivājñayā
sannidhānetathācānyetasyāmeva diśiddijāḥ
pālitaṃ bhīmanādena gaṇeśena mahātmanā
paścimaṃvāruṇaṃ dvāraṃtatra naṃdīśvaraḥśrutaḥ
pālitaṃhavi jivhenagaṇanāthena dhīmatā
kīrtidvāraṃtathodīcyāṃtasyāmevadiśidvijāḥ
yatrārkavaruṇaprakhyodvārādhyakṣomaheśvaraḥ
upakrīḍanakai śvitraiḥ krīḍate bhagavānprabhuḥ
yatrayāṃtijitakrodhājitalobhājiteṃdriyāḥ
śrūyaṃtepaśupaterbhaktyārudrabhaktiparā dvijāḥ
yecaivāgamasaṃyuktāḥ sāṃkhyāśca śrutabuddhayaḥ
yegṛhasthāśvadharmasthārudrabhaktājitaklamāḥ
nyāyatoyudhyamā nāśvasaṃgrāmābhimukhehatāḥ
kṣatriyogograhasyārthemitrārthairāṣṭrapālane
vaiśyāśvaniratādharme satyavācojiteṃdriyāḥ
rujeṃdra viṣṇuhṛdayāyevāla ṇahiteratāḥ
yesuvarṇasyadātārastathāsarvapriyaṃvadāḥ
vedādhyayanasaṃpannā dhyāyinovratacāriṇaḥ
yajatividhināyajñaiḥ kratubhiśvārudakṣiṇaiḥ
tetatragatvādṛṣṭāstunivasaṃtiyathāsukhaṃ
kalpāyutasahasrāṇāṃsahasrāṇicaturdaśa
jāyaṃte śreṣṭhavarṇe pusukhaiśva parame ryutāḥ
jagatīṃcābhinaṃdaṃticiraṃpramuditāstathā
tataḥparaṃpravakṣyāmiraupyabhṛṃganivāsitaṃ
rājataṃgirirājasyaśṛṃgaṃśrīsāgaraṃmahat
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi trīṇyevaṃ tu paraṃ hitam
prākāreṇāthamahatārāja tenasamāvṛtaṃ
alaṃkṛtena divyenapatākādhvajamālinā
rājatadvārasāhasairmaṇicitraiśvacitritaṃ
yatrastaṃbhasahasrābhyāṃdvābhyāṃprāsādamuttamaṃ
puramadhye sthitaṃkāṃ taṃ rājataṃdhātubhūṣitam
nānāviṣṇupadaṃnāmatatsurairapi kīrtitam
caturdvāraṃcatuḥśṛṃgakailāsaśikharaprabham
nānāra tnasamākīrṇenānādrumalatāvṛtam
tasya mūrdhnisthitedvārekṛṣṇarūpaḥ pratāpavān
dvārādhyakṣaḥ sthitastatrathṛdayajñakaro balī
pratīhāromahākāyohariprāṇasamojave
tasminmadhumatīnāmanadīsvārthaprakāśikā
kāṃcanaiḥ kamalaiśvāpinānāpakṣinināditā
tatrātha suciraṃkālaṃbhayaśokavivarjitāḥ
taistaiḥ karmabhirādiṣṭāḥ śaktitaḥ samanuṣṭhitaiḥ
prājāpatyaṃ pravakṣyāmitanmenigadataḥ śṛṇu
tṛtīyaṃsusthiraṃśṛṃgaṃma ṇiratnamayaprabhaṃ
yojanānāṃsahasredveviśokaṃnāmanāmataḥ
caṃdrārkagrahasaṃkāśaṃprabhākaramanuttamaṃ
tribhiśvitraiḥ suvipulaiḥ śikharaiśvāpyalaṃkṛtam
sthitaṃstaṃbhasahasreṇaprāsādapuramālinaṃ
harmyāṭṭālaka saṃyuktaṃvalabhīnāṃśate naca
gavākṣāṇāṃ sahasreṇaśobhitaṃpaṃktimālayā
dvāraiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃsvapramāṇaiḥ suśobhitam
alaṃkārairviśiṣṭādvyaiḥ sarvataḥ parivistṛtaḥ
nāmnādvārādhipaḥ śrīmān jvalanārkasamaprabhaḥ
dvārādhyakṣodvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sa jalāṃbudasannibhaḥ
nāmnāparamaya stasmisthitaḥ saṃdhyāruṇaprabhaḥ
prajāpatiḥsuraśreṣṭho vedasāṃkhyaviśāradaḥ
amṛtānāmavikhyātānadītasmin purottame padmanīlotpalayutā śubhakāṃcanavālukā
pitite susaṃdṛṣṭāstattoyaṃpuravāsinaḥ
tatpītvācajarānaivanaśokonapariśramaḥ
prāsādapuramālinaṃ prāsādānāṃpurāṇāṃcamālābhiḥ paritoveṣṭitam
valabhīvakadārūparivaṣṭivāraṇārthaṃkṛtā
śataśa
suprabhāḥśubhakarmāṇaḥ satyasiddhājiteṃdriyāḥ
kratudānaprasaktāśvagurū ṇāṃcapriyeratāḥ
yecabhikṣāmupāsaṃtetīrthāyatanavāsinaḥ
dharmeṣuniratāyecaviprāḥ krodhavivarjitāḥ
yecadhyānapa rānityaṃyogecaniratāḥ sadā
sāṃkhyadhyānaparāviprāsteṣāṃvaipratyayomahān
viśuddhānicakarmāṇiyecaraṃtitadarthinaḥ
teyāṃtiparamaṃsthānaṃśokamohavivarjitāḥ
kalpāyutasahasrāṇivartayaṃti sukhānvitāḥ
śaucācārasamāyuktāstela bhaṃteparaṃsukham
jñānenaiva catatsthānaṃprayāṃtiparamārcitam
sa tvayuktāmahātmānojitakrodhājiteṃdriyāḥ
prājāpatyamidaṃsthānaṃ kīrtitaṃcasanātanam
evametāniviprarṣebhūdhareṃdra syadhīmataḥ
trīṇitribhiśvabhuvanairātmasthānīkṛtānivai
tevaibhadrādikayutāyāvadbhāṃtisureśvarāḥ
meghābhūtvānu garjatividyunmālāivāṃbare
grahanakṣatratārāśvatebhavaṃtimaheśvarāḥ
kāmagāḥ sarvasiddhārthāramaṃtebhavane surāḥ
idaṃsva yaṃbhuvākhyātaṃ paṭhetparvaṇi parvaṇi
labhate'bhīpsitān kāmānmohaśokavivarjitaḥ
idaṃ paramaṃ pavitraṃ śubhaṃtacca kathitaṃvipulaṃmayāmunīṃdra
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesa natkumārasaṃhitāyāṃśivapuravarṇanaṃnāmadaśamo'dhyāyaḥ
idaṃparamiti viṣamacchaṃdaḥ
itidaśamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
bhagavanśrotumicchāmi māhātmyaṃpuṇyakarmaṇaḥ
yānisthānānirudrasyayathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
bhūrāyābrahma lokāṃtāḥsatyalokāḥprakīrtitāḥ
evaṃśatasahasrāṇiyo janānāṃpramāṇataḥ
vaiṣṇavātkoṭivijñeyaṃ yojanānāṃpramāṇataḥ
aṣṭamaṃ rudralokaṃtuetaduktaṃ triviṣṭapam
evaṃ triviṣṭapaṃtatradevānāmamitaujasām
brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃmanubhiśvasamanvitam
tasmātriviṣṭapasyaiva dvijārdhenapra māṇataḥ
śataṃrudrasahasrāṇiviṣṇukoṭiśatānica
śivaprasādātkīḍaṃ tisarvaivigatakalmaṣāḥ
sarve kusumagaṃdhāvyāḥkhaḍgayaṣṭidharāapi
śūlinodaṃṣṭriṇaścaiva sarve vigatamatsarāḥ
caṃdrā rdhamaulinaḥ sarve sarve vṛṣabhagāminaḥ
amalāste mahātmāna trailokya suviśāra dāḥ
sarvāmaṇimayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣmakāṃcanavālukā
natatra caṃdrāka vāyuśvaprakāśetenavātica
nayāṃtidevatāstatracaṃ drāṃkitavibhūṣaṇāḥ
svayaṃpratyakṣavaradāḥ sarva eva prakāśaṃte
prāsādaharmyamālānigopurelakṣaṇānica
tatravai brāhmaṇaiḥsārdhaigṛhasthāḥsatpathesthitāḥ
gaṃdhadhūpādibhiścaiva sadāya jaṃtiśū linam
sarvapāpavinirmuktāgṛhasthāḥ sūryavarcasaḥ
sarvelokā adhastāttudviguṇenapramāṇataḥ
bhuvanānāṃ prabhusyānaṃ dvitīyaṃ samudā hṛtaṃ
tṛtīyetu mahāyogībhūtaiḥ parivṛtoramat
tatrāpibhavanaṃ divyaṃmāyeśavasatiḥ smṛtā
gṛhāṇicaiva divyānipracurā ṇimahāṃtica
agnisthānaṃparaṃ divyaṃ paṃcamaṃ samudāhṛtam
agnisthānātparatvena dviguṇaṃtavyamāṇataḥ
ugranāmaprabhusthānaṃṣaṣṭhaṃ tatsamudāhṛtam
tatrapāśupataiḥ sārdhaṃ yogibhiḥparameśvaraḥ
anugrahārthailokānāṃ krīḍatebha smaguṃṭhitaḥ
damapraśamasaṃyuktābhūtānāmabhayapradāḥ
yathoktakāriṇodāṃtāyoginastatparāyaṇāḥ
bhaikṣacaryā vratānityaṃdhyānatatparapūjakāḥ
yāṃtipāśupataṃsthānaṃpunarāvṛttidurlabham
tasmātpāśupatātsthānādviguṇenapramāṇa taḥ
māheśvaraṃ paraṃ sthānaṃ saptamaṃ samudāhṛtam
māheśvaraiḥparivṛtovasatebhūtabhā vanaḥ
tatravaisarvalokeśaīśvaraḥ kāmarūpadhṛk
āviśyasarvabhūtānilokānaṃdaṃkarotivai
nateṣāṃ parisaṃkhyā naṃpramāṇaṃvāpividyate
īpsitāṃstusṛjatyeṣabhūtānāmīśvaroyataḥ
ataḥ paraṃdvijaśreṣṭhasthirasthānamitismṛtam
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāmekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣayaūcuḥ
sanatkumārauvāca śṛṇuviprāidaṃ sthānaṃśivasyaparamātmanaḥ
yannapaśyaṃtidurvṛttābrahmādyādevasattamāḥ
sāṃkhyāvāpyathavāyogānavi dustadvidojanāḥ
nacaviṃdaṃtigṛtyāstu umānacagaṇeśvaraḥ
naviṣṇurnacarudraśvanacānyeddijasattamāḥ
tasyaivacaprasādena yathājñānaṃtathāśṛṇu
śataṃkoṭisahasrāṇāṃ yojanānāṃpramāṇataḥ
vāmanetrāddiniṣkrāṃtā umādevīca suvratā
vāmapārśvopaviṣṭācatasmādvaivāmalocanā
dakṣiṇānnayanānmuktojalabiṃduḥ sitaprabhā
sāsarveṣuca lokeṣugatāvaibhūrbhu vādikam
upasthāyemāṃgāṃprāptātasmādgaṃgeti cocyate
netrābhyāṃ prathamājjātāgaṃgetidvijasattamāḥ
brahmaṇoyatnaśīlasya īśvareṇa mahātmanā
tattṛtīyaṃtuvijñeyaṃkapālavadanaṃmayā
viṣṇu cakraṃcaturthatupaṃcamaṃdakṣa saṃbhavaḥ
ṣaṣṭhakaṃtuyadādevohimavaṃtaṃmahāmune
taruṇādityasaṃkāśairudraiḥ parivṛtovasat
āha
dṛṣṭāntaiti dṛṣṭanāśejagativiśeṣajñānajanikā vicāraṇāpravartateto'līkamevedamiti yathārthajñānaṃcasaṃbhavatyagocaranāśakaparivāraviṣayetukathaṃviśeṣa dvitīyaṃtuparīvāraṃtatodviguṇavistarāt
rudrāṇāṃ hemavarṇānātriṃśatkoṭyaḥ prakīrtitāḥ
aparāhṛṣṭavarṇānāṃ koṭyośī nirdvijottamam
paṃcamaṃtu parīvāraṃ tatādviguṇavistaram
ṣaṣṭhaṃtu saptamaṃcaivaṃ yerudrāstānnibodhata
manaḥśilābhāvimalāha ṣṭānirdiśyate sadā
evamaṣṭaparīvāraṃmānasaṃtumahātmanaḥ
naśakyaṃtasyavijñānaṃdṛṣṭāṃtetadvicāraṇā
sarvebrahma purogāśva sarve viṣṇupuraḥsarāḥ
evaṃ yovadatisthānaṃśuddhaṃ paramanāmayam
sopigacchetparaṃ sthānaṃliṃgaṃśivamanāmayam
kiṃpunaḥ śucayodāṃtāmaheśva raparāyaṇāḥ
evaṃbrahmakriyāyogīlokānāṃbhūtivādinām
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ śivamāhātmyaṃ nāmadvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
māhātmyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhutvaṃ vartateśive
vidhinātuṣyeta kenakapardīvṛṣavāhanaḥ
vinītaveśanapraveṣaḥ
avimuktaṃvārāṇasī
oṃkāraṃmahākālasthānamujjayinī etatḻāgalādi
śṛṇuvyāsaimāṃvāṇīṃsarvapāpabhayāpahām
vidhināyena tuṣyetalokānāṃ bhuvaneśvaraḥ
tamahaṃkīrta yiṣyāmiśṛṇutattvena me dvija
meruparva tamāsādyadevāyakṣāmahoragāḥ
īśvarasyacamāhātmyaṃ śrotukāmāḥ sthitāḥ purā
namaskṛtvāpravakṣyāmipurāṇaṃbrahmanirmitam
tasminvibhīṣaṇāṃgatvāsatyaśāṃtojiteṃdriyaḥ
vinītaveśobhavanamī śānaṃparipṛcchati
etanme saṃśayaṃ devabrūhitvaṃvṛṣabhadhvaja
īśvarauvāca
sa tyaṃśṭaṇumahābāhoyasmāttvaṃ paripṛcchasi
vibhīṣaṇa mahārājaśṛṇugutyaṃparaṃmama
chāgalāṃgaṃbhadra karṇa gokarṇacaviśe ṣataḥ
avimuktaṃcaoṃkāraṃ paṃcāyatanamuttamam
etāndṛṣṭvālabhenmokṣaṃ gulyametadudāhṛtam
oṃkāraṃcitayānasyatasya tuṣṭo'smyahaṃsadā
yatrasā kṣātsthitodevārudrāvāsetumuktidaḥ
agniprākārasaṃyuktaṃ parikṣitaṃsamaṃtataḥ
yogīśvare suvarṇākhye tathaiva vātikeśavaḥ
bhadradaṃḍī mahākālodevastaruvanesadā
kālaṃjare ugra saṃvaikarkaṭeśvaranāmaca
bhūteśvarevāmakūṭoviśvasthāneśva reti ca
gutyasthānapavitrāṇimamai tānivibhīṣaṇa
yetuvrajaṃtimaccittāmadbhaktāmatparāyaṇāḥ
teśreṣṭhāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃbhavaṃtīhavibhīṣaṇa
ayutānyarbudānkoṭīstathāpadmāyutānica
krīḍaṃtirudralokāṃstānsadharmoyaisturādhyate
teṣāṃ samastayuktānāṃpuru ṣāṇāṃvibhīṣaṇa
mlecchastrīnapuṃsakānāṃ tu krūrāṇāṃpāpa karmaṇām
yatratatramṛtānāṃtudhruvaṃ māheśvarīgatiḥ
aṣṭaugu tyapavitrāṇiyeyajaṃtikṣitaunarāḥ
teṣāṃtuṣṭaḥprayacchāmigāṇapatyaṃvibhīṣaṇa
tetumāṃpratipadyate madbhaktāmatparāya ṇāḥ
kiṃteṣāṃyajñadānena kriyābhiśvavibhīṣaṇa
tatphalaṃvyāsasakalaṃlabhatenātra saṃśayaḥ
ahorātraśataṃtrātvāyatphalaṃlabhate naraḥ
cāṃdrāyaṇaśataṃkṛtvāyatphalaṃlabhatenaraḥ
hiraṇyānāṃ sahasreṇayatphalaṃ prāpyatanaraḥ
gomūtrayāvakāhāraśākabhikṣāśanaistathā
brahmaghnaḥ pitṛhāgonaḥ surāpogurutalpagaḥ
puṇyaṃtulabhate nityaṃ liṃgārcanā dvibhīṣaṇa
ahaṃkartācahartācasraṣṭā cāpi yugeyuge
prabhavaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mahātmānātra saṃśayaḥ
ahaṃbahmācaviṣṇuśvasomaśvāhaṃmahāmune
tipadādyamāṃtaṃtathaivapāsakāse māyāmupoṣaṇena bhavati
lavaṇaḥ kṣārasamudraḥ
lohitaḥ śoṇabhadronāmanadaḥ
śivārcanenābhilaṣitasiddhimāha
śivoddeśe yatkicidṛśyatelokesarva cāhaṃvibhīṣaṇa
kāmaścaivāthavāyuśvanānāṛṣayaevaca
pūjyamānepramāṇeca ahaṃkṛtira saṃśayaḥ
vṛṣodharmaśvaskaṃdaśvasarva cāhaṃ vibhīṣaṇa
vasaṃtogrīṣmakālaśvahe mataḥ śiśirastathā
prāvṛṭkālaśvavijñeyaḥśaratkālomahānadī
vāsukīta kaścaiva anaṃtanāgarāṭtathā
pa rvatomaṃdaromeruḥ kailāsogaṃdhamādanaḥ
meruśvāhaṃtrikūṭaśvapāriyātraśca parvataḥ
caṃdrobudhaśvaśaileṃdro mainākaśvavibhīṣa ṇa
pralhādaśrvagatanhādaḥ kṣīrodesuramastathā
lavaṇaścaivavijñeyolohitaśvavibhīṣaṇa
sthāvaraṃjaṃgamaṃ caiva ahame konasaṃśayaḥ
varṣemāsāśvapakṣaśca ahorātraṃvibhīṣaṇa
dīpapradānaṃ yodadyādviprāyaśuddhamānasaḥ
tenadīpapradānena matpuraṃyātimānavaḥ
svarṇadānaṃ tuyodadyādgāṇapatyena yāmyaham
dāsyāmicagatiṃpuṇyāṃ gāṇapatyaṃcadurlabha
yajñairṣahuviśiṣṭānnairyatphalaṃ labhateddija
yathābhilaṣitaṃpu ṇyaṃtataḥsatphalavānubhavet
evaṃ prakṣālya doṣāṃ stunepyāmiparamāṃ gatim
karmaṇāmanasāvācādehenāpi cayatkṛtam
mamārcanaratānāṃ ca teṣāṃ pāpaṃnavidyate
yastusaṃvatsaraṃ puṇyaṃpūjayedekaliṃga ke
tasyatuṣṭaḥ prayacchāmigāṇapatyaṃnasaṃśa yaḥ
prabhāsaṃcaprayāgaṃcanaimipaṃ puṣkaraṃ tathā
tīrthako ṭisahasreṣu kadā cinnarādhamāḥ
mamārcanagataṃ puṇyaṃ labhaṃte cavibhīṣaṇa
hāyātreti
teṣāṃmadbhaktānām
puṇyakṣayādidoṣaśūnyam
namujhetetiśiva māitibhāvaḥ
namāṃpaśyaṃtitemṛḍhāmanasāyemlīkṛtāḥ
agnipraveśanaṃrutvātthāmāsopavāsakam
kaṃdareṣvathavāraṇyegṛhevāpisamāhitaḥ
yomāmarcayate nityaṃ tasyagāṇeśvarīgatiḥ
yaścainaṃ paṭhatenityaṃya vainaṃkīrtayennaraḥ
yaścaivaṃniyatobhūtvāmāhātmyaṃ dhārayiṣyati
caṃdrārkaunaprakāśeteyasmindeśepurāsadā
prakāśaṃtehimanujāstasmindeśesute jasā
māhātmyaṃ tu suraśreṣṭha sarvabhūtanamaskṛtam
māhātmyaṃ me tataḥ puṇyaṃ paṭhi pyaṃtinarāḥ śuci
dhārayiṣyaṃtiyecānye khaḍgadhārasudhāśuci
natepāṃ kilbiṣaṃkiṃcinmayituṣṭebhaviṣyati
vibhī paṇauvāca
akṣayaśvāprameyaśvapurāṇaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
tvaṃvāyustvaṃ hutāśaścatvaṃ śivodakṣiṇāmukhaḥ
tvaṃśuciḥ sāgaraścaiva bhaktānāṃca sureśvaraḥ
eṣohaṃtesuraśreṣṭha sarvabhūtanamaskṛta
tvaṃgatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃśaraṇaṃ tvaṃna saṃśayaḥ
bhavānmokṣobhavāniṃdrobhavānagniḥ sanātanaḥ
bhavāndharmeṣupuṇyeṣusaṃkalpaśvamanīṣiṇām
tvaṃcatuṣṭirva purmedhābuddhiḥ kāmye manastathā
śivaṃ puṇyaṃ prapaśyaṃtidevā ṛṣigaṇāstathā
bhavān mokṣaśvaśāṃtiścabhavān kṣetrajña ātmanaḥ
bhavāṃ stu sarvalokānāṃ nityaṃ harṣavivardhanaḥ
sarvataḥ pāṇipādāṃtasarvatokṣiśiromukha
yaścainaṃ paṭhate nityaṃśivaproktamaniṃditaḥ
vibhīṣaṇayathānyāyaṃnityaṃdevena pūjitam
paṭhedvāśṛṇuyāccaiva caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣuca
tasyadeyamidaṃśāstramanyathānaprakāśayet
maheśvara stavaṃ śrutvā svargagacchenna saṃśayaḥ
itiśrī śivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ trayodaśodhyāyaḥ
vyāsa uvāca
devayajñaphalānīhadā natīrthaphalānica
upavāsaphalaṃ caivadānānāṃ tapasaḥphalam
akṛtvā phalameteṣāṃ trāhmaṇovidaṃta katham
yatravākauśikīgaṃgādevī kāmārthamokṣadā
kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃcanaimiṣaṃpu ṣkaraṃtathā
trisrotācapayoṣṇīcatṛtīyāgaṃḍakītathā
brahmāvartānidīśvāyamunācātipāvanī
gaṃgādvāraṃsa hasrābhyaṃbhadrakarṇahṛdastathā
dṛṣadvatīkaratoyālohitāca mahānadī
sarayūgaṃḍakīcaiva sāgaraḥ saritāṃpatiḥ kokānadyāru ṇātāmrāramyaḥ śoṇomahānhadaḥ
godāvarīnarmadācanadī vetravatītathā
kāverīkṛṣṇavarṇācavitastācamahānadī
oṃ namaḥ śivāya caturdaśejagaliṃgājjātaṃ tiṣṭhatilī dābhyarcayedityanvayaḥ
ititrayodaśo'dhyāyaḥ
sārasvatānitīrthānikīrtitānimanīṣibhiḥ
śivaliṃgapraṇāmasyakalāṃ nārhatiṣoḍaśīm
ṣaṣṭikoṭisahasrāṇipa ṣṭikoṭiśatānica
ṣaṣṭitīrthasahasrāṇiparisaṃkhyāprakīrtitā
ako dhanaḥ śucirdakṣaḥ sarvatīrtha phalaṃṃlabhet
sarveṣāmeva tīrthānāṃ yatphalaṃ parikīrtitaṃ
vyāsauvāca
kathaṃ liṃgodbhavaṃ nāma trailokyaṃ sacarācaraṃ
liṃgārcanavidhiḥ kovāgatirvā kutraśā śvatī
kasmāccadakṣiṇāṃ mūrtimīśvarasyāmitaiaujasaḥ
ṛṣayaḥ pitarode vāyajaṃtesaṃśitavratāḥ
sanaḥ tkumārauvāca
ahaṃte kathayiṣyāmiśrūyatāṃ medvijottama
liṃgaṃcayā dṛśaṃtasyadevadevasya dhīmataḥ
pralayaṃcayathāliṃgetanmenigadataḥ śṛṇu
yathācapunarāvṛttiryathānāvartatepunaḥ
mayā śrutaṃyathāpūrva gadatātrahmaṇaḥ svayam
maheśvaraśvasṛṣṭyādau prakṛtyā sahasaṃgataḥ
prādurbhūtā mahāvāyustasmādagnirajāya ta
liṃgaṃtasmātsamudbhūtaṃsūryarāśisamaprabham
taccasaṃbhavateliṃgaṃkāṃcanaṃratnabhūṣitam
liṃgarājaṃ suvipulaṃ praśāṃtādityavarcasam
tatrabrahmādayodevāyajñāśvasahaviṣṇunā
talliṃgaṃ samanuprāptāthṛtasaṃjñāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ
pitāpājanakatvenapraśāṃtatvamitibhāvaḥ
hṛtasaṃjñāḥ ataevamuduḥkhitāḥ
jvālāmālācibhiḥ
jvālāmālāivācaṣitaiḥ
yaḥ śivaḥ
vegāvegamutpādayituṃ pravarta umāpativirūpākṣonīlakaṃṭhovilohitaḥ
satvaṃrajastamaścaiva kṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtistathā
sāṃkhyayogastathānadyogirayaḥ sāgarākrarhāḥ
pṛthivītyaṃtarikṣaṃcadiśaśvavidiśastathā
nakṣatrāṇigrahāścaiva māsāḥ saṃvatsarāstathā
līyatetatra liṃgecaīśvarasya mahātmanaḥ
liṃgādutpādayāmāsatrīnlokāntsacarācarān
brahmāṇamasṛjatputraṃprājāpatye'bhya ṣecayat
kṛtvāprajāpatideva devalokāgryamīśvaram
punarviṣṇuṃcasṛjate līlayāgarbhasaṃbhavam
smṛtiṃsaṃ kṣipya sarveṣāṃtatraivāṃtaradhīyata
pralayaṃcayathāliṃgetanmenigadataḥ śṛṇu
purātyekārṇavevyāsaharasyāmitatejasaḥ
jvālāmā lācibhirvyāptaṃ sarvabhūta bhayaṃkaram
evaṃbhūtaṃcaviṣṭabhya tiṣṭhatijvālamaṃḍale
datyaṃ sarvabhūtāni rudramāyāvimohitāḥ
sasurāsuragaṃdharvāḥ sayakṣoragarā kṣasāḥ
pṛthivyāpastathāvāyurākāśastejaevaca
yāniyānicabhūtānisthāvarāṇi carāṇica
tānyāruṣyaṃte sarvā ṇicarāṇicabhayasthale
teṣāmākṛṣyamāṇānāṃvegārthaṃ mūrchitonilaḥ
karotibhairavaṃ nādamākāśaṃpūrayanniva
jīvamātrāṇisarvāṇidagdhānituyathāgninā
saṃvṛttānīha tiṣṭhatithānyānicadahanniva
tatotrahmāsuraśreṣṭhodevāca sahaviṣṇunā
liṃgaṃtesamanuprāptānaṣṭasaṃjñāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ
bhītāścaivanirīkṣaṃtaḥśivamāyāvimohitāḥ
tataḥ suptāśvatedevāścakṣuṣmaṃtoyaśasvinaḥ
upalabhyasmṛtidevāstatraivaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
brahmāviṣṇuścaśakraścaūcustatraumāpatim
tvaṃkumāraḥ kumārastvaṃjātastvaṃsarvatomukhaḥ
oṃkārastvaṃva paṭkārodaṃḍa nītistathaivaca
viśaṃtihṛdayaṃ sarve bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ
brahmādevāścayajñāśvaśakraśvasahaviṣṇunā
evaṃ māyāparāsūkṣmāyayāpaśyāmaīśvaram
śivauvāca
yoginaśvamahārūpājñānaiśvarya samanvitāḥ
ajarāścāmarāścaiva matprasādādbhaviṣyatha
svacchaṃda gatayāṃnityaṃ svargaloke maheśvarāḥ
evamuktvā tubhagavāṃstatraivāṃtaradhīyata
punaḥsṛṣṭeṣu lokeṣubrahmātatraprajāpatiḥ
tribhirmāsairavāpnotiśivaliṃgārcane rataḥ
samyagiṣṭaphalāḥ sarve śāṃtādāṃtāḥ samādhitaḥ
navamāsāntsamārādhyabrāhmaṇovijiteṃdriyaḥ
hi mavānmaṃdaromeruḥkailāsogaṃdhamādanaḥ
vālakhilyāścaṛṣayonaimiṣeyāsta podhanāḥ
yāścaivāpsarasodivyāyecamātṛgaṇāstathā
tārāgaṇāgrahagaṇāḥ sarvepitṛgaṇāstathā
cāraṇoduṃbarāścaivaviyā siddhāstathaivaca
pramāṇaṃparamaṃ jñātvāliṃgaṃyo'rcayate naraḥ
tasminbahuguṇāṃprītikarotivṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
ekānhitadavāpnotiśivaliṃgārcanerataḥ
trīṇyaṣṭauyānisthānāniyatphalaṃlabhatenaraḥ
ekāhaṃtadavāpnotivipro liṃgārcane rataḥ
kumāro brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
naṃdīśvarogaṇaśreṣṭhomahā kālaścavīryavān
bhṛṃgvaṃgirāmarīciśvadadhīciśvayamastathā
saṃvartaḥsaṃjigīṣuśvatathāśukrabṛhaspatī
dakṣaḥprajāpatiḥ śreṣṭhodakṣaputrāstusamavai
atrirvasiṣṭhobhagavānkāśyapaśvamahātapāḥ
gautamaśvabharadvājoviśvāmitraśvakovidaḥ
ādityāvasavo rudrāmarutaśvatathāśvinau
sādhyāvidyādharānāgāṛṣayoviśvadevatāḥ
kṣārodaḥpuṣkarogaṃgāśmaśānānicasarvaśaḥ
krīḍate bhagavānbhūtairbālaḥ krīḍanakairiva
eṣakārayate karmatena smovyākulīkṛtāḥ
brahmādyāṛṣayodevāstanme nigadataḥ śṛṇuḥ
brahmāviṣṇuśvaśakraścacaṃdrādityausamī raṇaḥ
yamaḥkālaśvamṛtyuśvavaruṇodhanadonalaḥ
upacāraviśeṣeṇaphaletāratamyaṃvadati
daśasāvarṇikaṃpaṃcakṛṣṇalakomāṣaitimānamanusṛtyaṣaṣṭyadhikaśatamāṣasuvarṇanirmitaṃ
saṃvatsaraṃtapobhaktyāvalmīkamṛttikāsuca
puṣpopahāra dhūpaiśvatulyaṃ phalamavāpnuyāt
daśāparādhāṃstoyenakṣīreṇaivaśataṃkṣamet
kṣīrasrānaṃ ghṛtābhyaṃgaḥ saghṛtaṃguggulaṃtathā
daśasauva ṇikaṃpuṣpaṃyobhavāyaprayacchati
yaṃyaṃkāmayate kāmaṃtaṃtaṃ pūrayateśivaḥ
mālayāśatasāhakhyājāpyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ smṛtaṃ
vidhiyajñājjapayajñoviśiṣṭodaśabhirguṇaiḥ
upāṃśusyācchataguṇaḥ sahasromānasaḥ smṛtaḥ
tṛṇānyauṣadhigulmāni latāvallīstathaivaca
tathaiva sarvavṛkṣāṇāṃ puṣpaṃ patraṃ phalaṃtvacaṃ
kāla jānisupuṣpāṇibījāniśatadhātathā
mahādevopayuktānisvargayāṃtinasaṃśayaḥ
śraddadhānastu yaḥ kuryācchuciḥpraya tamānasaḥ
prāpyaduḥkhaṃna te sarve svargayāṃtidvijottamāḥ
viśvedevāśvakārye ṇaśrutaṃ pūrvaṃ yathānaraiḥ
liṃgaṃcasthāpayettatravidhipūrvaṃsamāhitaḥ
saṃvatsaraṃtuśuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvātatraśucirnaraḥ
pūjā śvakārayennityaṃ tasyabhaktyāśivenavai
ṭī sanatku
pūjārthapratyahaṃ yastu gaṃdhamālyāsa taṃ śubham
yonasaṃpādayenmāhātpāpakṛnna sadhārmikaḥ
saṃpādayedataḥ pūjāṃpradṛṣṭenāṃtarā tmanā
ciraparyuṣitaṃmālyaṃbhavasyāpanayeccayaḥ
gosahasra phalaṃpuṇyaṃprāpnuyānnātra saṃśayaḥ
apūrvasya caliṃgasyaśuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ
stri yaḥśūdrāśvamlecchāśvayecānyepāpayonayaḥ
namaskāropyanujñātomaṃtrapraṇavava jitaḥ
śūdrāṇadeivabhaktānāṃ mahādevena dhīmatā
puṇyābhiradbhiḥ snānaṃ cacaṃdanenānulepanam
puṣpavāso pahāraiśva satataṃcanivedanaiḥ
sauvarṇairājataiḥ kuṃbhairmṛnmayauduṃbare stathā
apyaiśvavividhaiḥ śuddhaiḥ sabhṛṃgārairhiraṇmayaiḥ
iṃdranīlai mahānīlairvajñavaiḍūrya ke stathā
satataṃ cārcayeddevaṃ śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ
trikālamarcayedde vaṃśuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ
mūrtayopiśivasyaitāstanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu
yogamūrtiśvaprathama aiṃdrīīdrasamāsthitā
dvitīyādakṣiṇāmūrtiryāsamāvṛtyatiṣṭhati
tṛtīyāvāruṇīmūrtiḥ paśvimātuṣṭidāmama
caturthīsyāttuvaradādhanadāsu sukhāvahā
adhastātpaṃcamīmūrtiścacāravidhinātapaḥ
vedayajñagatiḥ ṣaṣṭhīvaiṣṇavīgatiriṣyate
ūrdhvacamūrtirāgneyī sarvabhūtapramardinī
praśatāniṣkalāmūrtiḥ sarvabhūtasukhāvahā
yatibhiḥsevyatevyāsajarāmaraṇabhīrubhiḥ
anenavidhināvyāsayaśvajānātiīśvaram
tenapāśupataṃ cīrṇavimalaṃvratamavyayam
śivaṃ sarvagataṃjñātvāsarvaduḥkhaiḥ pramucyate
evaṃ vijñāyamedhāvī bhaikṣavṛttisamācaret
mūrtīnāṃpravibhāgaśca śivaliṃgārcanaṃtathā
vidhayovividhāḥ śreṣṭhāyaiśvatuṣyatiśaṃkaraḥ
sarvāsāmapimūrtīnāṃ pūjārhadakṣiṇāparā
sācasṛjatibhūtānitathāsaṃharate prajāḥ
vṛttiśraddhāṃ sukhaṃ kāmaṃ medhāṃcaiva prayacchati
vividhānvidate kāmānmūrtiḥ sā dakṣiṇāparā
pārāśaryasadāyuktodakṣiṇāmūrtimarcayet
bhāvona yatisarvasvaṃniṣkalaṃcā yaṃdadet
etatte kathitaṃ vyāsaśivaliṃgārcanaṃparam
śraddhākāmasamāyuktāsteyāṃtipara māṃgatim
darśanācchravaṇāddāpināmasaṃkīrtanādapi
pramāṇaṃcaiva liṃgasya śrutvāpāpaiḥ pramucyate
striyaḥ śūdrāśvamle cchāśvayecānyepāpayonayaḥ
aśvamedhaphalaṃsamyaglabhaṃtenā'yasaṃśayaḥ
śraddhākāmasamāyuktāsteyāṃtiparamāṃ gati
śivanāmetihāsoyaṃbrahmaṇāsamudāhṛtaḥ
krodhamohapraśamano mahāpātakanāśanaḥ
yaścainaṃ paṭhate nityaṃ yaścainaṃśṭaṇuyānnaraḥ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃnāma kīrtanaṃnāmacatudarśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
sthānāniyānilokesminyeṣusannihitaḥ sadā
pramā ṇaṃcaiva sarveṣāṃteṣuyacchatyanugraham
satāṃtubhajanesamyaktuṣyatevākathaṃtataḥ
śṛṇuvyāsaparāṃvāṇīṃ sarvalokahitāṃ śubhām
yeṣusthāneṣubha gavān sānnidhyaṃ kurutesadā
nānārūpadharodevaḥ sarvabhūteṣuvartata
brahmā divākaroviṣṇuḥ skaṃdaścāgniḥ puraṃdaraḥ
arkaḥ somaḥ kuberaśvavaruṇaśvāpyumāpatiḥ
yohiyāṃdevatāṃ bhaktyā ārādhayatisarvataḥ
tasyatāṃmūrtimāsthāya mahāde vaḥprasīdati
sthānānāṃ parisaṃkhyānaṃ vaktuṃśakto nacakvacit
apivarṣasahasrairvāsamāsenatu me śṛṇu
ihaloketuyānya ṣṭausthānāniśṭaṇutāni me
pramāṇaṃcaiva sarveṣāṃteṣuyovāpyanugrahaḥ
māheśvarīmimāṃsṛṣṭiśucirbhūtvāniśāmaya
nā mnārudrapadaṃśreṣṭhatathāmāheśvaraṃ padam
śleṣmātakaṃtathāproktamavimuktaṃ mahālayam
gokarṇabhadrakarṇecasvarṇākhyaṃ sthāna maṣṭamam
sthāneṣveteṣusatataṃsāṃnidhyaṃ kurute bhavaḥ
māheśvaretubhagavānnityaṃpūjyastuśaṃkaraḥ
dviyojanaṃ tuta kṣetraṃ dakṣiṇottarataḥ smṛtam
vista reṇatutāvaddhievaṃ māheśvaraṃ padam
hamāsthāyaśivaevakarotītyāhayaiti
māheśvaraṃcolīmaheśvaraitināmnāloke prasiddham
avimuktaṃ vārāṇasī
mahālayamoṃkā
praviśaṃtimṭatāstatraparāṃmāheśvarīṃtanum
yakṣaiśvarāsa saiścaiva piśācaiḥ pannagaistathā
caturdaśaṃyojanaṃcatattuśle ṣmātakaṃsmṛtam
devadānavagaṃdharvāṛṣayaśvatapodhanāḥ
saṃpūjyasa tataṃśreṣṭhāḥsadārudrapadebhavam
viṣṇuḥ somaśvaśakraśca ādityāmaruto'śvinau
ardhayojanavistīrṇasuvarṇākhyaṃvidurbudhāḥ
vārāṇasyāṃtuoṃkāragamyoviśveśvaraḥ sadā
pū jyate bhagavāndevaḥparamātmāsanātanaḥ
viśveśvaraṃtuoṃkāraṃpra ṇamaṃtistuvaṃtica

vedavidyāvrataparāḥ siddhāśvaparamarṣayaḥ
upāsatesadāvyāsapaṃcāyatanavāsi nam
aciṃtyānāmatatrasthātanurdevasyanirvṛtiḥ
viśaṃticamahātmānaḥ parāṃmāheśvarīṃ tanum
brahmācāgniśvasomaśvaviṣṇuriṃdrobṛhaspatiḥ
upāsate mahābhāgaṃ bhadrakarṇe sadāśivam
tatrāhaṃniyatovyāsagaṃgādvārebhavapriye
etanmahādhanaṃnāmapurāṇaṃpuṇyamuttamam
teṣusthāneṣuvai pūrvamṛṣayaḥ siddhimāgatāḥ
divyāmāheśvarābhogāḥśa ktiryatrākṣayāparā
sthānamāhātmyamatulaṃpuṇyapāpapraṇāśanam
nānyabhaktāya dātavyaṃpiśunāyaśaṭhāya ca
ślāghineślāghamānāyaimaṃdharmyaprakāśayet
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃpaṃcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
sarvāṇi yānitīrthāniguptā nyāyatanānica
anugrahaṃcaya tteṣāṃ puṇyaṃ caiva hiśaṃsame
nahimetṛptirastīha śṛṇvatovākyamuttamam
māhātmyadeva devasyaśaṃkarasyamahātmanaḥ
thṛṣyāmisatataṃbrahmanparaṃ kautūhalaṃhime
sana tkumāraḥ provācavācāmadhurayātadā
śṛṇuvyāsaparāṃvāṇīṃvicitrāṃpāpanāśinīm
maṃgalāṃca pavitrāṃcapaṭhetparvasuparvasu
idaṃ sthānamāhātmyaṃ
itipaṃcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya sthānāṣṭakasyamāhātmyaṃ
uktasthānānāṃyātrāyāvidhimāha
rājasūyāśvamedhānitajjanyāniphalānītyarthaḥ
eṣusthāneṣumaraṇasya phalamāha
iṃdralokaṃsagacchettu dhārayaṃstusadāśuciḥ
yānyuktānipavitrāṇisvayaṃ devena dhīmatā
tānite kathayiṣyāmitasmādekama nāḥ śṛṇu
chāgalāṃḍaṃ kuruḍevāmukuṭamaṃḍaleśvaram
kālaṃjaraṃ vanaṃ caiva gadagaṃḍasthaleśvaram
eteṣucasadāvyāsa bhūtasaṃghairṭa taḥ prabhuḥ
vasateparayāprītyā pūjyamānodivaukasaiḥ
caturdaśayojanānāṃ sarveṣāṃ hiparigrahaḥ
ṛṣigaṃdharva juṣṭānisidvai rvācaritānica
sthānānyetānigutyāni rudreṇa sagaṇenave
vyuṣitāni sadāvyāsadevadevenaśaṃbhunā
pitṝṃśvatarpayettatraśṭaṇutasyāpiyatphalam
rājasūyāśvamedhāniprāpnuvaṃtinasaṃśayaḥ
yovaipātayateprāṇānaśṭaṇutasyā piyāgatiḥ
viśaṃtitumahādevaṃpa titāstyaktajīvitāḥ
munigaṇaparivṛtaṃmahātridaśagaṇairabhiṣṭutaṃpriyam
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ śreṣṭhākhyānaṃnāmaṣoḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ
phalabhogāḥsakāmānāṃca huśaśvamahāyaśāḥ
gutyānāmapigutyāniśṭaṇuvyāsasamāhitaḥ
yathācabhagavāndevaḥ rutavāṃścāpya nugraham
purāvaiṛṣayovyāsaṃpapracchurdagdhakilbiṣāḥ
vālakhilyāśvamunayastathābhāgavatābhavan
bhaktyātutoṣabha gavānbhaktānāṃ bhaktavatsalaḥ
śravaṇaphalamāha
munīti
viṣamamidaṃchaṃdaḥ
itiṣoḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥśivāya athasaptadaśevyā
kṛtavānanugrahaṃteṣāṃdarśanena maheśvaraḥ
tepraṇamya mahātmānobhūtānāmīśvaraṃprabhum
ūcuḥprāṃjalayobhūtvāvālakhilyā stapodhanāḥ
manasāprārthitaṃyacca tatkartāsaunasaṃśayaḥ
tataste prīta manasodṛṣṭvādevaṃvṛṣadhvajam
eṣadevaparaḥ pāroyaha ṣṭobhagavānsvayam
icchāmo bhagava njñātuṃgukhyānyāyatanānica
evaṃprasāditastaistumunibhiḥpuṇyakāṃkṣkṣibhiḥ
uvācatānṛṣīnsarvānvākyenajīvayanniva
śrīmahārudrauvāca
śrūyatāṃ paramaṃgutyaṃ yeṣunityaṃvasāmyaham
sṛjāmityanugṛhṇāmibhaktyāparamayāsadā
tānivaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmitīrthānicamahītale
śṛṇvaṃtuṛṣayaḥ sarve śuci śraddhāsamanvitāḥ
mahāpuraṃcakrapuraṃ gutyaṃśrīparvataṃtathā
jāpyeśvaraṃtatogutyaṃgutyamāghāḍikeśvaram
tathāma hākālapuraṃ gutyaṃmadhyamakeśvaram
etāndṛṣṭvātuyobhaktyātasya tuṣyāmyahaṃsadā
gulyasthānecayeyomāṃbha ktyāvaiśraddhayānvitaḥ
akāmovāsakāmovāgutyeṣveṣucayonaraḥ
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyovāpivaiśyaḥ śūdrastathaiva ca
mlecchāvākūrakarmāṇaḥ stri yovāpinasaṃśayaḥ
gāṇapatyaṃdhuvasthānamiṃdraloke mahīyate
pitṝṇāṃ 'caiva makṣayyaṃ sthāneṣveteṣu yonaraḥ
śrāddhaṃdayānmahābhāgodadyādvāpitilodakam
darbhāstaraṇasaṃkīrṇe piṃḍaṃsthānenive bhyaca
vaṃtiparāṃ gatim
tasmādvidvānadhīyīta śrāvayecca samāhitaḥ
nāpraśāṃtāyadātavyaṃna cā'nyāhitakāriṇe
karkaśāyā viśuddhāyapiśunāyaśaṭhāyaca
capalāyanṛśaṃsāyanadeyaṃsyātkathaṃcana
idaṃtuśreṣṭhaputrāyaśiṣyāyavahitāyaca
ślāghineślāghamānāyapraśāṃtāyatapasvine
priyaṃvadāyaśrotriyāya bhaktāyaca maheśituḥ
yatinecatathādeyaṃ tathājñā smādbhutyamitismṛtam
gatvātapasyatonityaṃmānasaṃvi malaṃśivam
tatrāhaṃniyatovipragaṃgādvārecanityaśaḥ
ādyasthāneṣu eteṣu pūjayaṃti sadāśivam
gacchaṃtivimalāḥ śuddhāḥ padaṃ māheśvaraṃhite
nateṣāṃpunarāvṛttirbhavammṛtyurmahātmanām
eṣaīśvarasadbhāvaḥ kathitaste samāsataḥ
yaṃ syopatiṣṭhati
etatte kathitaṃpuṇyaṃgutyānāṃcaiva kīrtanam
kīrtitaṃsuma hāpuṇyaṃ satyenaiva mahāmune
iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ māheśvaravarṇanaṃnāmasaptadaśodhyāyaḥ
itisaptadaśo udhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
mahādevaśvaviṣṇuśvabrahmācaiva hisuvrata
prabhāvaiḥ karmaṇāṃcaivakodhikovadaīśvaraḥ
etanme saṃśayaṃtāta brūhibuddhimatāṃvara
atrāpyudāharaṃtīmamitihāsaṃ purā tanam
purātrailokyavijayeviṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
balirbaddhomahārājatrailokyaṃprāptavāṃstadā
athājagmuḥ prabhuṃ draṣṭuṃ devadevaṃ sanātanam
yatrāsauviśvarūpākṣaḥ kṣīrodasyasamīpataḥ
siddhā vidyādharānāgānadyaḥsarvāśvaparvatāḥ
dṛṣṭavāṃ baragatāviṣṇuṃ devadevaṃ sanātana jasiprabho
tvatprasādācca kalyāṇaṃ prāptaṃ trailokyamavyayam
asurāścahatāḥ sarve baddhaścaiva balistathā
sthāpitaṃca tvayāpūrvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṃgamam
tvaṃgatiḥsarvadevānāṃtvaṃyogīprabhuravyayaḥ
evamuktaḥ surairviṣṇuḥ siddhaiśvaparamarṣibhiḥ
pratyuvācatatoviṣṇuḥsarvagaḥpuruṣottamaḥ
viṣṇuruvāca
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmikāraṇaṃ surapuṃgavāḥ
yastuṣṭaḥ sarvabhū tānāṃkhaṣṭṛtvamadadācchivaḥ
sṛṣṭāśvabrahmaṇācaiva saptalokāśvamāyayā
tasyaiva caprabhāvena ahaṃ śreṣṭhatvamāgataḥ
tadavastheṣu bhūteṣuekohaṃśayitastathā
sahasraśīrṣovaibhūtvā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasra pāt
śaṃkhacakragadāpāṇirmāyayāvimalāṃbhasi
etasminnaṃtaredūrātpaśyāmivimalaṃprabhum
kṛṣṇājinadharaṃdevaṃka maṃḍaluvibhūṣitam
dāditi
asurāśveti
gatiḥ śaraṇam
kāraṇaṃsarvasyabrahmāṃḍasyetiśeṣaḥ
grasitaṃnigīrṇa
nimiṣāṃtaramātreṇaprāptavānpuruṣottamaḥ
kastvaṃ kutovākiṃśeṣetattvatovada kiṃciram
ahaṃkartāsmilokānāṃ svayaṃbhūrviśvatomukhaḥ
mayāpyudāhṛtaṃtrahmannanārāyaṇaḥprabhuḥ
dhātākartācalo kānāṃsaṃhartācajagatprabhuḥ
evaṃsaṃbhāṣamāṇau parasparamititadā
uttarāṃdiśamāsthāyajvālāṃ paśyāmitiṣṭhatīm
tatastāṃ jvālāmālokyavismayāviṣṭamānasaḥ
taddṛṣṭvāparamāśvaryamubhauvismita mānasau
divaṃ bhuvaṃ caviṣṭabhya tiṣṭhatejvālamaṃḍalam
prādeśamātraṃ duḥprekṣyaṃ durnirūpyaṃcaduḥsaham
mahākāyaṃ mahātejovardhamā namivaujasā
jvālamālādibhirvyāmaṃ sarvabhūtabhayaṃkaram
tatomāṃ prābravīdbrahmā apyahaṃ tvatsamanvitaḥ
atyaṃtaṃcavijānīyāṃliṃgasyāsyamahātmanaḥ
tvaṃcādhastādvijānīhi aṃtaṃtasya mahātmanaḥ
evaṃcasamayaṃkṛtvāgata ūrdhvatyadhotyahaṃ
varṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇivimṭaśaṃtau parasparam
nacapaśyāmitasyāṃ taṃtataḥ śramavaśādaham
tayaivabrahmāsaṃśrāṃto aṃtaṃcaivanapaśyati
māyayāmohitītenanaṣṭasaṃjñāvubhautathā
dhyānādrudhvāmahādevamīśvaraṃ sarvatomukhaṃ
prabhavaṃ nidhanaṃcaivabhūtā nāṃbhṛtamavyayam
rodasīdyāvābhūmī
atyaṃtaṃsīmām
paśyāmi apaśyam
lakāraḥ
brahmāṃjalipuṭobhūtvātasmaiśarvāyaśūline
parameṣṭhiparaṃbrahmaparamātmāparaṃ padam
tvaṃyajñastvaṃvaṣaṭkārastvamoṃkāraḥ paraṃ padaṃ
svāhākāronamaskāraḥ sarvakarmasusūktavān
svāhākā raśvajāpyaśvavratāniniyamānica
kāmaḥ krodhodbhavaṃ duḥkhamicchādveṣodamaḥ śamaḥ
kriyācavyādhayaścaiva tvaṃpaścātsukhaduḥkhayoḥ
ṛtavovatsaṃrāścaiva vidyāvidyenalastathā
iṃdriyāṇāṃ sarveṣā miṃdriyārthāśrvate smṛtāḥ
sthaviṣṭhāścaiva sūkṣmāścabhagavāneva sarvaśaḥ
viśvarūpomahārūpaḥsarvarūpastathaiva ca
te jasateiparaṃtejaḥsparśānāṃsparśamevaca
rūpagaṃdharasā āpodhipaścabhuvaneśvaraḥ
ākāśastvaṃ ca vai chaṃdobhūtānāṃ prabhuravya yaḥ
tvaṃ kartā sarvabhūtānāṃlokeṣu pralayāṃtakṛt
tvaṃdhārayasilokāṃstrīṃstvamevassṛjasiprabho
paścimenatuvatreṇavaruṇa stvaṃprakāśase
ādityāvasa vorudrāvaruṇaśvatathāśvinau
siddhāvidyādharānāgāapsaroyakṣarākṣasāḥ
siddhābrahmarṣayaścaivacāraṇāśvatapodhanāḥ
vālakhilyāśvaṛṣayastapaḥsiddhāḥ sahasraśaḥ
tvattaḥ prasūtādeveśa akṣarāśvamahābalāḥ
sahasraśīrṣonaṃtaścava survā sukirevaca
varuṇaśvamahātejāgaruḍaśvamahābalaḥ
arthodharmaśvakāmaśvayaśomohaḥ samīraṇaḥ
agniścaivama hāvviśvaprajātāste maheśvara
ramāsītātathākālīdevīgāyatrirevaca
yetyatramayosasīti pāṭhāṃtaram
paśvāditi
akṣarājarāmaraṇaśūnyāḥ
lakṣmīḥkīrtirdhṛtiḥsiddhirmedhālajjāvapuḥsmṛtiḥ
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭistathānaṃdāja yādevīsarasvatī
tvattojātāmahābhāgaa nyecāpi mahābalāḥ
ṛtuḥ saṃvatsaromāsaḥ pakṣo'horātra eva ca
kalākāṣṭhā nimeṣāśvamuhūrtāścala vāstathā
nakṣatrā ṇigrahāścaiva aśvāgāvo ajāvikāḥ
rajobhirmāyayāchannaṃ natvāṃ paśyaṃti kevalam
yoginonityamuktāyepaśyaṃtitvāṃ budhāstathā
māyayāmohitaṃ lokaṃtvatpadaṃcasanātanam
natvāṃpa śyaṃtisaṃmūḍhā magnātamasidāruṇe
ādaumadhyetathācāṃtenavidaṃtikadācana
parātparastvaṃparamaṃcaśāśvataṃ
namostutebhasmavibhūtiśīlanamostutekāmaśarīranāśin
namonageṃdrātmakadeva nityaṃ namostu te śaṃkara nīlakaṃṭha
paṭṭiśamasijātīyaṃkṣepaṇīyaṃśastram
saevaheturbhūtvā jagatkāraṇaṃbhūtvā sarvajidbhavatītiśeṣaḥ
ityaṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
evaṃsaṃstūyamāno hi kīrtyamāno maheśvaraḥ
babhāṣe catathātuṣṭaīśānovaradaḥ prabhuḥ
ādidevo mahāyogīsūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ
ekagrīvaḥ sujaṭharonānābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
nānāmaṇivicitrāṃgonānāgaṃdhānulepanaḥ
pinākadīpitakaraḥ paṭṭiśāśani śūladhṛk
vyālayajñopavītī cacīravastra bhayaṃkaraḥ
muktohāsastadātenalo kāstatraprakaṃpitāḥ
tataḥ provāca bhagavānprītothāpyāvayostathā
ayaṃmedakṣiṇobā hurbrahmātvaṃhimamātmajaḥ
vāmabāhuśvameviṣṇusaṃyuge tva parājitaḥ
munayaḥ sadṛśaṃsamyakvaraṃ vṛṇutasuvratau
tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasaupādayoḥ patitāvubhau
evamuktaḥ suraśreṣṭhaḥ sṛjadhvaṃ vipulāḥ prajāḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥprabhāvastasya yoginaḥ
tena sarvamidaṃ dṛṣṭaheturbhūtvātu sarvajit
idaṃ casvargyamāyuṣyamidaṃśāṃtikaraṃtathā
tasyavighnaṃ kurvatidānavāgraharākṣasāḥ
piśācāyātudhānāśvagulya kā bhuja gāstathā
yaḥ paṭhetaśuciḥ prātarbrahmacārījiteṃdriyaḥ
itiśrīśi vamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ liṃgodbhavanāmā'ṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
abhyaṃgecaiva kiṃproktaṃ kṣīratrāneca kiṃ phalam
saptānāṃsomasaṃsthānāṃyatphalaṃ samudāhṛtam
phalaṃvaisarvakāmyānāṃphalaṃba husuvarṇakam
ayutārbudakoṭīnāṃ teṣāmaṣṭauyutānica
krīḍaṃterudrapārśvatuputravatparipāli tāḥ
striyovāpuruṣovāpiyadivāthanapuṃsakaḥ
māse māsetuyaḥ strāyādyāva jjīvaṃrutīśuciḥ
gaṃdhadānenatatpuṇyaṃprāpnuyānnātra saṃśayaḥ
gaṃdhādabhyaṃgadānena ṣaṣṭikoṭyastathaiva ca
catuḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇigavāṃvehemamālinām
yodadyātkapilānāṃtukṣīrasnānasya yatphalam
māsemāsetriṣavaṇaṃyaḥstrāyā nmunipuṃgavaḥ
pakṣepakṣecayaḥsnāyādyāvajjīvaṃdvijaḥ śuciḥ
aparādhaśataṃdevaḥ kṣamatenātra saṃśayaḥ
puṣpadānenatatpuṇyaṃprāpnuyānnātra saṃśayaḥ
utpalaṃkaravīraṃca arkapallavakāṃstathā
āghāti ājighrati
nāgapuṣpaṃ nāgacampakapuṣpam caṃpakaṃbilvapatraṃcadevedeyaṃsadānaraiḥ
kālaśvateṣāṃsaṃproktastanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu
apāmārgakuśāṃścaiva āśvayuktenivedayet
sadāsitānipuṣpāṇiyāvatkālaṃ nivedayet
caturṇāṃ puṣpajātīnāṃgaṃdhamāghrātiśaṃkaraḥ
utpalānāṃsahasreṇa arka me kaṃviśiṣyate
caṃpakānāṃ sahasreṇadhattūraṃcaviśiṣyate
dhattūra kasahasreṇanāgapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate
siṃdhupuppasahasreṇapunnāgaṃtuviśiṣyate
punnāgānāṃ sahasreṇakarṇikāraṃviśiṣyate
siṃdhupuṣpasahasaistu bṛhatīnāṃviśiṣyate
bilvapatrātparaṃnāstiyenatuṣyati śaṃkaraḥ
sarveśuddhāḥsugaṃdhāḍhyākṛṣṇanaiva nivedayet
yatraikaṃbilvapatrasyacatuḥṣaṣṭirudāhṛtam
yathālābhaṃyathāpakṣaṃ puṣpāṇinivedayet
alābhenatupuṣpāṇāṃparṇānitunivedayet
viśeṣeṇatuyobhaktyāteṣāmekaphalaṃśśṛṇu
saviṃdatimahāpuṇyaṃrudrasāyujyamāvrajet
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ puṣpasāra samuddeśonāmaikonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
bhūyaevāhamicchāmiīśvarārādhanaṃ katham
janaprakāramabhidhāyajñānināṃ phalasaṃsargavimukhānāṃ pūjāprakāramāha
itiekonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
sulopābhāva ārpaḥ
śivaprītayekāñcanadānasya phalamāha
gaṇeśvarapatirnadī sūryāyutasamaprabhaḥ
īśvarasya tu māhātmyaṃ pṛcchate naṃdikeśvaraḥ
yathoktaṃ pṛcchate devyāīśvareṇa mahātmanā
naṃdikeśvarauvāca
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmitava snehānmahāmune
maheśvareṇapārvatyāḥ puratobhi hitaṃpurā
yatrāhaṃtatra sonityaṃ bhavedaṣṭaguṇānvitaḥ
tasya haimavate śṛṃge gṛhaṃbālārkasannibham
yastugāvo hiraṇyaṃvāsa muddiśyapradāpayet
tasyakāmadughāṃ pṛthvīṃ dadāminirupadravām
upahāraiśvajāpyaiśvabhāvitaiśvāpinityaśaḥ
agniṣṭomādibhiryajñairyomā'rcayatiśobhane
śa kasyārdhāsanaṃ prāpyasuraloke mahīyate
sayakṣāṇāṃ gururbhūtvāyakṣobhava tivīryavān
sthāpanā'bhyarcanāmālyairdhūpagaṃdhānulepanaiḥ
jātarūpaiśvarūpyaiśva arcayaṃtisureśvaram
liṃge pūjāṃtuyādevīkarotima maśobhane
abhyaṃgenapaṃcaśataṃ strāpanedviguṇaṃ bhavet
kṣīraṃpaṃcaśataṃdevistrāpa netu caturguṇam
mālyepaṃcaśataṃ devi gītavādyavarapriye
agaruṃśatasāhasaṃ daśaguṇaṃcaṃdanaṃbhavet
gaṃdhaṃdaśaguṇaṃ sarvayathoktaṃtadanaṃtaraṃ
mālyaṃpaṃcaśataṃdevinirmālyaṃ tadanaṃtaram
caturguṇa sahasraṇidhūpaḥ kṛṣṇāguruḥ smṛtaḥ
aparādhasahasraṃca kṣamate dubhāṣiṇi
yadidaṃ kṛṣṇasāraṃ tugugguluṃsaghṛtaṃ dahet
dakṣiṇāyāṃtumanmuktaudivyānāṃ ca ghṛtaprado
akṣa bhaktasamānaṃtudevaṃ sarvaharaṃśi vam
ghṛtābhiṣekaṃyaḥkuryātsaṃvatsaramataṃdritaḥ

caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyāmubhaupakṣauvidhānataḥ

taḥ
jātikāletyādināniṣṭhāparanipātaḥ
śivadhyāne'ntarāyānāha
bhāvanāṃdhyānaṃvināpividhinācitaḥbha ktyāyathābhāvitaivaphalaṃdāsyāmi anyathā'bhābakānāmarcanaṃvinānetyanvayaḥ
arcāyāṃpratimāyāmacitonatathātuṣyā miyathā lage'citastu tasyapuṇyaphalaṃdevimatprasādādidaṃśśṛṇu
śrutimātreṇayedevimamabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ
gāṇapatyaṃhiteṣāṃ vai dadāmikamalānane
yathāsthānāni sarvāṇima yābhiracitānivai
maheśvarītathāteṣumṛtyutonakadābhayam
yastukāmakṛtaṃtyaktvāekabhaktikṛtonaraḥ
kāya vāṅmanaḥ saṃyuktoyāvajjīvaṃtugacchati
devitiṣṭhatitāvacca yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
aneka vighnasaṃbhūtātamasābahulī kṛtāḥ
vyādhitānityayogasthāḥ satyasaṃdhājiteṃdriyāḥ
ekāgramanasonityaṃpaśyaṃtiniścitāśvaye
narāṇāmalpavittānāṃvidhinābhāvanāṃvinā
arcanaṃ cayathoktaṃvaigutyaṃvāpimataṃ śṛṇu
liṃgārcitoyayātasyatuṣyāmihariṇekṣaṇe
arcitohaṃvarārāhepūjitaḥ sarvadaivataiḥ
dhūpairgedhaiśvamālyaiścaraktakāṃcanavāsasaiḥ
karātroṣito martyaḥ puṃḍarīka phalaṃ labhet
bhaktyāparamayāyuktāḥ sakhyiyogaviśāradāḥ
gacchaṃtimama lokāṃstubhinnomattaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
tapasātunaśaknotidraṣṭuṃ māṃ devatāapi
dhyānenaiva niyuktāmāṃ paśyaṃtidevinānyathā
sarvalokeṣu sarveṣāṃsāṃkhyānārāyaṇī stutiḥ
madbhaktānāṃtu sarveṣāṃ saṃkhyādevina vidyate
kṣīyaṃ sarvabhūtānisthāvarāṇicarāṇica
vināśomamabhaktānāṃsaṃhārepinavidyate
yobhūyodevatāyuktaḥ śraddhayācaya tenaraḥ
tasyatāṃmūrtimāsthāyaprasīdāminasaṃśayaḥ
tasyāhaṃnapraṇaśyāmi sacamenapraṇaśyati
sarvāraṃbhetuyonityaṃ satataṃdhyānaka rmaṇā
samāṃpraviśatedevināstita travicāraṇā
dhattūrakaiścapuṣpaiścavilvapatraiśvaśobhanaiḥ
karavīrasahasraṃvāyāṃmedadyādviśeṣataḥ
karavīrasahasetu yatphalaṃ śṛṇu sāṃpratam
arkāṇāṃtu sahasreṇapadma me kaṃviśiṣyate
caṃpakasya mahābhāgepuṣpaṃdhattūrakaiḥ smṛtam
tathāparvasu suśroṇitasyapuṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
saṃvatsareṇa caikenapuṣpāṇāṃyatphalaṃ labhet
śobhanairdivyagaṃdhāṭyaiḥ bhṭaṇutasyāpiyatphalam
bakapuṣpapradānena aśītisvarṇajaṃ phalam
kāmenābhyarcamāna syaśṭaṇucaiva phalaṃ mahat
mamatulyonarobhūtvātriśūlīvṛṣavāhanaḥ
yastuśaṃkaranirmālyaṃpādenākramatenaraḥ
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇitiryagyoniṣujāyate
ṣaḍhana āsanādinā
yamaniyamayoḥ sādhāraṇyāditibhāvaḥ
padmārcitaiḥ praśastapāḥ
'dhattūrakaiḥ samamitiśeṣaḥ
aśītisvarṇajaṃtāvaddānajam
bhūtvācaratītiśeṣaḥ
akāmādvāakāmādapi
itiviṃśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
trayatriṃśatsahasrāṇidevadānavarākṣasāḥ
pūjayaṃtiṃtumāṃnityaṃdharmakāmārthasiddhaye
akāmātpaṭhatenityaṃyaścaivaṃśṛṇu yānnaraḥ
rudralokamavāpnotituṣṭastasya vṛṣadhvajaḥ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃpuppasa muddeśonāma viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
śrotumicchāmi bhagavanyena tuṣyatiśaṃkaraḥ
puṣpaṃcakīdṛśaṃproktaṃpuṣpamūlyaṃtu kīdṛśam
kenapuṣpeṇakiṃpuṇyaṃ parimāṇaṃprakīrtitaṃ
tepāṃca kīdṛśaṃyogamupayuktaṃ mahatphalam
yenakenaprakāreṇaā ryapūryaśvaśaṃkaraḥ
mahātmānaṃ mahādevaṃsvayaṃdevītapaḥsthi tā
vijñāpayatideveśaṃbhūtānāmādimavyayam
tvaṃnāthadevadeveśayena tuṣyasiśaṃkara
etatpraśnavaraṃbrūhiyathāṣpṛṣṭamaharṣibhiḥ
śaṃkarauvāca
puṣpāṇira ktapītāni asitānitathāpare
lomaśādaṃbhamāyecadurgaṃdhāśva sugaṃdhinaḥ
agaṃdhāvā sugaṃdhāścanānāgaṃdhāstathaivaca
teṣāṃtrasaṃkhyāṃvakṣyāmidevi ekamanāḥ śṛṇu
devānāṃśuklapuppetudurgaṃdhādānaveṣuca
karkaśā lomaśāścaivarākṣasānāṃ cchaṃṃticayemartyāḥpuṣpāṇivividhāni ca
tepāṃ kīdṛśodharmaḥ saṃmārjanopalepane
śaṃkarauvāca
śṛṇudeviyathātathyaṃ kīrtyamānamidaṃśṛṇu
śaktito'syapradānenabhaktimānīśvaredvijaḥ
daśacaiva sahasrāṇi apsarobhiścakrīḍate
karṣāśītikāvijñeyā māṣāekādaśāpyatha
etaddevipramāṇena suvarṇāśīrtibhaktimān
droṇapuṣpaṃcakuṃdaṃca kuruteśaṃkarārcanam
jātimallikapuṣpāśrvapaṃ casauvarṇikāḥ smṛtāḥ
varṣakoṭiṃśataguṇaṃ mamaloke mahīyate
tailenāpipriyodāhṛtābhāvetumānavaḥ
tena dīpapradānenaśaśivadrājatedvijaḥ
puṣpopahāra dhūpaiścaśataṃyoginamuttamam
mālāśatasahasrasyajapyaṃśataguṇaṃ smṛtam
agaruṃgaṃdhadhūpaṃca caṃdanaṃcavilepanam
ekaviṃśatsuvarṇānimayāte kīrti taṃpṛthak
kṣīreṇastrāpayelliṃgaṃghṛtābhyaṃgaṃ ca kārayet
pitṛgaṃdharvayakṣāṇāṃnāgānāṃrāsāṃtathā
sarvalokahitārthāya mayāte kīrtitaṃtathā tathānaṃ dīmahākālegaṇaiḥsahavṛṣadhvajaḥ
eṣapuṣpavidhiḥpro ktaḥ svayamīśenavaidvija
puṣpādibhiryoginaṃ sevamānaṃ śataguṇaṃ phalamāmotītyarthaḥ
ityekaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃ namaḥ śivāya dvāviṃśe'nāśaka vidhirnānāśubhaphalāvahaḥ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumāra saṃhitāyāmekaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
tī rthānāṃcaivamāsānāṃvidhānaṃparamaṃtathā
upaviṣṭāstudevādyākhyarkṣatripuraśāsanam
deva gaṃdharva sahitāmunisaṃghasamākulāḥ
praṣṭuṃcaparameśānaṃparamaṃṛṣipūjitam
pareśobhagavāniṃdrobhavānagniḥ sanātanaḥ
bhavāndharmaśvakāmaśvasaṃkalpaśvamanīṣiṇaḥ
tvaṃtuṣṭistvaṃ dhṛtirmedhā śraddhākāmomanastathā
caṃdrārkaunaprakāśeteyasmin deśegatāmama
prakāśaṃteca madbhaktāstasmindeśe sutejasā
eṣamaṃtrohi japyaśvahavyakavyemanīṣibhiḥ
māhātmyaṃtesuraśreṣṭhayaḥ paṭhenniyatonaraḥ
dhārayiṣyaṃtiyecānye śraddadhānāśvamānavāḥ
natepakilviṣaṃkiṃcittvayituṣṭebhaviṣyati
akṣayaśvāprameyaśvapurāṇapuruṣo ttam
tvaṃvāyuranalaścaivaṃtvaṃjalaṃtvaṃ mahīsmṛtaḥ
jātimallikayūthyaśvapaṃcasauvarṇikāḥsmṛtaḥ
raktotpalaṃtathā cānyesaptasauvaṇikāḥ smṛtāḥ
daśasauvaṇikājñeyābilvāśokamitismṛtāḥ
ekādaśasuvarṇānināgapuṣpaṃsa kesara
vṛkṣotpalaṃtuvijñeyaṃ suvarṇānitudvādaśa
dvātriṃśatsuvarṇāni padmapuṣpaṃtra kīrtitam
śivaāhajātītyādi
paṃcasauvarṇikāḥ suvarṇapaṃcakadānaphalakārpaṇāḥ evamapi
bhavatītiśeṣaḥ
yāniti
prābhuvaṃtītiśeṣaḥ
vyāpakaṃcirasthāyiphalamupabhogamāṃchataāyāmayataḥ āchiāyā aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇikuśapuṣpaṃ prakīrtitam

sahasrāśītivijñeyaṃbakapuṣpaṃnigadyate
śatasāhasikojñeyodhattūrakaitismṛtaḥ
etāvatpuṣpajātīnāṃgaṃdhamāghrāmyahaṃsadā
aṣṭa mīcāparānhetutathākṛṣṇacaturdaśī
etaiḥ puṣpaviśeṣaiśvakuryānnāmārcanaṃsadā
āyamārgasiṃhārūḍha māṃcchato vyāpakaṃ phalam
śaivāttaraṃtyeka manāḥ pūjayenmāṃtuyonaraḥ
kiṃvrataiḥ kiṃtapobhirvāmahāsāṃkhyaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ
ākāśenaiva pāśena badhyate brahmavādinaḥ
dhāroṣṇena tukṣīreṇa pūjayitvāmamāgrataḥ
nivedayedyathākāmaṃtasyapuṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
koṭiśatasahasrā ṇivarṣāṇāṃ tuhimālaye
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīmarcayitvā yatratatrayathātathā
sarveṣāṃcaiva puṣpāṇāṃ viśeṣeṇopalabhyate
sabaladevadāruṃvābhaktyā dhūpaṃ pradāpayet
śivārcanaṃpraśaṃsati
mahātmānopimuniyātanaiḥ munīnāmapiyātanātatsthānī
sadṛśaṃdeviliṃgānāṃtasyapuṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
dvātriṃśattu suvarṇānisārddhāśītipunaḥpunaḥ
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇimodatecama mālaye
kāladīpaṃtamodadyātsaṃva tsaraṃmamāpicaṃ
hṛdayasthaṃśivaścaiva bhaktānāṃtu sureśvaraḥ
yavohaste suraśreṣṭha sarvabhūtanamaskṛtaḥ
aṣṭaukāmā nprayacchasvaakṣayānimahāmate
tvaṃgatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃśaraṇaṃtvaṃnasaṃśayaḥ
ṛṣibhiḥ strāpayeddha maṃlabhate mahatīṃ śriyam
bhavapārśvamupāgamyaprāṃjaliḥprayatākaraiḥ
upavāsaṃparaṃdharmaspṛśaṃtimanasāsmṛtāḥ
sarveṣāmevavarṇāna kiṃphalaṃlabhate naraḥ
śrīmahādeva uvāca
śṭaṇude viyathānyāyamupavāsaphalaṃ śubham
yathācavālakhilyānāṃnaimiṣāraṇyavāsinām
upavāsaphalaṃ divyaṃ kathitaṃbhā vitātmanām
samṛddhānāṃ daridrāṇāṃ jaṃtūnāṃ duḥkhajīvinām
śṛṇuvakṣyā mitatvenamamavatrādviśeṣataḥ
upavāsaphalacaiva mokṣaṃvāpiviśeṣataḥ
sarvametadaśeṣeṇapravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ
yathāpidevisaṃproktāstathātvekamanāḥ śṛṇu
paṃcamīcaivaṣaṣṭhīcapaurṇamāsītathaivaca
upoṣyāmamabhaktena śṛṇutasyā piyatphalam
subhagodarśanīyaśvajñānabhāgībhaviṣyati
kṛṣṇāyāṃcacaturdaśyāṃ tathaiva cāṣṭamī bhavet
upoṣyāeka rātreṇabhṭaṇutasyāpi yatphalam
vasvāḍhyobahuputraśvavidyābhāgīcajāyate
śuklāṃcaturdaśīṃcaivayāvacchuklāṣṭamībhavet
upoṣyāekarātreṇaśṭaṇuta syāpiyatphalam
subhagodarśanīyaśvajñāṃnabhāgībhavennaraḥ
ruṣibhāgīdha nāṭyaścabahuputrobhavennaraḥ
dvādaśyāṃtusadāvyāsa ekabhaktena pūjayet
vidyābhāgīdhanāvyaścadhanabhāgītunirdiśet
amāvāsyāṃtrirātreṇayastu saṃvatsaraṃkṣipet
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate
māsemāsetrirātreṇaya stusaṃvatsaraṃkṣipet
apsarogaṇasaṃghṛṣṭevi mānedivirājate
yodīpodīpyamānastu kārtike cavicakṣaṇaḥ
apaścaivapivenmāsaṃnivṛttobhojanāṃtare
pauṣamāsaṃmahābhāgetasyāpitvaṃvidhiṃśṛṇu
vidhinātenapānenatarpayitvācabrāhmaṇān
śaktyātudakṣi ṇāṃdadyācchṛṇutasyāpiyatphalam
mahātmānaḥ śubhān lokānsarvadevena vaṃditāḥ
śatavarṣasahasrāṇāṃ sukhaṃ tatrava saṃtica
trirātraṃ kṣapayedyastu māghemāsetuyonaraḥ
vividhenānnapānenatarpayitvātubrāhmaṇān
śaktitodakṣiṇāṃdadyācchṛṇutasyāpiyatphalam
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇitriṃśadvarṣaśatānica
mamatejasā bhāgaśaḥ kāmacārīsakāmarūpīvalokate
sarveṣāmeva saṃmānaṃrājarājena pūjitaḥ
phālgunaṃtuyadāmāsamekabhaktenayaḥ kṣipet
śaktitodakṣiṇāṃdayācchṛṇutasyāpi yatphalam
jñānavijñānasaṃpannāvinītāśvabhavaṃtite
dharmajñāścasubhāryāśva anekakratuyājakāḥ
caitramāsaṃmahābhāgee kabhaktenayaḥkṣipet
tasminmāsesamāptetupūjayitvātumāṃpriye
vidhinānnenapānenatarpayitvātubrāhmaṇān
śaktyātudakṣiṇāṃdayācchṛṇutasyāpiyatphalam
aśītiṃtusahasrāṇiśatavarṣāṇipaṃcaya
vāruṇaṃlokamāpnotiyā nena mamatejasā
vaiśākhaṃtuyadāmāsamekabhaktenayaḥ kṣipet
tasminmāse samāptetupūjayitvātumāṃpriye
vidhinānnena pānenatarpayitvātubrāhmaṇān
śaktyātudakṣiṇāṃdayācchṛṇutasyāpiyatphalam
triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate
tataśvāpicyutobhūyogavāṃ koṭipradobhavet
jyeṣṭhamāse caikabhaktaṃmadbhaktenāṃtarātmanā
tasminmāsesamāptetupūjayitvātumāṃpriye
vidhinānne napānenatarpayitvācabrāhmaṇān

medhāvīvīryasaṃpannodhanībhavatimānavaḥ
māsemāseyadāvyāsa anukūlena kīrtitam
aṣṭavarṣasya kālasyapaṃcadhā sabhavennaraḥ
mamabhaktiratānāṃ caikāṃta ropavāsināṃ
pakṣopavāsināṃcaivatathāmāsopavāsinām

brahmacārivratānāṃca phalamūlāśināṃ tathā

yastukalyaṃcasāyaṃcabhuṃjānonāṃtaraṃ pivet
ahiṃsānirataścaiva śṛṇutasyāpiyatphalam
pauṃḍarīka syayajñasyaphalaṃ prāpnotimānavaḥ
ahiṃsānirataścaivaśṭaṇutasyāpiyatphala
avyādhitonirogaśvadī rghāyuścaiva jāyate
yastudvādaśavarṣāṇiekāhārobhavennaraḥ
ahiṃsānirataścaiva śṛṇutasyāpiyatphalam

padepadeyajñaphalaṃ labhatecā'nupūrvaśaḥ
kāṃ cīnūpuraśabde vasutaḥ saṃpratibuddhyate
mṛdaṃgaveṇuśabdena vaṃśaiśvadhruvamutthitaḥ
kalyaṃprātaḥ
vīrāsanamaraṇyacāritvādikam
