vastradānaṃca yodadyādrāhmaṇeṣuviśeṣataḥ
kapilādānaṃyodadyādrāhmaṇeṣuvi śeṣataḥ
yāvaṃtiromakūpāṇita syāgātreṣuvaidvija
kanyādānaṃ tuyodayādrāhmaṇebhyoviśeṣataḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃvivāhecavidhinādvijasattama
śayyāpradānaṃ yodayādrāhmaṇeṣuviśeṣataḥ
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate
yattudānaṃ mayāvyāsatavastre hādudīritam
upavāsasya yatpuṇyaṃsāraṃcaiva sanātanam
tītyarthaḥ
itidvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥśivāya trayoviṃśeśivaprītikārako dharmauttamaḥ
bahudharmasamāśritya ahiṃsāḥ satya vādinaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāmupa vāsavidhirnāmadvāviṃśodhyāyaḥ
tryakṣatribhuvana śreṣṭha tryaṃbakatridaśeśvara
yakṣarakṣaḥ pramathanaśūlapāṇeripuṃjaya
kovāvidhiḥkiṃvataṃcakathaṃ caiva anāśakaḥ
paricaryāniyamāyamāḥkathaṃpuṣpāṇigaṃdhāni phalānikiṃsvit
kasyatithau vātavapūjanaṃ syātprabrūhideveśvaraśūlapāṇe
śrīmahādevauvāca
caturdaśīmaṣṭamīcamadbhaktoyaḥ kṣipennaraḥ
aṣṭamyāṃ tuvarāro hegavāṃ kṣīreṇayomama
snāpayecca nirāhāraḥ prasannātmājiteṃdriyaḥ
devasyotpādanaṃ kṛtvā amunāvividhāḥ kriyāḥ
siddhamaṃtraṃsādhayetaśākamūlaphalānica
caturvidhāyāṃmṛtatu sthaṃḍilevāyaciṃtayet
jānubhyāṃjānunāvāpimahīṃ gatvāsamāśritaḥ
yathāśri topaviṣṭovāśraddhayāparayāyutaḥ
tāutatvena gṛhṇātibhaktānāṃbhaktivatsale
śraddhayāīdṛśīceṣṭābhaktisaṃbodhalakṣaṇā
khaṃḍakhādyavicitrāṇi divyānyannāniyānica
śaktihīnānyadeyānisa dyodbhūtarasāṃnica
tasyāhaṃnaivatuṣyābhivimukho'haṃvarānane
maṃtraṃ caivapravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvāyatalocane
tamahaṃpuṃḍarīkākṣaṃrudramoṃkārayāmyaham
āyāṃtudevāḥ sagaṇāumādevī maheśvarī
bhagavate mahādevāyapārśvagatāya anucarāyasvāhā
āmalakaṃsūkṣmama yaṃśivastrānaṃ punarbhajasvāhā
pradakṣiṇaṃ parāva taisarvameva umāyutesvāhā
imā āpaḥ śāṃtāḥ śatitamā aṣṭatā amṛtatamā āpaḥpūtāḥ
brahmapavitreṇapūtāḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ
āṃhāraḥsarvadavānāṃgaṃdho'yaṃ pratigṛhyatāṃ svāhā
sugaṃdhaṃsumano divyaiḥsarvagaṃdhairalaṃkṛtaṃm
pūtaṃbrahmapavitreṇapūtaṃsūryasya raśmibhiḥ
puṣpaṃdattaṃmayā bhaktyāpratigṛhṇanamostute
namaḥprajānāṃpatayenamābhaktagaṇācita
pratigṛhlaimaṃ dhūpaṃ śivaliṃga namostutesvāhā
āpojyotiśvatejaśvadevā nāṃprabhavaḥ smṛtaḥ
pūtobrahmapavitreṇapūtaḥ sūryasyaraśmibhiḥ
pratigṛhlaimaṃdīpaṃśivaliṃga namostute
nivedyamanasāyu ktaṃdevānāṃgaṃdhamuttamam
pūtotrahmapavitreṇapūtaḥ sūryasyaraśmibhiḥ
āhāraḥ sarvadevāna niveyaṃpratigṛtyatāṃ svāhā
arcitaḥ pūjitaścaivamayābhaktyāniveditāḥ
gaṃdhapuṣpopahāreṇa tatkṛpāṃ kartumarhasi
caturdaśīṃpravakṣyāmi naivedyasyavi dhiśṭaṇu
raktacaṃdanagaṃdhaiśvaharitālānulepanaiḥ
kadaṃbaiḥ kiṃśukāśokairgaṃdhapuṣpātimuktakaiḥ
patraiśvamamasānnidhyaṃphalaiḥ puṣpaistṛṇaistathā
maṃtreṇacadaheddhūpaṃ ghṛtena sahaguggulaṃ
namaḥ śrīvatsadhārāyanamojyeṣṭhabhujāyaca
namaḥ pinākadhāriṃstenamaścakragadādhara
umāpatiṃnamasyāmijaṃbūdvīpapateprabho
dvāvetaudevasaṃghātauprasīdetāmane kadhā
śṭaṇuyātkutsitovāpiyatravāmṛtasūtakam
tasyāhaṃsatataṃ prītobhaviṣyāmiyaśasvini
etatte kathitaṃ devi caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣuca
vyāsauvāca
nāmāṣṭamīkathaṃcaiva kartavyāmānuṣeṇavai
tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmitvatprasādānmahāmune
śrutaṃ pūrvaṃ mayāvyāsa rudrasyatumahātmanaḥ
devyācasaṃśayaṃpṛṣṭohimavatinagottame
yathā śrutaṃmayāvyāsa kathayāmicasuvrata
nāmāṣṭamīṃpravakṣyāmidevasyavidhimuttamam
yāṃśrutvānirmalaṃyātirudrasyacama hātmanaḥ
mārgaśīrṣetuvai māse aṣṭamyāṃ śaṃkaraṃnaraḥ
yambakaṃcasanātanetipāṭhāntaram
gomūtraprāśanaṃ kṛtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
labhatecākṣayaṃ puṇyaṃyaupoṣyati cāṣṭamīm
pauṣamāsetathāṣṭamyāṃ devadevaṃ prapūjayet
akṣayaṃlabhatepuṇyaṃyadyupo pyaticāṣṭamīm
māghamāsetathāṣṭamyāṃ maheśvaraṃ prapūjayet
kṣīraṃcapāyasaṃ caiva dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
labhatebahu śaḥpuṇyaṃyaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
phālgunecatathāṣṭamyāṃ tryaṃbakaṃcaivapūjayet
tilasyaprāśanaṃrutvādakṣiṇāmūrtimāśri taḥ
labhatebahuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
caitre māsetathā'ṣṭamyāṃ sanātanaṃtupūjayet
yavāṃścaprāśayettatradakṣiṇā mūrtimāśritaḥ
labhatebahuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
vaiśākhecatathāṣṭamyāṃ sadāśivetipūjanam
jalasya prāśanaṃkuryāddakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
labhatevaḍuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
jyeṣṭhamāsetathāṣṭamyāṃ bhagavānitipū jayet
gomayaprāśanaṃ kuryāddakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
labhatebahuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
āṣāḍhetutathāṣṭamyāṃ nīlakaṃṭhaṃ prapūjayet
śṛṃgāṭakaprāśanaṃ cadakṣiṇāmūrtireva ca
labhate bahuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
śrāva ṇetusadāvyāsa aṣṭamyāṃ sthāṇumevaca
pūjāṃca mahatīṃ kṛtvātrāśayellavaṇodakam
dakṣiṇāmūrtimāsthāyaprāśayecca vicakṣaṇaḥ
labhatebahuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
bhādrapadeyadāvyāsa aṣṭamyāṃśaṃbhumevaca
daghnaśvaprāśanaṃrutvā dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
labhate bahuśodharmayaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
aśvinetusadāvyāsa aṣṭamyāmīśvaretica
taṃdulodakamaśnīyāddakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
labhate bahuśodharmayadyupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
kārtiketuyadāvyāsaaṣṭamyāṃ rudramarcayet
dadhicaivehaprāśnīyāddakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
śṛṅgāṭakaṃphalaviśeṣaḥ
evamaṣṭamīmātra pūjanamabhidhāyanityapūjanamāha
sārūpyaṃ teṣāṃ bhavatītyāha
mahātmanāśivenasaha
ititrayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
labhatebahuśodharmaṃ yaupoṣyaticāṣṭamīm
arcayetsatataṃrudraṃprasannātmāsamā hitaḥ
gaṃdhairmālyaiśvadhūpaiśvapuṣpaiścaiva viśeṣataḥ
samāpte bhojayedviprāndadyātsauvarṇadakṣiṇām
bhakṣayeccayathāśa ktyāśivayogīviśeṣataḥ
tatomṭatyuvaśaṃprāpyaśivalokaṃsagacchati
saṃgacchaṃtiśivaṃ lokaṃsvacchaṃdogatimuttamām
divyāpsaraḥ samākīrṇakrīḍate camahātmanā
vṛṣayuktena yānena svacchaṃdolalitaḥ sadā
prārthitaṃ labhaterājyaṃprajñāyuktobahuśrutaḥ
śṛṇumānītudharmajñomithyādaṃbhavivarjitaḥ
pūjāṃcasmaratenityaṃdevaṃ pūjayate punaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃnāmāṣṭamīvidhikathanaṃnāmatrayoviṃśodhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
kunnāśva rogiṇoraudrājāyaṃte yena mānavāḥ
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃ pannāḥ saubhāgyāśivadarśanāḥ
kenavākarmaṇādeva jāyate 'pūrvalakṣaṇāḥ
brūhi tattvena kathaya pramāṇalakṣaṇāṣṭamīm
śrutaṃ pūrvaṃ mayāvyāsayaddevyai proktavānharaḥ
śṛṇu devi paraṃ divyamupavāsaṃparaṃmama
lakṣaṇāṣṭamīṃpravakṣyāmitacchṛṇutvaṃtrilocane
kārtikasyatathāṣṭamyāmupoṣyamamabhaktimān
ahorātroṣitobhūtvā śiveticaprapūjayet
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktojāyate mānavottamaḥ
nai vaṃbuddhyāmiśūlāṃkanikhilaṃtadravīhi me
nāmanāmatathāṣṭamyāṃvistareṇabravīhime
vistaraṃteprava kṣyāmiśṭaṇudevinagātmaje
nāthaṃśirasi vaidevipādeśaṃkaramevaca
jaṃghe'tirudramedeviīśānaṃkaṭirucyate
tryaṃbakaṃcatatodevikaparyaṣṭāṃgamevaca
śūlapāṇistuvakṣogaḥskaṃdhetuvṛṣabhadhvajam
umāpatiśvamedevināsāpaśupatistathā
purahākarṇayorde vitripu raghnaśvacakṣuṣī
śmaśānavāsīśbhūmadhye bhūteśetikapolayoḥ
dakṣayajñavināśītudaṃtasevanamevaca
jaṭilaṃjivhayā deviśiraḥpaśupatītica
śaśāṃkāṃketicamūrdhnilalāṭetu umāpriyaḥ
gaṃgādharetikeśeṣusarvāṃgeśivamevaca
ahanyahaniyobhaktyāupoṣyavidhināṣṭamīṃ
arcayenmāṃtatorudraprayatātmāsamāhitaḥ
gaṃdhadīpaiśvamālyaiśva dhūpaiścaiva viśeṣataḥ
dadyāttāmraghaṭānpūrṇānbrāhmaṇāyaviśeṣataḥ
dakṣiṇāṃcayathā śaktyāsuvarṇānāṃyathāmati
mṛnmayaṃ bhājanaṃ pūrṇatai lenacaviśeṣataḥ
tataḥ kālakṣayaṃprāpyajāyatecapu naḥkramāt
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannojāyatemānavottamaḥ
nakaścilakṣaṇairhīno bhavatepuruṣottamaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃnāmalakṣaṇāṣṭamīkathanaṃnāmacaturviṃśodhyāyaḥ
kathayiṣyāmyahaṃ dharmaṃyathāvadanupūrva śaḥ
annadānātparaṃdānaṃnaiva kiṃcidviśiṣyate
annādbhavaṃtibhūtānitasmāttadadhikaṃ smṛtam
mayūra haṃsa saṃyuktaṃ sarvakāmasamṛddhimat
vimānaṃsūryasaṃkāśamannadolabhate śubham
yadimānu ṣyamāyātikadācitpuruṣottamaḥ
dhanadhānyasamākīrṇe kuleyātisurūpavān
yathāśaktyātuyodayādviprāyānnaṃvaro naraḥ
kadācidapiyodadyādannaṃviprāyasaṃskṛtam
tasyaśataguṇaṃpu ṇyaṃ sahasraguṇa mevaca
avaghātamavajñātamasaṃskṛtamathāpivā
annaṃpradayā grodeviyādṛśaṃtādṛśaṃśubhe
tasyāpinara keghorepātyamānasyarākṣasaiḥ
ya dimānuṣyamāyātikadācitsanaraḥpunaḥ
annamevaviśiṣṭaṃhitasmātparataraṃnahi
annaṃprajāpatiḥ proktaṃ sacasaṃvatsaraḥpunaḥ
tasmādbhavaṃtibhūtānisthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
tasmādannaṃviśiṣṭaṃvaisarvebhyaitiviśrutiḥ
annadānātparaṃdānaṃnaivakiṃ cidviśiṣyate
annādbhavaṃti bhūtānitasmāttadvaiviśiṣyate
sugaṃdhāḥ śītalāścāporasairdivyaiḥ samanvitāḥ
vimānaṃsūryasaṃkāśamapsarogaṇanāditam
tatrāsāvayutānyaṣṭauuṣitvādevavatsukhī
kulemahatisaṃkīrṇejāyatedhanadhānyavān
tayānnapūrṇayobhāṃ ḍaṃbrāhmaṇāyaprayacchati
rasāstasyopatiṣṭaṃtipūjyatecadivaṃgataḥ
bhājanānicayodadyādannapūrṇa śubhānane
bho janasyārthabhogānāṃtārayeccapitṛnbhayāt
taḍāgaṃyastu kurvītavāpikāṃcasamṛddhimān
tārayitvāca sa pitṝṃstathaiva ca pitāmahān
prapitāmahalokeṣu kāmageṣuvihaṃgamaḥ
bhogībhavatibhogyānāṃrājāmātyaśvajāyate
dātāya jvācabalavānsubhagaḥpriyadarśanaḥ
avaṭayonaraḥkuryādapapūrṇa śucismite
dadyācca brāhmaṇebhyastubhojayitvāyathā rthavataṣṭabhiḥsuvicitrābhiḥpatākābhiralaṃkṛtam
hiraṇyaṃhemabhūmiṃcatilānratnānivāpiyaḥ
dāne phalamāha
bhājanānīti
sapitṝn bhojanasyārthabhogānāṃcabhayāttārayeditiyojanā
tatpitṝṇāṃ bhojanādyalābhajaṃbhayaṃnabhavatītyarthaḥ
pradadyātsarvabhūtebhyastasyapuṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
tatayutaśvadharmātmāsarvakāmasamṛddhimān
yastuvṛkṣaṃcakurute chāyāpuṣpaphalānvitam
ya tphalaṃsamavāpnotitacchṛṇuṣvamahāmate
yāvadṛkṣasyapatrāṇiupayuṃjatidehinaḥ
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇitārayitvāpitṝnapi
somalokaṃsamāsāṃya samṛddhaṃ phalamāpnuyāt
phalānāṃ satubhāgīsyādrūpavānsubhagavaha
so' psaraḥśatasaṃkīrṇe vimāne divimodate
tāmrayo bhājanaṃdadyādrāhmaṇebhyoviśeṣataḥ
salokaṃbrahmaṇaḥ prāpyasarvakāmaiśvasaṃvṛtaḥ
varṣakoṭiśataṃcaivatatpraśastena karmaṇā
gṛhamedhī sadādātābhogavāṃścaiva jāyate
oṣadhīryaḥ prayacchetabāhmaṇāyamahātmane
bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi carate kāmarūpavān
hemnācitraṃbhūṣitaṃsulakṣaṇaṃcetyarthaḥ
rathamaśvaṃgajamitipāṭhāntaram yadimānuṣyamāyātisanaraḥkālaparyayāt
paśuṃyastuprayacchetabrāhmaṇāyasa māhitaḥ
annaṃyastu prayaccheta saṃskṛtaṃ brāhmaṇāyaca
yastuśayyāṃ prayacchetatrāhmaṇāya svalaṃkṛtāṃ
sagatvāpitṛlākevaivarṣāyutaśataṃvasat
bhāryāprāpnotibhadrāṃgīṃprajāvāśvopajāyate
rathamaśvayujaṃdāsīṃkanyāṃgṛhamathāpivā
jaladhenuṃ cayodadyāttasyadānaphalaṃ śṛṇu
prapāṃgavāṃtaḍāgaṃvākūpaṃ tasya supuṣkalam
rutvākuṃbhāṃścasaṃpūrṇānmālyaiśvasamalaṃkṛtā
bhakṣyabhojyaiḥ susaṃvṛtāntalapātrāṇidāpayet
dakṣiṇāṃ puṣkalāṃ dayāttebhyastāndarśayedbudhaḥ
āpaḥśivāśvasaumyāśvatarpayaṃtipitṛnyathā
kāmadāḥ kāmadātārobhavaṃticapadepade
evaṃ datvā cagāṃdhenuṃ puraskṛtya cavaitadā
tilapātrāṇiyodayātta thāvastrayugaṃnaraḥ
vṛtaṃgā vaḥprasūyateghṛtaṃ bhūmyāṃ pratiṣṭhitam
ghṛtamagniśvadevāśvaghṛtaṃmesaṃpradīyatām
brāhmaṇāṃstarpayitvātugaṃdhamālyairalaṃka tān
dānakāle tatastasyāṃ surāgātrāṇisaṃśritāḥ
brahmātasyāḥśrito mūrdhniśako bhālaṃsamāśritaḥ
caṃdrādityaune deśe prāṇevāyuḥprabhaṃjanaḥ
mukhaṃtasyāśritovanhirjivhāṃsomaḥ svayaṃbhavaḥ
karṇayoścāśvinaudevauśirorudrāḥ samāśritāḥ
pādayorlokapālāśvasarvaicaivatupannagāḥ
samudrāḥ samajaṭhare grīvāyāṃtapanāḥśritāḥ
stane gaṃgāsaricchreṣṭhāpārśvatuvasa vastathā
upasthaṃcagudaṃtīrthāḥ prajāpatisamāśritaḥ
purīṣaṃśrīrbabhūvāsyānāgāḥśvāsānilāśritāḥ
sādhyā viśve'thalokāśvapucchameva tusaṃsthitāḥ
maṃtrāyajñāśvadānāniyamaśvaṛṣibhiḥ saha
nakṣatrāṇigrahāścaivatārārūpā ṇiyānica
gāyatrīcaiva viṣṇuśvajagatīpaṃktireva ca
anuṣṭup caiva yajñaśvasāmānyātharvaṇastathā lokasya mātaraścai vameghavarṣamathāpivā
dharmonārāyaṇaścaiva bhūtānisaritastathā
romakūpāṇisaṃśrityatasyadivyāṃvyavasthitāḥ
yakṣāśvarākṣasāścaivapiśācāścaiva pakṣiṇaḥ
yajñastathādakṣiṇāśvatathā apsarasaḥ śubhāḥ
gaṃdharvāśca mahātmānoyecā 'nyepyevamādayaḥ
tasyāviṣāṇayorvyāsa sarva eva samāśritāḥ
phalānisarvadānānāṃpatayaśvapṛthagvidhāḥ
kuśāḥ suvarṇabījānitilāḥ siddhārthakāsta thā
sarvadevamayīṃ dogdhrīṃ sarva lokamayītathā
prayacchāmimahāmūrtimakṣayāṃme śubhāmiti
evaṃ sadatvātāṃgāṃtuyatrayatraprajāyate
tatratatragatā sātaṃtārayettubhayāttathā
sarvānkāmānsaṃṭaṇotigoṃdānena yathāmaraḥ
ihajātaścatāmeva kāmagāṃpratipadyate
yāitiśeṣovā
pṛthivīphalaṃtaddānaphalam
āvāsaṃnivāsasthānam
puṇḍarīkaṃpauṇḍarīkayāgaphalam
uddharecciki manasāmānuṣobhūtvāgosahasrīmahābalaḥ
rūpavānbalavāṃścaiva bahuputraśvajāyate
prasūyamānāṃyogāṃtudadyādubhaya tomukhīṃ
hemaśṛṃgīraupyakhurīṃsajātismaratāṃlabhet
ruṣṇājinaṃtuyodadyādvatinebrahmacāriṇe
prāpnuyātpuṃḍarīkaṃtugosa hasaṃtuviṃdati
sasmṛtiṃcaparāṃlabdhvāyogamāpnotisuvrate
kamaṃḍalaṃca yodadyādrāhmaṇāyanarottamaḥ
vyādhitaṃyastuviprarṣedīnaṃmūḍhamacetanaṃ
daśānāmaśvamedhānāṃphalaṃprāpnoti mānavaḥ
yaścaivaitāniramyāṇidānā nyuktānikṛtsraśaḥ
sarvāṇiyugapaccaiva pṛthivyāmekarāṅgavet
idaṃyaḥśṛṇuyānnityaṃdadyāccaivasvaśaktitaḥ
paśyati camahābhāgaḥ sopigacchetriviṣṭapam
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃdānadharmavidhinirūpaṇanāmapaṃ caviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
īśvarauvāca
deviśṛṇuṣvabhūyopiyathādānaṃvināśubham
satena karmaṇādevimāṃbhajanniva nityaśaḥ
māghamāsetu kurvāṇaḥ śriyamāpnotivaipriye
itipañjaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥśivāya ṣaḍiśeniḥsvadayayāvinādāne mahāphalam
pūrvatramārgaśīrṣopavāsaphalābhidhāne bhajannivetīvapadadyātyaṃphalaṃsphorayati
śakralokatāṃśakasālokyaṃ
ekaeka ekabhaktaṃtukurvāṇaḥ phālgunemāsinityaśaḥ
strīṣusaubhāgyamāpnotistriyaśvaparamaśriyaṃ
vaiśākhaṃyaḥkṣipenmāsamekabhaktena mānavaḥ
jñātisaṃśreṣṭhatāṃtrā pyapūjitodhanavānapi
jyeṣṭhamāsaṃkṣipedyovai ekabhaktaṃsamācaran
jyeṣṭhobhavatiśbhrātṝṇāṃbhogānāpnotipuṣkalān
āṣāḍhavāpiyomāsamekabhaktaṃsamācaret
sarājñomānyatāṃprāpya kāmānāpnotipuṣkalān
śrāvaṇedeviyomāse eka bhaktaṃsamācaret
saināpatyaṃcasaṃprāpyabalavānapijāyate
yāpicāśvayujaṃmāsamekabhaktenatiṣṭhati
vāṇijyaṃ labhatetasya kṛṣiḥ paśugaṇāstathā
kārtikaṃ vāpiyomāsamekabhaktenatiṣṭhati
yaḥ kṣipedekabhaktena mārgaśīrṣa nasaṃśayaḥ
saṃvatsaraṃtuyaḥ pūrṇamekabhaktena tiṣṭhati
sapārthivasamobhū tvāmahīṃpātimaheṃdravat
daśānāṃsasuvarṇānāṃ phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ
māsemāse ahorātraṃ sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ
māsemāsecayaḥkuryātrirātraṃ kṣepaye nnaraḥ
yobhuṃ ktedivaseṣaṣṭhenityaṃniyamamāsthitaḥ
vāruṇaṃlokamāsādyasacaviṃdenmahāpadaṃ
aṣṭame'haniyo bhuṃktepratimāsamataṃdritaḥ
vāruṇaṃlokamāsthāyasacaviṃdenmahatphalam
agnibhyāṃcasa mobhūtvā sūryavajvalate sadā
mānuṣyaṃcapunaḥprāpyadaśabhāryālabhetasaḥ ekādaśetuyorbhuktedivase mānavaḥ śuciḥ
ekādaśyāḥ phalaṃprāpyayajñavānihajāyate
athehamānuṣobhūtvāsana rojāyateśuciḥ
iharājāmahānbhūmauyatratatrābhijāyate
pūjyamānoyathādevaḥ stūyamāno'tha sarvaśaḥ
jvalanādi tyasaṃkāśaḥsanityaṃmukhamaśnute
tataḥ padmāsanaṃprāpyadaśabhāryālabhetasaḥ
athavāpunarāvṛttirbrāhmaṇobhavatīśvaraḥ
snātaścaśucirathavāhutvānīṃśvasamāhitaḥ
dīkṣayitvātathātmānamupavāsaṃcareddijaḥ
taṃyāṃtiśaraṇaṃcaiva durgaṃ pālognirevaca
yojapandevagāyatrīṃpavitrāṇicanityaśaḥ
rudranāmaguṇānvāpirātraucasthaṃḍileśayaḥ
kuśānāstīryavidhivatstrī śūdraparivarjitaḥ
samaśnīyāttuvairātrauvītarāgovimatsaraḥ
yāvatyahānisaṃtiṣṭhettāvadviprāṃstubhojayet
tataḥ pūrṇe tukālevaibrāhmaṇānāṃśataṃgavām
sahasramathavāśaktyāpūjayitvātu sarvaśaḥ
haviṣyaṃ bhojanaṃdadyādgāvovāsāṃsicakra māt
vṛṣabhaṃ yastu nīlāṃgaṃgāṃ dadyāccapayasvinīm
yāvadromasahasrāṇivarṣāṇadivimodate
tilapātrāṇiyodadyādviprebhyaḥ śraddhayānaraḥ
amāvā syāṃsamāsāgrakṛṣṇāṣṭamīsamāhitaḥ
yastu cāṃdrāyaṇaṃ kuryādyathoktaṃmusamāhitaḥ
sapitṝṃstarpayitvātu akṣayaṃnarapuṃga vaḥ
pavitrāṇāṃvidhiṃbhū yaekacittā'vadhāya
mahāsāṃta panaṃyastukarotisumahāmanāḥ
tulāpuruṣa kaṃyaśvātidvijasattame
rucchrātikṛcchreṇa tathāgāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
yaśrvasarvāṇidānānikurutenarasattamaḥ
yaṃyaṃprārthayate kāmaṃtaṃtamevasamaśnute
yāva kaṃcopayuñjānogomūtre ṇāpisaṃskṛtam
piṇyākamātrabhakṣovāvāyubhakṣoyavāpunaḥ
yā vaduktaṃsamāsena mahātmānaṣṭakilviṣaḥ
sālokyaṃvāmahāśabdaṃ yatheṣṭaṃmokṣamevaca
aiśvaryaṃca mahatprāpyadīpyamāno' vatiṣṭhati
varaṃprāpyacasarvāṇidānānicayathepsitam
vināmaṃtreṇa satataṃ śūdrāṇāmihasarvaśaḥ
amaṃtrāstesṣṭatāḥsarveśūdrāvigatakalmaṣāḥ
strīṇāṃcadaivataṃ bharttātatonā'nyovidhīyate
sāgatiḥparamodharmaḥsadhāmparamaṃsmṛtam
tenasāabhyanujñātāidaṃdharmasamācaret
yātutenānanujñātādharmaṃ kuryācchucismitā
yācabha tra'bhyanujñātākṛtvādhamai supuṣkalaṃ
dadyācca paṭhate nārītasyānaṃtaṃhi tatphalam
vaśyaśvāsyābhavedbhartāpriyātasyacasātathā
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇeṣaviśo'dhyāyaḥ
lokakartāramīśānaṃ sarvajñamaparājitam
praṇamāmitrinayanaṃ bhavaṃtaṃśūlapāṇinam
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃca yaccavedyaṃ paraṃhara
yatpṛcchāmimahāde vatanme brūhi yayātathā
yāṃścavainiyamāṃścakurbrāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāviśaḥ
yecānyeniyamāḥ kecitteṣāṃ vai brūhiyatphalam
yeputīrthapusarveṣāṃ samṛddhāḥ phalavṛddhayaḥ
dṛśyateniyamānāṃca yogadhyānatapolayāḥ
eṣa me saṃśayodevacittavyākulakā rakaḥ
śamayasva mahābuddhenīhāramiva bhāskaraḥ
śrīmaheśvarauvāca
niyamaṃtunaraḥ kṛtvāniyamānniyatendriyaḥ
duṣkaraṃniyamaṃ kartumanuṣyeṇaviśeṣataḥ
narālobhābhibhūtāścanarādha mahiṃsakāḥ
devatvadevatāḥ prāptāniyamānniyamānvite
niṣkalmapātapaḥ kṛtvāniya maṃcayathātathā
mamapatnītvamāyāsitvaṃśubhenātra saṃśayaḥ
varṣeca niyamaṃyaśca kuruteniyamāṃstataḥ
dvijātīnāṃpriyaṃ tanmeniśāmayanagātmaje
vārāṇasyāmabhūdvipraḥ kevalaṃnāmadhārakaḥ
vikṛtaḥ karmamūḍhaścaparadravyāpahārakaḥ
niṣṭhurokaruṇodevijātikarmavighaṭṭakaḥ
sūcako tyāṃdhrajaḥpāpo'viśuddhobhātimatsaraḥ
mithyāvinītodurmedhādevadānavadhikkṛtaḥ
paradravyeṇa saṃtuṣṭaḥ paradravyāvicārakaḥ
uddejanīyaḥ sarvasyaduṣṭāhirivapārvati
mithyāvinīto durmedhāvedavādavahiṣkṛtaḥ
cchinnadaṃṣṭroyathāsarpaḥśṛṃgahīnoyathāvṛṣaḥ
nunnapakṣoyathāpakṣīvipuṣpaiva pādapaḥ vārāṇasyāṃ sarvaiviproviprakoṭiśatārdanaḥ
āste smaśatapatrākṣisolasavā rthahārakaḥ
tasyāṃpuryāna sostīhapuruṣaḥ pramadottame
yasyeṣṭaḥ sa bhavedbhīrurduṣṭāhirivaduḥkhadaḥ
vaṇigāpaṇagaḥsothaniya taṃrucirānane
tasyavarṣaśatānyeva vaṇigāpaṇagasya vai
atikrāṃtāniviprasyanavāśiṣṭasya pārvati
athāṃbu japadaḥsiddhaḥsiddhagaṃdharvapūjitaḥ
vārāṇasīṃgatodraṣṭumoṃkāraṃ siddhavaṃditam
vratamāsthāya kāśyāṃtumunisiddhaistusa tkṛtaḥ
ārtabhūtāḥ kalāvāsa ntsarve taṃpraṇamaṃtica
pradakṣiṇaṃprakurvatijanmapāpakṣayāvaham
rudrāvāsetupānīyaṃpibaṃtiviharaṃtica
vārā ṇasyāṃviśālākṣiśśramaṃtetridivālayāḥ
satatraśśramamāṇaśvasiddhovikṛtarūpadhṛk
sataṃvikṛtamāyāṃtaṃsiddharūpaṃ svamāgatam
bujapadanāmā
paṃcāyatanasaṃsthitaṃoṃkāreśvaraṃ
gṛhṇāt agṛhṇāt
apūrvadarśanaṃtvāṃtuṣpṛcchāmyahamayobhavān
kutaḥ kathaṃtuprāptosiśaṃkesva gatsamāgataḥ
nahīdṛśena rūpeṇa katinacatureṇatu
dṛśyatenyaṃstataḥ śaṃkesvargabhraṣṭobhavāniti
sādhu bhoḥsvargavijñātamahājñānamayotyasi
svargādahamanuprātaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃnasaṃśayaḥ
brāhmaṇauvāca
raṃbhāmapsarasāṃ śreṣṭhāṃya dijānāsikathyatām
abhijñāṃsvargasaṃsthānāmapsarāṇāṃnasaṃśayaḥ
bā hmaṇauvāca
kohisvargāliyāṃraṃbhāṃnavidecceṃ dusannibhām
pariyāsipunaḥ svargakadācidrāhmaṇarṣabha
raṃbhāmanāmayaṃ pṛcchavacanānmamasattama
apakrāmandivaṃ kāṃtāṃvāyuravyāhatoyathā
satugṛhṇādviniṣkrāṃtāṃ caṃdralekhāṃyayāṃbarāt
apaśyatsukatīraṃ bhāṃbhbhraṣṭapadmāmivaśriyam
pūrṇacaṃdrābhavadanāṃmadanāṃgamayīmiva
gajakuṃbhaniśābhyāṃcastanābhyāṃtūpaśobhitām
pīnavistīrṇajaghanavakṣorumukhanāsikām
phullatāmrāraviṃdābhyapādābhyāṃ saṃpratiṣṭhitām
raṃbhāṃvīṇā nvitāṃteṣāṃ surāṇāṃ svāṃtacāriṇīm
siddhodṛṣṭvānavadyāṃgīmidaṃ vacanamabravīt
vārāṇasyāṃnivasati brāhmaṇohiva rāṃgane
satvāṃ pṛcchatisuśroṇiyadijānāsikathyatām
raṃbhovāca
svamevāvasayaṃtūrṇamābhiveśānnalocane
vārāṇasīmanuprāptaḥpaṃcāyatanamāsthitaḥ
dvijātinācasaṃpṛṣṭaśvireṇapunarāgataḥ
sataṃprahasya provācavārāṇasyāṃniketanaḥ
kathaṃ brāhmaṇadṛṣṭāsātvayāraṃbhāvarāpsarāḥ
kānisāvadatedṛṣṭāpṛcchatevāsurāṃganā
raṃbhādṛṣṭātatastubhyaṃ prahasyavacanānmama
vyaśālinī
athasaeva siddhaḥ svargātpunaḥ kāśyāṃsamāgataste
ciraṃviciṃtyamāmāhanaivajānāmi kopyasau
brāhmaṇauvāca
brāhmaṇo'smipunaḥ svargaṃ yadānāma mahādyute
svarge sukṛtināṃvāse saṃgatoraṃbhayāca saḥ
sāraṃbhāpṛthu suśroṇistanabhārānatāmudā
apaśyatpaśyatāṃ cittaṃharaṃtīmivasubhruvam
satapadmarāgavarṇāmu nnatastanaśālinīm
uvācasiddhaḥ prahasanbhāṃbhāvapracaṃcalāṃ
vārāṇasyāṃ punaścāhaṃnādviyetupunaḥkatham
smitaṃvihasitaṃ kṛtvātataḥsarvāpsarovarā
raṃbhāsiddhaṃsahakhāṇāmuvācāmaṃ tryakāraṇam
siddhataṃbrāhmaṇaṃbūhiyadijñātuṃ kilecchasi
niyamaṃkuruvijñānaṃtataḥ svargebhaviṣyasi
ityuktvāsiddha māmaṃtryanamaskṛtvātusāpsarāḥ
naṃdanaṃvanamāgatya saṃgatātatracāpsarāḥ
rudrāvāsamanuprāpyataṃtrāhmaṇamapaśyata
athainaṃbrāhmaṇaṃ prāhasmaritvāsukhasaṃpadaḥ
yadīcchasiparijñā tumātmānaṃ kilaraṃbhayā
devaiścaniyamaṃ jñātvāniyamaṃ kurvasaṃśayam
brāhmaṇauvāca
adyaprabhṛtipāṣāṇaṃ nakhādāmi dvijottama
pāṣāṇaṃkhādatinayaḥ satvāṃ pṛcchatibrāhmaṇaḥ
divameva gatastūrṇa vāyuravyāhṛtoyathā
saraṃbhāmatravīddevi satvāṃ pṛcchatibrāhmaṇaḥ
raṃbhetaṃvai vijānīhipāṣāṇaṃyonakhādati
tameva divasaṃraṃbhātāṃ purīmasya citayat
prakāśājajñiredevi pradīpenayathāniśi
sayasyanāyātigṛhaṃyasyavāyātivaigṛhāt
kathaṃjīvā mikovāhamititasyā'bhavanmatiḥ
smaritvāsmṛtvā
khādāmikhādiṣyāmi
ayaṃtraṇā akleśāḥ
itisaptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya aṣṭāviṃśe caṃdrakhaṇḍadhāraṇe tanotyupāsitaḥ svarganayatenaramaṃbike
niyamādbrahmalokaṃ vāprāpyatenāpipārvati
prāpnuvaṃtinarāḥ śubhraṃrutvāciramayaṃ traṇāḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃniyamanirūṇaṃnāmasaptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
niyamasya phalaṃ coktaṃśrutvāprītābhavatsatī
bharttāraṃlokakartāraṃ punarapyāhapā vatī
dhāryatecaṃdrava rṇābhicaṃdrasyārdhatvayākatham
kāraṇaṃcaivakathayayenatvaṃ caṃdraśekhara
umāmāhapariṣvajyaśṭaṇudeviśubhānane
mahādevauvāca
nirvedaṃ paramaṃ gatvā mokṣa senāṃtarātmanā
guhāsuramaṇīyā sunadīnāṃ pulineṣuca
vṛkṣavāsipuvṛkṣeṣudevodyānavaneṣuca
ahamiṃdīvarābhyāśevasāmivicarāmi ca
niyamaṃtī vramāsthāya ghanapīnonnatastanī
śṛṃgāṇidharaṇīdhārādatyaṃte mamatejasā
tiṣṭhāmi atiṣṭham
dharaṇīdhārāḥ parvatāḥ
niṣprabhaṃgrahacaṃdrārkaṃjarārditamivāṃtakam
tatodevagaṇāḥ sarve saśakāḥsapi tāmahāḥ
samīyurmaṃdarasyāgremamatejaḥ pariṣṭute
athabrahmāṇamāmaṃtrya maheṃdrodevatādhipaḥ
narudrasyagatiṃjñātuṃprabhavāmimahātmanaḥ
navayaṃtra mukhādāsyanacavāryāsyaniśvayaḥ
avaśyaṃcamayātubhyaṃhitaṃ kāryaṃjagaddhitam
sahijāyāvirahitodivādīptaivānalaḥ
vahiṣyatīdaṃśirasāsaumyaprītaṃnasaṃśayaḥ
tejobhibhavitāsaumyaṃcaṃdracūḍāśritomaṇiḥ
evaṃnaḥ sukṛtaṃ kāryaṃsacaprītobhaviṣyati
prabhāvācchaśinaśvāpisaśītaśva bhaviṣyati
gṛhītaṃdaivataiḥseṃdraiḥrmaṇivarṇaśubhaṃsthitaṃ
tenasabrahmakāḥ seṃdrādevādaivatavaṃdite
tato'mṛtasamāpūrṇamekamekaṃviṣasyaca
kuṃbhātkuṃbhādupādāyadevāste samupasthitāḥ
amuṃcetāṃśubhaṃgaṃdhaṃcaṃdanāvivapuṣpitau
tatodevāḥ samarutaḥprasanneṃdriyamānasāḥ
deveti pūrvamāmaṃtrya prāhadevaṃ pitāmahaḥ
devāmṛtamidaṃ cāpikuṃbhaṃhālāhalābhidhaṃ
tatogrātyaṃgṛhāṇatvaṃtataḥ paśyaṃtudeva tāḥ
tato mayā smṛtaṃdevīprathamaṃpramathācite
punaśrcaṃdraṃśirobhāge lekhāmātrovinirmitaḥ
spṛśyagrīvāsamālabdhāpradeśinyāmayānaghe
ammṛtenaiva caṃdraścakaṃṭhaścaivaviṣeṇame
ṭī
tītiśeṣaḥ
adhomukhoviṣayāṃtarānāsaṃgāt
dadyāt śivaitiśeṣaḥ
ityaṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya una yugapajjanitaumūrdhnilalāṭedehajāviva
tatte jomṭatatāṃnītaṃ mahīrajaivāṃnu nā
tenahālāhalenāpiviṣeṇamamapārvati
kaṃṭhomamakṛtaḥśyāmoyasyamevāmalocane
tataḥśivaśvasaumyaśvadevā nāmasmi suṃdari
darśanīyaśvasaṃvattovṛttapīnakucodari
ityevaṃ te mayāproktaṃyathā caṃdraḥ śirogataḥ
yaidaṃ śṛṇu yāddevicaṃdrārdhotpattisaṃbhavaṃ
kalikalupaṃnihantiyaścedaṃ puṇyaphaladaṃ sarvakālaṃ pitṝṇāṃ sukhaprāpakam
tiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāmaṣṭāviṃśodhyāyaḥ
viṣadoṣapha laṃśrutvāgirīśatanayā'vyayā
āśāvasanadeveśanāstidhanyatarāmayā
vibhūtyāparayāyuktaṃ bhūtyāca suvibhūṣitam
paśyāmitvāṃśmaśānasthaṃ nṛtyaṃtaṃpramathaiḥ saha
gośīrṣakana kaśyāmairanyaiśvava racaṃdanaiḥ
kutaeṣākathaṃ caiṣāvallabhatvamupāgatā
bhūtirbhūtividāṃ śreṣṭhavadabā leṃdubhūṣaṇa
evamuktaḥprabhurdevaḥ somayāsomabhūṣaṇaḥ
uvācasaṃpariṣvajya gaurīṃdīmābhisaṃnibhām
caṃdrābhe caṃdravada necaṃdrapaṃkajahāsini
śṛṇudeviyathābhūtirvilepanamabhūnmama
brahmaṇobrāhmaṇotyāsīdbhṛguvaṃśeprabhāvataḥ
niyamaṃtīva māsyāyatanāpavipulaṃtapaḥ
grīṣmepaṃcatapābhūtyā hemaṃte ca jaleśayaḥ
varṣāsvākāśagaśvāpi so'bhavañcabubhukṣitaḥ
kālekāle mitālāpe'pūrṇamāhāramāharat
tamṛkṣāḥśarabhāḥ siṃhāḥ śṛgālādyāśvajatavaḥ
yecasasyaṃ kuśāhārāyecamāṃ sāśinomṭagāḥ
tete prabhāvāttasyāthanirvairāḥ sahacāriṇaḥ
sacāpitapasāddvīnodīptāgnisadṛśaprabhaḥ
tatāpalokāntra hmarṣistāpayantsayathāpurī
śākamakṣāralavaṇaṃta syāhāra mataḥpriyaṃ
nāmnāparṇādaityeva tatolokeṣuviśrutaḥ
eka parṇāśinastasya yathāpūrṇāśinastathā
bahūnyahāniyātānivarṣāṇyamṛtavarṣiṇi
tasya dharmaraterāsīnmānasaṃsaṃpratiṣṭhi taṃ
yadāśākarasābhāsaṃbhaveddhirudhiraṃmama
nunnavānpadmagarbhābhedarbhānvaiḍūryasaṃnibhān
asitīkṣṇena darbheṇa pāṭitātha pradeśinī
tato'gulīvra ṇāttasyaśākaniryāsasannibhaṃ
susrāvaśoṇitaṃ tāvadrasaṃdṛṣṭvā prahasyaca
sahasannṛtyamānaśva nardamānaśvabrāhmaṇaḥ
trāsayāmāsa sahasāmṭagāṃstānanugā napi
tasyāpūrvavi kāraṃtudṛṣṭvā sarvamṭagāṃbike
trastābhūtvāsamutsṛṣṭāmṭagāḥ siṃhārditāiva
mayātmāviprarūpeṇa tasya viprasya darśitaḥ
sanṛtyanninadaṃśvāpinacamāmapyabhāṣata
yadātasyānuvṛccyāca virarāmatapodhanaḥ
tapodhanaṃ mahaddhitvāpraśaṃsāma śramaṃlabhet
tapoyajñaśvakīrtiśvamāhiṃsīśvirasaṃcitāṃ
anaṃtarātmāpṛthivīmātebhūdvismayomune
niṣkalmaṣaṃśarīraṃmetapasāpa śyabrāhmaṇa
ahaṃtavānupaśyāmi kilbiṣastvaṃsa kilviṣam
śarīraṃsravate bhasmadatyamānaṃḍhaṇaṃyathā
tataḥ pradeśinīde vīmayā suṃdara suṃdari
kṣīradhārāḥ pataṃtyasmādaṃgulyāṃtādṛśīsitā
bhūtidhārāpramukhāvavasudhārāivādhvare
mamāṃgulivraṇāttasmādbhasmadhārāṃsamīkṣyasaḥ
anaṃtavarṣāpṛthivīyaduktaṃ tadidaṃtathā
svayaṃśākarasodbhūtaṃ bhūtyāpraśamitaṃhi me
kobhavānkiṃca tegotranāmakiṃkiṃcatetapaḥ
nūnaṃ varṣasahasrāṇibahūni mamabrāhmaṇa
mahādeva prasādācca kurvataḥ paramaṃtapaḥ
meghaśyāmācyutovāpibhavānmegharathoharaḥ
darśitaṃ darśanīyākṣirūparūpa sahasrade
tataḥsuvalitairgācaiḥ saṃbhramāccalitekṣaṇe
samepanyāṃpapātāśutuṣṭāvaca samapriye
parṇādauvāca
namotrāhmaṇarūpāyamahādevāyaline
bateṃdra viṣṇupūjyāyaśaṃkarāyanamostute
namobhasmāṃgarāgāyabhasmotpattivikāriṇe
bhasmaliptāṃgadehāyaduḥkhāṃtaphaladāyine
taṃbhāvaśuddhabhāvaṃtaṃbhāvaśuddhena cetasā
amarāśvaramā yuktāḥsarvaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ
mamādyavaiyathāceṣṭaṃmameṣṭosigaṇādhipaḥ
goṣuvipreṣubhakteṣudeveṣvastu catedayāṃ
yogātpramuditobhūtvāmāṃpraṇamyagaṇeśvara
mayaivadattamāvāsaṃ sumerausuṃrasaṃni bham etasmātkāraṇādeṣāmamā mṛtasugaṃdhini
bhūtirvilepanaṃjātāsnānaṃcānuttamaṃtriye
brahmāviṣṇuranaṃta śvaśakrognirvaruṇoyamaḥ
snānenānenasaṃpannāḥ sarveṣāmuparisthitāḥ
ādityāvasavorudrāmarutaśvāśvināvapi
tatsnānamupāsaṃtodevādevatvamāgatāḥ
tapodhanāśvayecānyesiddhāśvoragacāraṇāḥ
snānasyacaprabhāvena jātājā tivivarjitāḥ
piśācebhyorākṣasebhyoyakṣebhyaśvāpipārvati
bhūtilakṣaṇavasyānidhanānivividhāni ca
rākṣasānāma hiṃsyāśca bhavaṃtigirinaṃdini
yejanāstūpajīvaṃtibhūtiṃpāra mikāṃdvijāḥ
tecariṣyaṃtigaṇapāmamalokemadājñayā
bhūtisnānasamaṃstrānaṃ nāstivaivāmalocane
snānasya caphalaṃyaccatadviṃdatigaṇeśvarāḥ
nāstigaṃgāsamaṃtīrthenāsti vedasamāśrutiḥ
nāstimmṛtyusamaḥ śāstānāstibhūtisa maṃtapaḥ
ucchiṣṭaṃvāpramattaṃvāhiṃsatenacahiṃsakāḥ
nanaraṃbhūtisaṃsṛṣṭaṃdharṣayaṃtivināyakāḥ
evaṃparṇāda muddiśyamamaiṣā śubhagaṃdhini
bhūtirvilepanaṃ jātādevitāmarasekṣaṇe
oṃ namaḥ śivāya
triśeyaśītisaṃkhyākaiḥ ślokaiḥ śaṃkarauktavān
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃvibhūti kīrtanaṃnāmaikonatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
bhūtyutpattiśubhāṃśrutvātatogirivarātmajā
lokaniṣṭhā gṛhecaivaśavadhūmāruṇekṣaṇe
siddhacāraṇasaṃpattau saṃkulīkṛtasaṃtatau
āṃtragaṃ dhavasādhāreniṃditebhūtabhūṣite
śivārudita gaṃbhīre kā kolūkaśatākule
nā nāpakṣimṭagākīrṇesāramai yakṛtasvane
paśukṣatavapuḥ pṛṣṭhaśavamālyairalaṃkṛte
kuśakāśakṛtoddeśebrahmasūtrānubhūṣite
muśa lolūkhalayuteśivāśataravotkaṭe
ājyāhutinipātaiśvavardhamānacitākule
nānāpakṣimṭagākīrṇe sārameya kṛtasva ne
bālahasta kṛtāpīḍebhūṣitevanamālayā
vasāpūrṇa kapālaiśvacitāgnaumahiṣaṃpacan
nṛtya mānodṛhāsāśvasṛjamānobhayaṃkarān
cāsayan sarvabhūtāni pātayannivadānavān
tavanāmamahādevaciṃtitaṃvṛttamīśvara
tava bhāryāniyuktāhaṃbhāryā trailokyabhāvinī
śśramatīvahimecittaṃdūyatevahimemanaḥ
sādhvācārasyavikṛtaṃtavācāraṃniśāmyahi
tavanāmamahādevagarhitaṃvṛttamīśvara
ahaṃśoṇitapaḥkālaḥ karālavadanombike
tatomāmavadaddevaḥ purāṇo'nādiravyayaḥ
kumārakimidaṃghoraṃrodiṣītibhayātura
tadāvocamahaṃ devaṃ vadataṃ vadatāṃvaram
natiṣṭhāmi rudāmyeva tatomāṃpunarabravīt
brūhimāṃkimatobhūyaḥ karavāṇita vā'nagha
saptanāmānimetenajanitāniguhāraṇi
tatomāṃpāṇināspṛṣṭvālokeśaḥ prāha keśavaḥ
tathaivacānyā nso'dānmenāmadheyānipārvati
samāṃviditavedyastuviditātmābravīdvacaḥ
mahādevosidevānāṃta tohaṃnārudaṃpriye
aśucīnprārthayeyasmātsubhuvāṃcasamaṃtataḥ
saṃharāmicasaṃhāre harastenāsmināmataḥ
kālo bhūtvā mahākālastenāhaṃkālasaṃjñitaḥ
dhātudvayamitiproktaṃlakṣaṇāgrasitātmakaṃ
yacchukramimamādāyalokānsajjanapaṃḍitān
chāgānṛpavasādigdhe yatkṣiṇominraṇevaram
mahatsvapi mahāṃścāhaṃmatyādipatireva ca
ahaṃpīnāyataśroṇiīśvarāṇāmapīśvaraḥ
kartu hartuṃ cadātuṃ catenāhaṃ parameśvaraḥ
gulyānyetānināmānimameṣṭānīhapārvati
yenacāpihitātmāvai stutastuṣyāmyatīvahi
tataśvitāsumāṃdeviyopya caṃyatināmabhiḥ
śāśvataṃ padmā pnotigāṇapatyaṃcasaṃkṣaye
yaḥkarmaṇivisṛṣṭostividhinādevi bhāvini
sakarmakurutenātradṛśyādṛśyeniyojyate
prajāpateścakaḥśakta ādeśaṃkartumanyathā
niyuktaḥ kalikālena karmādeśaṃtataḥ priye
ahaṃsaṃva tsaraḥkālaḥprajāsaṃhārakārakaḥ
ahaṃ hitvāṃvijānāmimāṃ catvaṃ parvatātmaje
puṇyaṃcaramaṇīyaṃcasiddhakṣetraṃcapārvati iṣṭaṃśmaśānamevametatratatraramāmyaham
imecātragaṇā dhyakṣāramaṇīyāyatekṣaṇe
ramayaṃtiramaṃtomāṃśmaśānaṃtenamematam
sata caramatejaṃturbhūtireṣāprakīrtitā
leāha
dṛśyādṛśyeśubhe'śubhevā nāṃpuruṣaḥ
upadeśanāmupadeśam
karmādeśamājñataṃkarmakaromī tiśeṣaḥ
nayanānnīteḥ nayanādācaraṇāt
satasminpaśyamānastuguṇācaguṇavarṇini
snehaṃsadācakuruteśmaśānehamivānaghe
yaccāgameṣu tīrtheṣu śrutiṣucapha laṃviduḥ
phalaṃcasnānacaryāyāmanaghepravadāmyahaṃ
asauhisādhakaścāhaṃvedādiranukīrtitaḥ
uvācapunarapyāśupramathārtiharaṃharaṃ
kālakālakaleśānavacomevadatāṃvara
anyetuyercayaṃtitvāṃnṛtyagītaiśvamānavāḥ
anyetuyenamaskāraṃ kurvatyanimiṣekṣaṇāḥ
ghṛtenadanākṣīreṇaja lenacamu gaṃdhinā
gomayenatathācānyenarāstvāṃstrāpayaṃtica
gaṃdhairdhūpaiśvamālyaiśvaupahāraiścapuṣkalaiḥ
pūjayaṃtiphalaṃ teṣāṃkiṃbhaveddhitrilocana
saṃbodhyavācayābhāryāmāryāvacanamabravīt
vāmoktāsaṃbhavedevi gajanāsorumeśṛṇu
taṃtathāvipulaśroṇitārayāmibhavāṃbudheḥ
saṃbhāvitaṃmayāsamyagucyamānaṃniśāmaya
vājapeyasya yajñasya phalaṃprāpnoti mānavaḥ
so'śvame dhaphalaṃprāpyagavāṃlokemahīyate
lokaṃliṃgātmakaṃjñālvāliṃgeyorcayate himā
vedajānāsi
gokṣīreṇa caturdaśyāṃ liṃgasnāpanakāraṇāt
tena meṣṭāśvajāyaṃte akṣayāste jarāmarāḥ
tathāviśvajitodeviyeliṃgā cainatatparāḥ
brahmalokaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ golokamāmakaṃtathā
avyāhatāścaratyeva liṃgārcanaratā narāḥ
iṃdraḥ somobhagaḥ pūpāvāyuragnirdivākaraḥ
arcayaṃtitamabhbhrāṃtāliṃgārcanaratānarāḥ
gaṃdharvāpsarasāṃvandaiḥ sevyaṃ te gītavādibhiḥ
naranārāyaṇodevi jaigīṣavyovaliḥ sadā
tuṣṭimetavijānaṃtiliṃgemāma rcayaṃtiye
yo'rcāyāmarcayenmāṃhi pūrṇa varṣaśataṃnaraḥ
ekaṃca divasaṃ liṃgaṃsamametannasaṃśayaḥ
sopahāraiḥ śubhairiṣṭairmahāgaṇapatirbhavet
yastuparyuṣitaṃ mālyaṃmamāpana yatenaraḥ
yaśvāpiprayato bhūtvāliṃgamevārcayetpunaḥ
mayātavākhyātamaniṃdite kṣaṇe mano harapraśnakutūhalaṃca
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāryātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
aṣṭaṣaṣṭistuyāproktāśiva syaparamātmanaḥ
maṃdarasthaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ bahmāpṛcchatiśaṃkaram
keṣu keṣucabhāveṣudraṣṭavyosimayāprabho
vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevaṃprayā getumaheśvaraṃ
vyāsauvāca
oṃoṃnamaḥ śivāya eka
kurukṣetre tu kāleśaṃ prabhāseśaśibhūṣaṇam
puṣkaretu ayogaṃdhaṃviśvaṃcavimaleśvare
aṭṭahāse mahānādaṃmarukoṭemahotka ṭam
śaṃkukarṇemahātejaṃgo karṇetumahābalam
rudrakoṭyāṃmahāyogī mahāliṃgaṃsthaleśvare
avaṃtyāṃtumahākālaṃśarva madhyamakeśvare
kedāredevamīśānaṃ rudraṃ caiva himālaye
suvarṇākṣe sahasrākṣaṃṣetuvṛṣabhadhvajam
devadāruvanebhinnaṃ caṃḍaṃcaka bhijaṃgala
ūrdhvaketuṃsuraṃḍetumaṃ galāṃḍekapardinam
kṛttivāsetuvaradaṃsūkṣmamāghāḍikeśvare
kālaṃjare nīlakaṃṭhaṃ śrīkaṃṭhamaṃḍaleśvare
vijayaṃ caiva kāśmīrejayaṃ camarukeśvare
yamasyāṃgeviduḥsthāṇukāpilaṃkaravīrake
kāyāvatārelaguḍiṃdevikāyāmumāpatim
hariścaṃdreśvaraṃ caiva puracaṃdretuśaṃkaram
jaṭiṃkāleśvarevidyātsaumyaṃkukkuṭa keśvare
jaleśvaretriśūlaṃtu śrīśailatripurāṃtakam
lepane vai paśupa niṃdīta maṃgeśvareviduḥ
gaṃgāsāgaretyamaramoṃkāramamarakaṃṭake
saptagodāvarībhīmaṃ pātālehāṭakeśvaram
karṇikāre gaṇādhyakṣa kailāsa tripurāṃtakam
hemakūṭevirūpākṣaṃbhūrbhuvaṃgaṃdhamādane
diḍīśvare'nalaṃprāhurjvalalliṃgaṃsthaleśvare
bhūtaśvare gaṇādhyakṣaṃkairātaṃca kirātake
dānavānāṃvināśāyavārāhaṃ viṃdhyaparvate
gaṃgāha dehimasthānaṃmāna vaṃvaḍavāmukhe
śreṣṭhikoṭīśvaraṃ tīrthe viśiṣṭaceṣṭakāpathe
aṣṭaṣaṣṭistunāmā nitatradevasya cāśrayāt
purāṇecopagītānibrahmaṇāca mahātmanā
yaḥ śuciḥ prayato bhūtvāubhe saṃdhyepaṭhennaraḥ
daśānāmaśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
vyāsauvāca
āsīnaṃmaṃdarasyāgre nānāratnavibhūṣite
tatranaṃdīśvarādevaṃvibhūrtipa ryapṛcchata
naṃdīśvarauvāca
śṛṇunaṃdīśvaramattovibhūtiryādṛśamama
ekāgramānasobhūtvāniśāmaya samāhitaḥ
agniprākārakoṭistha āvatorhanasaṃśayaḥ
carāmipṛthivīṃ sarvāmāsamudraṃ surāmuraṃ
yatheṣṭacaiva tiṣṭhāmicatvareṣudhuvasthitaḥ
parvateṣusadāhṛṣṭodevyā sahavasāmyaham
pradakṣiṇaṃ sadākuryādgośa tasyaphalaṃlabhet
gavāṃśatasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpnotimānavaḥ
caṃdro'smivaruṇaścāhaṃvasāmipṛthivīmaham
dinaṃ kṣapācasaṃdhyāca kālohaṃmmṛtyunā saha
iṃdriyāṇīṃdriyārtheṣukṣayaṃ caivāhamā yam
vṛttīnāṃvṛttirevāhaṃjayohaṃ sarvabhūtiṣu
vināśaśvasurādaityāḥ pavanoḍhahanastathā
mārutohaṃ jalaṃ cāhaṃkṣipāmiba lavatsadā
ahaṃsṛjāmibhūtānisaṃkṣipāmiyugeyuge
yoniśatasahasreṣubhrāmyatetyātmalīlayā
mayātenihatādaityāstārakādyāmahābalāḥ
yeṣāṃniḥśvāsavātenatrayolokāḥ prakaṃpitāḥ
sarvabhūtakṣayaṃtyevaṃ kṛtavānnātra saṃśayaḥ
sarvabhūteṣuvai nityaṃvasāmi muditaḥ sadā
itihāsapurāṇeṣuvede caivavasāmyah
nataṃdeśaṃvijānāmimayāśūnyaṃhiyadbhavet
bhaktānāṃsarvabhūtānāṃyacamāṃśaraṇāgatāḥ
ananyamānaso bhūtvāyomāṃpūjayatenaraḥ
saṃtuṣṭohaṃpradāsyāmigāṇapatyaṃ sudurlabhaṃ
vasāmyahaṃpuṣpiteṣuvṛkṣeṣucalatāsuca
naṃdikeśva ranārīṇāṃsthitohaṃrūpayauvane
samaṃjīvaścadāsaśvasarveṣāṃniyamaiḥ saha
sarvatīrthābhigamanaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati bhārata
mahātmāsajana śreṣṭhojarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ
bhaktānāmityādisārdhamekānvayi
jīvaḥsvāmī
sukhāsīnāyathāśāṃtikrīḍate cayathāsukham
prāpnuvaṃtiśubhān lokāntairvai karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ
caṃḍālādyāśvamabhaktāḥśū karīpakṣipoṣakāḥ
matprapannāśvakravyādāḥ sarpadaṃśopajīvanaḥ
brahmapu trasya tadvākyaṃ śrutvānaṃdīgaṇādhipaḥ
pratyuvāca śubhaṃvākyaṃyathāpūjayathāvidhi
adhyātmadhyānayukta śvayena sidhyaṃti mānavāḥ
mānavāsteṣutatveṣutulyakarmavaśānugāḥ
tāvadbhamaṃti saṃsāreyāvaddhyānaṃnaviṃdati
asurāścaiva devāśvakapayaḥ pitarastathā
yathābrahmādayoṃdevādīpyatedhyānatejasā
brāhmaṇāḥkṣatriyāvaiśyāḥ śūdrā yāvarṇasaṃkarāḥ
cāṃḍālāśva aṃtyajāśva sarvetepāpakarmaṇaḥ
tecaraṃ tiśubhān lokāndhyānaṃdahatikilbiṣam
sarvapāpeṣusaktāyeteca siddhyaṃ timānavāḥ
dhyānayogavidhitsaṃ mokṣadvāravidhiśṛṇu
agamyāgāmībrahmanaḥ surāpogurutalpagaḥ
śataṃśakaṭabhārāṇāṃjaṃtūnāṃyena hiṃsitam
tatpāpaṃharatedhyānī kāṣṭharāśimivānalaḥ
kumārīdūṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā mātaṃgīgamanaṃtathā
abhakṣyabhakṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā apeyaṃpītamevaca
tadviśodhayatedhyānīdīptāgniriva kāṃcanaṃ
tatvajñānāṃtaraṃprāpya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
pāpakarmaṇaḥ pāpakarmāṇaḥ
pītaṃ kṛtvetyanvayaḥ
yadimokṣaṃnagacchati bhogavāsanāyāḥ satyāditibhāvaḥ
brahmalokepivāvāsoviṣṇuloke yadṛcchayā
somasūryāgnideveṃdrāviśeṣaṃsthānamāpnuyāt
yamalokepivāvāsaḥpū jyamānasyadaivataiḥ
yathoktenavidhānenaviśuddhenāṃtarātmanā
sadaivaṃdhyānayuktasyaśivaṃprāpnotinānyathā
adhītya caturovedān sāṃgopaniṣado dvijaḥ
dhyānasyadeva gulyasya kalāṃ nārhatiṣoḍaśīm
vinādeva varaṃdhyānaṃśaucācārasama nvitam
natacchakyaṃ phalaṃ prātuṃ ṛtukoṭiśatairapi
adhītyacaturāve dāndhyānayogaṃviśiṣyate
yaḥ sahasraṃsahasrāṇāṃ bhojayedvai dvijāṃstathā
yaḥsahasraṃsahasrāṇāṃbhojayetsatyavādinām
saṃkalpināṃsahasreṇastrā takānāṃśatenaca
gṛhasthānāṃsahasreṇatrahmacāriśatena ca
sāṃkhyayogaviśuddhānāṃbhuṃjānoyasyayogavit
pratigraheṇa mūḍhātmānavimucyeta kilviṣam
punātidhyā ninasteṣāmitijñānaparigrahe
yathāparvatamāsādya āśrayaṃtimṛgādhipāḥ
tatvaviśvavidoyogamāśrayaṃti dvijottamāḥ
viśvavitsarvakarmāṇitathākṛtvānalipyate
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāmekatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmi kena maṃtreṇadhyāyate
dhyānaṃkativi dhaṃdevapratigṛhṇaṃtitattathā
akṣarāśvakathaṃdevārudra viṣṇupitāmahāḥ
naṃdīśvarau vāca
brahmāvaivāmapārśvatudakṣapārśvatu keśavaḥ
ubhābhyāṃmadhyatorudrastiṣṭhatetyekavigrahāḥ pūrvādhyāyatebrahmāmadhyānhe cajanārdanaḥ
trailokyaṃ devadevasyarudra viṣṇupitāmahāḥ
anugrahārthalo kānāṃbhaktānāmanukaṃpayā
ātmadehaṃtridhādevaḥ sakarotipṛthakpṛthak
ru drasāyujyatāṃyāṃtiityāha bhagavānśivaḥ
natānsaṃkramatepāpaṃmriyateceddivaṃga taḥ
akāro bhagavānviṣṇurukāraścapitāmahaḥ
makāraśvasvayaṃrudrovijñeyādhyānatatparaiḥ
akāraṃcatvadhaḥ kṛtvā oṃkāraṃcaprayojayet
ukāraṃcamakāraṃcamātra yāsahayojayet
makāraṃtu śanaiḥrutvāyojayetrividhaṃtathā
oṃkāraṃ hṛdaye kṛtvādhyānaṃyuṃjītayogavit
oṃkāraṃvaidikānāṃ tuyogināṃcatathaivaca
oṃkāraṃdhyāyamānasyajanmasūtraṃnavidyate
tataoṃkārayogīca akṣarādakṣaraṃ bhavet
nigṛtyasarveṃdriyāṇi dhyānaṃyuṃjīta yogavit
aṃguṣṭhamātraṃ puruṣaṃhṛdikṛtvāśivaṃprabhum
lalāṭamadhyecaṃdrābhamacyutaṃlokapāvanam
avyayaṃ sūkṣmabhāvaṃ taṃ mūrdhni kṛtvāśivaṃ prabhum
omiti brahmayuṃjī triguṇaṃ caiva tristhānaṃdhyakṣaraṃtathā
uccāryamāṇamapicetsaṃyamyātmānamā tmavit
prāṇāyāmeciraṃprāṇasaṃyamyacapunaḥpunaḥ
nimeṣamātramapicetdhyānaṃyuṃjīta yogavit
oṃkārepratha maṃyogaṃnityaṃdhyāyītamānavaḥ
kūrmogānīva saṃhatya iṃdriyāṇi sukhāni ca
prakāśayettadātmānaṃnirvātedīpavaddudhaḥ
oṃkāraṃ dhyāyate dhīrovi śuddhenāṃtarātmanā
dhārayitvāyathāśaktyātataḥ pratyāharetpunaḥ
prāṇāyāmairvaśaṃrutvāmanaśvasthiramevaca
akāraśvaukāraśvamakāraścaivatetrayaḥ
ekaikaśastrayodevāviṣṇurudrapi tāmahāḥ
naṃdīśvaraṃ pariṣvajyatdṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭastapodhanaḥ
yogaṃgulyatamaṃ śrutvāsthāneṣucayathātatham
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesa natkumārasaṃhitāyāṃnaṃdīśvarayogākhyānaṃnāmadvātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
prāṇāyāmaṃyathādhyānaṃpratyāhāraṃcadhāraṇām
teṣāṃkramaviśeṣeṇa yogānāṃlakṣaṇaṃparam
pravakṣyāmiyathātattvaṃsvayaṃrudreṇabhāṣitam
prāṇāyāmastathācāpiprāṇasyāyāmaucyate
prāṇāpānanirodhaistumaṃtrai mātrāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ
ityeṣavividhaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmasyalakṣaṇaḥ
siṃhovākuṃjarovāpitathā'nyovāṭa govane
naivagrāhonavā'nyovādurādharṣaśrajāyate
yogaṃniviśamānastunadoṣaṃprāpnuyātkvacit
kālāṃtaravaśādyogādabhīkṣṇaṃparimardanāt
paricī yamānayogasyatathājāyetamārutaḥ
vaśitvaṃ catathācāpigacchateyogamāsthitaḥ
yathāsiṃhomṭagovāpinīyamānovyavasthitaḥ
abhayaṃcamanuṣyāṇāṃmṭagebhyaḥ saṃpravartate
mārutoyoginovaśyobhavatītibhāvaḥ
vyavasthitaḥ vaṃśesthito bhavatītiśeṣaḥ
manasipīvāyāṃcasamaḥ viṣayāṃtarama dhyāyanka jukāyaśveti bhāvaḥ
sīvanyāḥ vṛṣaṇamadhyagarekhāyāḥ
tathāparicīyamānaḥśarīrakilbiṣaṃdehat
prāṇāyāmenayuktasyaviprasyaniyatātmanaḥ
sarvadoṣāḥ praṇaśyaṃtisatvastha ścaivajāyate
tīrthāniyānipaṭhyaṃteniyamānitratānica
prāṇāyāmairda heddoṣāndhāraṇābhiśvakilbiṣam
pratyāhāreṇaviṣayāndhyānenānaśvarānguṇān
tasmādyuktaḥ sadāyogīprāṇāyā mānsamācaret
ataḥparaṃpravakṣyāmiprāṇāyāmasyalakṣaṇam
āsanaṃsvastikaṃkuryātpadyaṃbhadrāsanaṃtathā
samajānumekapādapāṇyottānaṃcasaṃsthitaḥ
manogrīvāsamobhutvāsaṃgṛ tyacaraṇāvubhau
jānṛvaraṃtareviprakṛtvāpādataleu
aṃguṣṭhāvapigṛhṇī yāddhastābhyāṃvyutkrameṇatu
gu lphautuvṛṣaṇasyā'dhaḥsīvanyāḥ pārśvayoḥ kṣiṣet
pārśvapādacapāṇibhyāṃdṛḍhabadhvāsuniśvalaḥ
saṃvṛtāsyomīlitākṣaupaviṣṭaśvavāgyataḥ
pāṇibhyāṃdapaṇaṃrakṣettathāśephena nityaśaḥ
kiṃcidu nāmitamukhodatairdatānnasaṃspṛśet
jivhāṃnacālayetkvāpipāṣāṇaivaniśvalaḥ
kṛtvābhūtvā sthiroyogī saṃyuktaḥ susamāhitaḥ
iṃdriyāṇīṃdriyārthaścamanaḥpaṃcamavāyavaḥ
nirudhyasa mabhāvena kūrmogānīva sarvaśaḥ
nivṛttiviṣayāṇāṃtupratyāhāramupakramet
tathādvādaśamātrastuprāṇāyāmovidhīyate
dhāraṇādvādaśāyāmesevecca dhāraṇātyayaṃ
daśadvādaśaviṃśatyācatu viṃśatidhāraṇāḥ
dhāraṇādhārayedyogīnityamadhyātmacitakaḥ
paśyate paramātmānaṃdivyamevaṃ kutojaniḥ
dhārayitvāyathāśaktyāśanaiḥ pratyāharetpunaḥ
jitvājitvāśanairbhūya ārabheccasadāmuniḥ
vivardhayatisaṃmūḍhaṃtasmādeva jitāmahī
prāṇāyāmasya saṃrodhāt prāṇāyāmastupaṭhyate
dhārayeccāpi yadvāyuṃdhāraṇāmitinirdiśet
nivattaviṣayāṇāṃtupratyāhāraṃnasaṃśayaḥ
sarveṣāṃsamavāyena siddhiḥ syādyogalakṣaṇā
dhyānayuktāstupaśyaṃti ātmānaṃjalacaṃdravat
tathāsaṃdarśanaṃprāpte kṣemaprāptivinirdiśet
deśakālavideśa staṃvijñeyaṃtattvalakṣaṇam
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃyo gavidhirnāmatrayastriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
sukhopaviṣṭamāsīnaṃ mahādevaṃ svayaṃbhuvam
papracchamuni śārdūlodurvāsāstumahāmuniḥ
bhagavaṃtaṃbhavodvignaidamāharutāṃjaliḥ
bhagavan kena mucyatenarāḥ pāpeṣuyeratāḥ
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāvaiśyāḥ śūdrāścaiva tathāvibho
śvapākāmleccha mātaṃgāḥśūkarāḥ pakṣighātakāḥ
pāpāśrayāḥ kṛtaghnāśva lolupāścahavirdhakāḥ
kanyānāṃ dūṣakācaiva kulaghnāḥ strīnapuṃsakāḥ
mātṛtyāgīpiṭatyāgīrājaghnāścaiva ye narāḥ
paradra vyāpahārīcayuddhecāpiparāṅmukhāḥ
aśaktāvaṅkuśa ścaivaśaktyāvṛttibhujaśvaye
cāṃḍālā matsya vaddhāśva agamyāgama neratāḥ
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ sarvapāpeṣuye narāḥ
gacchaṃtena kathaṃ tātapāpiṣṭhāṃ gatimevaca
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāvaiśyāḥ śūdrāścaivatathāpare
śvapākāmlecchamātaṃgāyecānyepāpakarmiṇaḥ
evaṃtedhyāninoviprādate pāpakaṃkṣaṇāt
pitṛpatnībhrātṛpatnīṃ bhagi nīṃgāvamevaca
dhyānināṃśuddhabuddhīnāṃdhyānenaviditātmanām
dhyānaṃ ciṃtayamānasyaekacittenadhyāninaḥ
ekenadhyānayogena tatpāpaṃnirdahetkṣaṇāt
pitṛpatnīṃ bhrātṛpatnīṃ bhaginīṃgāva me vaca
śuddhāśuddhonarovipradhyānena tuna saṃśayaḥ
dhyānahīnoyastu nityaṃdṛḍhayuktodṛḍhavrataḥ
agnilokaṃvā yulokamiṃdralokaṃprajāpatiḥ
viṣṇulokāṃtaraṃgatvābrahmalokātparāṃgatim
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ catustriṃśo'dhyā yaḥ
durvāsā uvāca
kiṃcadhyānaṃsuraśreṣṭhakaśvadhyātāca nityaśaḥ
etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ tvatprasādā dravīhime
ahaṃvakṣyāmitatsarvaśṛṇuṣvāvahitomama
oṃkāraṃ paramaṃdhyānaṃyogaṃyuṃjīta yogavit
upaviśyāsanaṃtatra somamaṃḍalakaṃ tathā
padmamaṃḍalakaṃcaiva svastikaṃsamudāhṛtam
rudrapoṭhaṃcavacaṃcavajjadaṃḍoṃ nnataṃtathā
ityeteāsanāḥ proktānānārūpaguṇānvitāḥ
eteṣāmekamāsthāya āsanaṃtuvicakṣaṇaḥ
patirbhūtvā rudrādilokān gacchatītyarthaḥ
iticatustriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya paṃcatriṃśattame'dhyāye
ladhvāhārojitakrodhaekāṃteca nirāmayaḥ
śiṣṭasaṃsargava jitve darśanābhyāgamaṃtathā
ciṃtayeḍyāninonityaṃśāstradṛṣṭe nakarmaṇā
ekāgramānasobhūtvāutpattiṃpralayaṃtathā
yuṃjīta svaśarīrasyayuṃ jānonacahiṃsakaḥ
yathāhyahaṃśarīrasya śukraśoṇitasaṃbhavaḥ
kimasmākaṃśarīrārthe'nitye caivaśarīrake
majjā medosthisaṃpūrṇeśirājālenasaṃvṛte
śleṣmamūtrapurīṣe pudurgaṃdhajanmasaṃbhave
vyādhi śokagaṇeghoraṃ mamatvaṃhiśarīra ke
prāṇāstu rudrāvijñeyā avimuktaṃ paraṃ smṛtam
bātyaṃtukathayiṣyāmi hitārthaṃ sarva jaṃtuṣu
āṃtaraṃśṛṇuyādyogaṃyogaviyaṃvaraṃ sadā
śrotraṃtvakcakṣuṣījivhānāsikā cetipaṃcamī
pṛthivyāpastathātejovāyurākāśapaṃcamāḥ
mahābhūtānikartavyaṃ jñānārthajñānamevaca
avyaktaṃ parisaṃkhyātuṃprāṇāyāmastudhāraṇā
prāṇāyāmairvaśaṃkṛtvāsarvāmiṃdriyavāhinīm
tatoyuṃjīta medhāvīprāṇaṃcama nasāmuniḥ
pṛthagbhāvanatattvānāṃ paśvākuṃjītamūrdhani
ekatvaṃ prāṇamanaso riṃdriyāṇāṃsamanvitaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃ hitāyāṃ durvāsopanipannāmapaṃcatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
ātmanāmanasā
itipaṃcatriśodhyāyaḥ
prāṇopānaḥ samāna udānovyānaevaca
tānhitvāvāyavaḥ paṃcadhārayaṃtyātmanātmani
pādecaivorujaṃghāsuśilevṛṣaṇayostathā
pāyūpasthakaṭī vāvhorhṛdaye pārśvayostathā
hṛda ye vipulemadhyepṛṣṭhecāthalalāṭayoḥ
nābhimadhyeśarīrasyaviditaṃ sūryamaṃḍalam
jvālāmālā sahasaistu āpyamāneputejasā
somamaṃḍalamadhyetuparamātmābhitiṣṭhati
asthisnāyuśirāmāṃsavarjitāduḥkhavarjitaḥ
nacaśyā monacaraktonakṛṣṇonacapāṃḍuraḥ
nāpiṃgalonapiṃgaścalohitonanaśābalaḥ
ādityavarṇapuruṣaṃsataṃvidyādvicakṣaṇaḥ
īśvaraścabhavaścaivacityaḥkartāsakīrtyate
śuddhasphaṭikavarṇābhodṛśyatenacacakṣuṣā
krīḍārthasṛjate lokān khyātyarthe ca maheśvaraḥ
lokepukrīḍatenityaṃvālaḥ krīḍanakairiva
palāśasyaya thāpatraṃ sarvavyāptaṃhitaṃtubhiḥ
paramātmātathālokān jagatkṛtsraṃhitiṣṭhati
sūryairaśmiryayātyeṣasarvatejāṃsidhāraya
evaṃtenatathāvyānaṃśarīraṃparamātmanā
paramātmetivijñeyojñānābhyāsenabhodvija
abhyāsātpaśyate sarvaṃ paramā tmānamātmani
imaṃyogavidhirutvāśṭaṇutattvaṃmanīṣiṇaḥ
daśaprāṇavahānāḍyodehideheṣusaṃsthitāḥ
catasro vastuvijñeyāddecanāḍhyaucapārśvayoḥ
ūrdhvaṃtu caturojñeyānāḍyastuparikīrtitāḥ
nāḍīnāṃtusahasrāṇidvāsaptatiriti
padmasaṃkāśasaṃsthānaṃhṛdayaṃtatradṛśyate
sūkṣmohipuruṣojñeyaḥ parātmāhṛdisaṃsthitaḥ
śuddhasphaṭikavarṇābhaṃnirguṇaṃśā śvataṃdhuvam
tvaṃsavageṣusarvagāmītīrthasraṣṭādhātācaprayuktavānprasūtaḥ
pra thitābhāvānāṃstraṣṭāhartāprasavitādharmotsukastadevāgnistadādityaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃṣaṭ triṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
durvāsāuvāca
jñāpayāmipunardevaprasādaṃ kuruśaṃ kara
kīdṛśothabhaveddeheṣaḍaṃgoyogaucyate
prāṇāyāmastathādhyānaṃdhāraṇāyogaucyate
prāṇasyagra haṇaṃnityaṃprāṇāyāmaḥsaucyate
oṃkāraṃmanasādhyāyedekāgremanasāsmaran
dhyānenatusadāyogīdhyānasaṃvittatāparaḥ
sarveṣāmidriyāṇāṃtuviṣayāṇāṃtathaiva ca
pratipacyāharaṃ kṛtvāpratyāhāraḥsaucyate
daśānāmiṃdriyāṇāṃtu oṃkā reprītamānasaḥ
paṃcamaṃbrahmacaryacaityeteniyamāḥ smṛtāḥ
akrodhoguruśuśrūṣāśaucaṃsaṃtoṣama ryavat
etetuniyamāḥpaṃcavijñeyābrahmavādiṣu
ṣaḍaṃgoyogaityeṣaśuddhevijñānaucyate
sagacchetparamaṃsthānaṃśāśvataṃ pa damavyayam
atiśūnyaṃtuyasyārtheśarīraṃkīrtitaṃbudhaiḥ
tasyacāṃteśarīrasya saśarīraḥsaucyate
jñānaṃniraṃjanaṃcaiva avyaktaṃtriguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
draṣṭāsaṣṭācasapitāmantāboddhātathaivaca
puruṣaṃśāśvataṃsūkṣmaṃdraṣṭavyaṃ dhyāna cakṣuṣā
avyaktaṃtriguṇaṃ bhadrapuruṣaśvātraśāśvataḥ
paṃcaviṃśattuvijñeyamīśamīśā namavyayam
saṃbhūtiṃcavināśaṃcabhāvābhāvautathaivaca
yastuvettinaraḥprājñaḥ sarve draṣṭāṣṭaviṃśakaḥ
paṃcaviṃśakatattvānijñāyaṃtetusadānaraiḥ
paṃcaviśattadājñeyamīśānamavyayaṃparaṃ
puruṣaḥ saṃca ditvācajñātvācasagacchetparamāṃ gatiṃ
saevaṃ paṃcaviṃśatikaḥ ṣaḍūiṃśakastathaivaca
ūnaviṃśatikaṃvidyāttatvajñānārtha ciṃtakaḥ
viṃśakaṃtu tadājñātvā amṛtatvāya kalpate
caturviṃśagṛhaṃyogaeṣavaipaṃcaviṃśakaḥ
ṣaḍśitistathājñe yāadhyakṣaḥsaptaviṃśakaḥ
aṣṭaviṃśakaḥ puruṣastriṃśat puruṣalokadhṛk
yaṃviditvānaśocaṃtitaṃśivaṃkathayāmite
oṃ kāraṃ paramaṃdevaṃ paṃ cāyatanavāsinaṃ
durvāsā uvāca
kathaṃjñeyaṃhibhagavanmātrākṣaravivarjitaṃ
śṛṇuvi prayathānyāyaṃmātrākṣaravivarjitaṃ
śarīraṃ hitadābrahmayajjñātvāmucyateyatiḥ
prathamāvaidvitīyācavijñeyākṣara mālinī
tṛtīyā'nimiṣācaivavijñeyāyoga citakaiḥ
pipīḍitārdhamātrāvai vijñeyāguṇavarjitā
praśāṃtācākṣaraṃ caiva tāṃviditvātumucyate
akārovaidyu tācaivaukārokṣaragāminī
makāronimiṣānāmapraśāṃtaṃtupipīḍitā
ma kārastuumājñeyāpraśāṃtaṃśāśvataṃ dhruvaṃ
oṃ kāraṃtuyadāyogīyuṃjānaḥ samudāharet
vijñānākhyātadājñeyānityamakṣaragā minī
cityamānaṃtuba huśomaṇi sūtranidarśanaiḥ
iṣukāra ivāsakto yathāgniṃnatupaśyati
tādṛśaṃbhāvayedrahmata dāviṃdatitatparaṃ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ durvāsa upaniṣatsu saptatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
idaṃśarīraṃvipreṃdrasarvadevamayaṃ śṛṇu
viṣṇustupādevijñeyo jaṃghayormarutastathā
jānubhyāmaśvinaujñeyau ūrubhyāṃvaruṇastathā
oṃnamaḥśivāya atriśeśarīraṃtu sarvadevamayaṃva
aṃtesamudrāvipreṃdraudarepaṃcadeva tāḥ
romakūpe dharmaeva mūrdhyādityonasaṃśayaḥ
saṃdhisamarṣayojñeyāścakṣubhyaṃ sūryaeva ca
śrotrāṇica diśaḥ sarvāvijñeyābrahmavādibhiḥ
nuvostuparvatājñeyālalāṭevasavastathā
śivaḥ svayaṃbhūrvijñeyonityameva pratiṣṭhitaḥ
aparāṃteyamaścaivatathāvedhāḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
aparāṃgerātrayaśradevatāścaiva pārśvayoḥ
śubheprāṇagatiḥ kaṃṭhebhavaṃtivṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
etajjñātvā ca budhvācagacchaṃti paramāṃ gatiṃ
durvāsā uvāca
ete proktāḥśarīrasyādevatā ṛṣayastathā
prāṇāhutiṃ kathaṃ sarvela bhaṃte vṛṣabhadhvaja
mahādevauvāca
prāṇopānaḥ samānaśva udānovyānaevaca
ityetevāyavaḥ paṃcaśarīrecapratiṣṭhitāḥ
sāvitrīcaturovedāḥ sapaḍaṃgapadakramāḥ
oṣadhyaśvavanaspatyaḥ somabhāskara mārutāḥ
tenānnenatutṛpyaṃtiyatprāṇejuvatidvijāḥ
tenanāgāḥ samudrāśvasaritaḥ sāgarāstathā
ṛṣayaḥpitaraścaiva sarvedevāḥ savāsavāḥ
samānejuhute yastutṛtīyāmāhutiṃddijaḥ
aśvinaumarutoviṣṇurvaruṇaścayamastathā
prajāpatiḥkuberaśvasarvedevagaṇāstathā
tenāhaṃcabhavaścaivatyu bhaunaṃdīgaṇeśvaraḥ
umābrahmāpivipreṃdramanaḥprāṇāstathaiva ca
vyāne vaijuhuteyāṃtupaṃcamī māhutiṃdvi jaḥ
saptalokāśvabrahmāṃḍāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
bhavaḥ rudraḥ
oṃnamaḥśivāya ū evaṃtu satataṃviprājuhutepraṇavenave
śvapākasyāpibhuṃjānonasapāpena lipyate
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāvaiśyāḥ śūdrāvā yadivāpaṭhet
vedāhametaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāṃtamādityavarṇatamasaḥ parastāt
viṣaṃhālāhalaṃpītvānadhruvaṃ mṛtyumāpnuyāt
etamevamidaṃjñātvā amṛtatvamavāpnuyāt
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ durvāsopaniṣatsu aṣṭatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
yattvayoktaṃ bhagavatāsāṃkhyayogaviśārada
yoganāḍīmimāṃtra lanśrotumicchāmitadvratam
praṇamyaśirasādevamakṣayaṃbhuvaneśvaram
kātyāyanīṃnamaskṛtvārudra patnīṃviśeṣataḥ
pārameṣṭhyamidaṃjñānaṃnāḍīsaṃcārasaṃsthitam
viśvamūrti ryadāśrīmān dehasyaḥ krīḍatetadā
anaṃtāraśmayastasyajagaddehāśritāstathā
yoganāḍīḥ pravakṣyāmithṛdayasthānamā śritāḥ
pūrvadakṣiṇapaśvārddhauttarāṃmūrtimāśritāḥ
adhastādevanāḍyastutāsāṃvarṇānnibodha me
pītalohitakṛṣṇāśrva uttarāḥ pāṃḍupiṃgalāḥ
pūrvāḥ śvetāstathānāḍyodakṣiṇāḥ kṛṣṇapiṃgalāḥ
ūrdhvatuniṣṭhitāyāstu kṛṣṇānāḍyastu coditāḥ
paṃcapaṃcasmṛtānāḍyothṛdi saṃsthāna saṃśritāḥ
śatamekottaraṃnāḍīmupāsatecayoginaḥ
sarvāśvatāḥ samutsṛjyabrahma nāḍīṃsamāśrayet
nābhināḍībhi ratyartha krīḍāmohavisarjanam
ṣaṇṇavatyaḥ sahasrāṇināḍīnāṃhṛdisaṃsthitāḥ
pūrvanāḍyastuyāḥ paṃcaprāṇādyāḥ parikī titāḥ
dakṣiṇāyāḥsthitānāḍyastāsāṃpaṃcajalāiti
paścimottaranāḍyostu udānaṃcottarāṇica
samānasyānibodhyāni adhastāyāḥ samāśritāḥ
dviguṇaṃtupraviṣṭāstuhṛdayānaṃtaraṃtatāḥ
etannāḍīpramāṇaṃtuviśvaṃyatrapratiṣṭhitam
ktāścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktamaṇoraṇīyānāḍītyadhastātsa tu viśvakarmaṇā
tenaivanāḍhyaṃtara saṃcareṇaśuddhasya nāḍidimūrdhnilakṣayet
sābrahmanāḍītivaṃdatitajjñāḥ parāparajñānanidhānabhūtāḥ
paṃceṃdriyā ṇisaṃyuktāpaṃcakarmabhiriṃdriyaiḥ
sarve te hṛdisaṃvaddhāyogena hṛdipādayoḥ
sarva nāḍīsahasrāṇāṃ guṇāneva catuṣṭayam
tāḥ
mūrdhnibhitvāna bhoyātināsikāmūrdhaeva ca
śukra mūtravahānāḍīekī bhūtātumiśritā
retasāsaṃprasūyaṃ te mūtraṃ caivatathaiva ca
brahmanāḍīmukheyasya manasāthṛdiceśvaram
trīṇicāsthi sahasrāṇivarṇasṛṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā
snāyūnāṃ sahasrāṇiparaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ smṛtam
sūkṣmātsūkṣmatarobhāvoyaṃviditvānayujyate
somasūryāṃśubhiḥ pītaṃ padmaṃcaiva saviṃdati
tatroparinayaṃtyeva yogināṃ mūrdhniśāyinām
jñānenavijñāyanivṛttakalmaṣābhitvāsthitiṃtrahmavidaḥprayāṃ ti
sanatkumāreṇedaṃtunāḍīsaṃcārasūcitam
yogaśāstramidaṃ puṇyaṃmokṣaśāstraṃsuniśvitam
brahmādyairṛṣibhi gataṃyogaśāstraṃviniścitam
puṇyātpuṇyataraṃsyetatpavipāpanāśanam
nāḍīmukhetucitātmāsarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
nāḍīmadhyagataṃviśvaṃśudhyatepitṛmātṛjam
gomūtraṃ saptamepāpaṃdahatecāṣṭametathā
tenāpiśraṅgyānāḍīmūrdhnyadhastādvi niḥsṛtā
sanāḍītotha maṃtavyoyena viśvaṃ hṛditrajet
pūrvāstetyaditiṣṭhatitanmanastatparāyaṇāḥ
tāvatsaṃcita yedugraṃyāvatātanmatomataḥ
nāḍīsūkṣmeṇa mārgeṇaurdhvayātyuttarāyaṇam
tā bhyāmadhastādyatkāryaṃ tadgataṃtasya saṃsmṛtaṃ
vidhānaṃcaivanāḍyāstuśarīreyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
snāyustrīṇisaha srāṇisarvāstānābhijāḥsmṛtāḥ
ṣaṇṇavatyaḥ sahakhāṇiśirāṇāṃhṛdisaṃsthitāḥ
tevaiśivānimārgāṇiviśvoyatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ
sarvanāḍīḥparityajyabrahmanāḍīṃsamāśrayet
sānāṃḍīsarva durgāṇitārayennaurivārṇavaṃ
ekanāḍīnirālaṃ vātālumadhyeśirogatā
sānāḍīyogayuktānāṃmokṣadāsādivaṃgatā
śukramajjāvasāmedaḥkaphaṃpittaṃśarīrayoḥ
śirāṃsitasyasrotāṃsiekaikaṃśukraraṃdhrayoḥ
dhūtapāpādivayāṃtimūrdhnibhitvātamīśvaram
dhyāyaḥ
devaiḥsadivyairṛṣayaḥsamagrābrahmācaviṣṇuśca maheśvaraśca
vāyuryamognirvaruṇaḥ śaśāṃkaḥ sarvānnirīkṣyaivadivaṃprayāṃti
guṇaistuvaṃtopi mukhābhimukhyairdhyāyaṃtigāyaṃticapūjayaṃti
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃekonacatvāriṃśodhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
tathācoṃkāradevasya mahābhāgyaṃ vadasva me
śṛṇuvyāsaparaṃgutyaṃrahasyaṃ yogamuttamam
yaddevāpinavidaṃtikāṃkṣamāṇāḥ paraṃ padaṃ
tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmiyanmayātu śrutaṃpurā
pārvatyāsahasaṃ vādaṃdevadevasyaśūlinaḥ
tīrthopaniṣadaṃ puṇyaṃmokṣadaṃ sarvadehinām
kathayāmāsa deveśorahasyaṃjñānamuttamam
svapuraṃcitayāmāsa sovimuktagaṇādhipaḥ
vārāṇasīṃvinādevonaratiṃprāpya kutracit
uvācavākyaṃvaradojagannāthapinākadhṛk
yenakāryeṇa suśro ṇitadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
siddhāṃtānāṃca sarveṣāṃ smṛtīnāṃ caivasuṃdari
caturdaśānāṃbhuvanānāṃyaśvasāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
ātma jñānaṃparaṃgulyaṃyajjñātvāmokṣamaśnute
soyaṃdevisthitaḥ sākṣātdrāvāsesvayaṃprabhuḥ
tridhāsthānaṃtribhoktāraṃtribhojyaṃcatathāparaṃ
yatayośvaparaṃvidyātsijyaṃte dbhāvaṃparamāsthitāḥ
oṃ kāraṃparamaṃtrahmaparamaṃcavidurbudhāḥ
paṃcabrahmasamāyuktaṃpaṃcāyatanavāsināṃ
yedrakṣyaṃti śivaṃtatratedrakṣyaṃtiparaṃpadaṃ
brāhmaṇāstavamuṃcativedavedāṃgapāragāḥ
yatayaḥ puṇyakarmāṇoyecānyevedasaṃsthitāḥ
nānāliṃgadharāvipravedaśāstraparāyaṇāḥ
gṛhasthāścaiva yatayastasmāttīrthaupāsa kāḥ ekadaṃḍāstridaṃḍāśca haṃsavratadharāśva ye
śaivāḥpāśupatāyecakapālavratacāriṇaḥ
upāsatecamāṃnityaṃ mūkaṃ cavratamāsthitāḥ
karmabhedena teṣāṃtu sarveṣāmāsthitotyahaṃ
vibhajāmi paraṃsthānaṃtanmokṣaṃ paramaṃ padaṃ
śmaśānaṃtaṃtra nityaṃsannihitādevojaṃtūnāṃcaivatārakaḥ
tasyāṃpuryāvyavasthānātprakhyātāmevimuktatā
avyaktaliṃgaṃbhitvaivata thāsaṃsārabhīrubhiḥ
tatraviśveśvaraṃdṛṣṭvāsaṃsārenapatetpunaḥ
viśveśvaraṃcakāraṃetatsāraṃprakīrtayet
siddhakṣetraṃtapaḥkṣetraṃ yathāvārāṇasīmune
sparśanādarśanāttasya kṛtārthāmānavābhuvi
tāraṇaṃ sarva jaṃtūnāṃnānāpāpasyanāśanaṃ
saṃdhyopāsitābhavatisakṛtvādaśamāsakṛt
devadevonadīgaṃgāssṛṣṭimaṃtraḥ stutā patiḥ
vārāṇasyāṃmahāpuṇyaṃ kasyavāsonarocate
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ catvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
pūrṇabhadrasutaḥ śrīmān āsīdyakṣa pratāpavān
tadāsītannamaskārastadbhaktasyaparāyaṇaḥ
āsīnaścaśayānaścagacchanti ṣṭhannanuvrajan
bhuṃjānovāpidhāvaṃśvarūpamevānuciṃtayan
tasyaivaṃ yuktamanasaḥ pūrṇabhadraḥ pitābravīt
nahiyakṣa kulīnānāmevaṃ vṛttirbhavetsuta
gutyakāratnayūyaṃ vai svabhāvātkrūra cetasaḥ
ka vyādācaiva kiṃtatrahiṃsāśīlāścaputraka
naiva kāryānatevṛtirevaṃdṛṣṭvā mahātmanām
oṃnamaḥ śivāya
ekacatvāriṃśaketra harikeśākhyaguhmakaḥ
daṃḍapāṇirabhūddevapra vameva asatiananyabhāvenaśaraṇaṃgacchatisaḥ
bhāvapradhānāpaṃcamī
svayaṃbhuvāyathādṛṣṭvātyaktavānmahitebhavet
āśramāṃtarajaṃ karmanakuryādgṛhiṇastataḥ
devatvaṃnodhimārgeṣumānuṣyaṃjātimevaca
namayāvihitaṃtasyaka rmatannātra saṃśayaḥ
ityevamuktvāputraṃtupūrṇabhadraḥ pratāpavān
vārāṇasīṃsamāsādya tapastepe mahātmavān
sthāṇubhūtotyavi śeṣaḥśuṣkakāṣṭhopalopamaḥ
tyaktvāgotrakṛtāṃvṛttiṃtathājātikṛtāstataḥ
ihāgatyacadharmātmāgokarṇāyatane śubhe
ārādhayanyeyogīśaṃgokarṇadevamīśvaram
saṃniyamyeṃdriyagrāmama vātiṣṭhataniścalaḥ
sahasramekaṃvarṣāṇāṃdivyaṃ saṃnyativarttata
vālmīkena samākrāṃtobhakṣyamāṇaḥpipīlakaiḥ
rājasūcīmukhaistīkṣṇairvidhyamānastathaiva ca
nirmāsarudhironnaṃ vaikuṃdaśaṃkheṃ dusapra bhaḥ
etasminnaṃtaredevīvijñāpayatiśaṃkaram
udyānaṃpunarevedaṃdraṣṭumicchā mitevara
itivijñāpitodevaḥpārvatyāparameśvaraḥ
śarvaḥ pṛṣṭoyathānyāyamākhyātumupacakrame
nirjagāmacadeve śaḥpārvatyāsahaśaṃkaraḥ
udyānaṃdarśayāmāsadevyādevaḥ pinākadhṛk
vijñāṣayativyajijñapat
prajvālanānādrumagulmaśobhitaṃlatāpratānāvanataṃmanoramam
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥsugaṃdhitaṃ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṃ ṭakibhiśvaketakaiḥ
aśokapuṃnāgavanaiḥ supuṣpitairdvi rephamālākulasaṃcayaiḥkvacit
kvacitpraphullāṃbujareṇubhūṣitairvihaṃgamaiśvāruphalapraṇādibhiḥ
kvacicca kāraṃḍavarā vanāditaṃkvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtam
mahākalābhiśraṃmarāṃganābhirniṣevitaṃcārusugaṃdhipuṣpitam
pragītavidyādharacāraṇaṃcapravṛttanṛtyānugatāpsarogaṇam
prahṛṣṭanā nāvidhapakṣisevitaṃpramattahārītakulopamoditam
mṭageṃdranānākulamānasaiḥ kvacit gajaiḥ kvaciddaddhakadaṃba kaṃmṭagaiḥ
praphu lanānāvidhacārupaṃkajaiḥ sarastaḍāgairupaśobhitaṃkvacit
niviḍaniculanīlaṃnīlakaṃṭhābhivāsaṃmadamuditavihaṃga bātanādābhirāmam
kusumitataruśākhālīnamattadvirephenava kisalayaśākhāśobhitaṃprāṃtaśākham
kvacicca daṃtakṣa tacāruvīrudhaṃkvacillatāliṃgita cāruvakṣam
kvacidviśālālasagāminībhirniṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṃganābhiḥ
pārāvatadhvaninikūjitacāruśṛṃgairakarṣaiḥ sitamanohara cārurūpaiḥ
nīlaiḥpuṣpastabakataralaprāṃtaśākhairaśokairmattālitrātagītaśrutisukhajanakairbhā sitāṃtaṃmanojñaiḥ
haṃsānāṃpakṣavātapracalita kamalasvaccha vistīrṇa toyaṃ toyānāṃtīrajātapravikaca kadalīvāṭa nṛtyanmayūraṃ
māyūraiḥ pakṣa caṃdraiḥkvacidapipatitairaṃjitaṃkṣmāpradeśaṃdeśedeśe muditavilasanmattahārītanṛtyaṃ
kṛṣṇābhiḥkvacidapikiṃnarāṃganābhiḥkṣīrābhiḥ samadhupa pītavṛkṣakhaṃḍam
saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacidupa liptakarṇapuṣpairāvāsaiḥ parivatapādapaṃ munīnām
āśrāṃtotpalanicitaiḥ kvacidviśālaiḥ svīkartuṃ saralamahīruhairupetam
phullapriyaṃgutarumaṃjarisaktabhṛṃgaṃbhṛṃgāvalīsarali tārdhakadaṃbapuṣpam
gulmāṃtara prasṛtatīramṭa gīsamūhaṃvallīlatātanubhṛtāmapavargadaṃtam
caṃdrāṃśujāladhavalaistilakairmanojñaiḥ siṃdūra kuṃkuṃmakusuṃbhanibhairaśākaiḥ
cāmīkarapratisumairnava karṇikāraiḥ phullāraviṃdapadaci traviśālaśākhaiḥ
kvacitsakāśaiḥśobhāṭyaiḥ puṣpairācitabhūtalaṃ
puṃnāgeṣuddijagaṇavirutaṃraktāśokastaba kataralitaṃ
sakalabhuvana kartālokanāthastadānīṃtuhina śikhara saṃvāsyardhaniṣṭhairgaṇeśaiḥ
vividhataruviśālaṃmattadṛṣṭānyapuṣṭairupavanataruramyaṃdarśayāmā sadevyāḥ
udyānaṃdarśitaṃdevaśobhayāparayāyutaṃ
sadāvārāṇasīmama
sarveṣāmeva jaṃtūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā
asmisiddhāḥ sadādevi madīyaṃtratamāśritāḥ
nānā liṃgadharānityaṃmamalokābhikāṃkṣiṇaḥ
abhyasyaṃtiparaṃyogaṃyuktātmānojiteṃdriyāḥ
nānāvasasamākīrṇe nānāvi hagarājite
kamalotpalapuṣpādyaiḥsarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte
apsarogaṇagaṃdharvaiḥ sadāsaṃśobhiteśubhe
rocate mesadā vāsoyena kāryeṇatacchṛṇu
yathāmokṣamihāpnoti anyathānatathākvaciṃ
brahmādayovijānaṃtiyecasiddhāmumukṣavaḥ
nātaḥ priyataraṃkṣetraṃ tasmānme harate manaḥ
mahākṣetramidaṃtasmādavimuktamitismṛtaṃ
saṃha
mattāḥdṛṣṭāśvānyapuṣṭāḥ kokilāyatra
devyāḥ devyai
prayāgādapitīrthāgryādidameva mahatsmṛtaṃ
jaigīṣavyaḥ satasiddhiyogataḥ sa mahātapāḥ
asyakṣetrasya māhātmyaṃta dvaktyāmamabhāvanāt
jaigīṣavyomahāśreṣṭhoyogināṃjñānamicchati
dhyāyatetyatra māṃnityaṃ yogānnirvāpyatebhṛśaṃ kaivalyaṃ paramaṃyā tidevānāmapi durlabhaṃ
ātmanaścaiva sāyujya mīpsitaṃsthānamevaca
kuveraḥsa mahāyakṣastathāsarvārpitatriyaḥ
kṣetrasya vaṃdanādevagaṇeśatvamavāpaha
parāśarasutoyogīṛṣirvyāsomahātapāḥ
brahmācaṛṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ viṣṇurvāyurdivākaraḥ
upāsanemahātmānaḥ sarveṣāmihasuvrate
anyecayoginaḥ siddhāśchannarūpāma hāvratāḥ
alaṃkārapurīmenāṃmatprasādādavāpsyasi
tenaivaṃ pūrvataḥ kṛtvā caturvarṇasamākulāṃ
sphītāṃjanapadākīrṇābhūtvāca vasatiṃ naraḥ
tataḥ prabhṛticārvagiyeyekṣetranivāsinaḥ
gṛhiṇāliṃginovāpimadbhaktāmatparāyaṇāḥ
matprasādāgamiṣyaṃtimo kṣaṃparamadurlabhaṃ
ihakṣetremṭataḥsopisaṃsārenapunarviśet
yepunarvimamādhīrāḥ satvasthāvijiteṃdriyāḥ
vratinaśvanirāvasthāḥ sarvathāma vibhāvitāḥ
dehabhaṃgaṃsamāsādyadhīmaṃtaḥsaṃgavarjitāḥ
gatāeva paraṃmokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvratāḥ
janmāṃtarasahasreṣuyuṃ janyogīsamāpnuyāt
etadeva paraṃjñānaṃetadevaparaṃśivam
vārāṇasītubhuvanatrayasārabhūtā ramyāpurīma masadāgirirājaputri
atrāgatāvividhaduṣkṛtakāriṇopipāpakṣayāddirajasaḥ pratibhāṃtimartyāḥ
yasminṭatāstanubhṛtaḥ padamāpnuvaṃtimūrkhāgamenarahi tānahisaṃśayotra
etasminnaṃ taredevādevīṃprāhagirīṃdrajāṃ
dātuṃ prasādaṃyakṣāyavarabhaktāyabhā vitaṃ
jagāmayakṣoyatrāstekṛśodhamanisaṃtataḥ
taṃdṛṣṭvā praṇataṃ bhaktyā harikeśaṃvṛṣadhvajaḥ
divyaṃ cakṣuradāttasmaiyenāpaśyataśaṃkaram
apaśyatsagaṇaṃ devaṃvṛṣayuktamumāpatim
sāmagryaṃcaśarīrasya yāhimāṃviga tajvaraḥ
ataḥ salabdhvātuvaraṃśarīreṇākṣatenatu
pādayoḥ praṇatastasthauddhatvāśirasi cāṃjalim
uvācāthatathācainaṃvara dosmīticoditaḥ
yadāyenatvāmitiśeṣaḥ
udbhūmasaṃbhramaukarmaṇī
ityekacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃ annadatvaṃcalokānāṃgāṇapatyaṃtathā'kṣayam
avimuktevane sthānaṃ paśyeyaṃsarvadāyadā
bhaviṣyasi gaṇādhyakṣovaradaḥ sarva pūjitaḥ
jeyaśvāpisarveṣāṃyogaiśvaryasamanvitaḥ
annadaścāpi lokebhyaḥ kṣetrapālobhaviṣyasi
tryakṣaśvadaṃḍapāṇiśvamahāyogītathaivaca
evaṃcabhagavāṃstatrayakṣaṃ kṛtvā gaṇeśvaram
jagāmavāsadeveśo rudrāvāsaṃsureśvaraḥ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃdaṃḍapāṇivarapradāne ekacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
āśvaryatatrayadvṛttaṃpaṃcāyatanamuttamam
purākalpedvijaśreṣṭhatadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu
caratetatramaṃḍūkī paṃcāyatanamuttamam
paṃcatvamāgatābrahman kālena kaṃtināṃjasā
jātisma ratvaṃ saṃprāptārājñaḥ sumanasogṛhe
yauvanaṃtuyadāyātātadārājāsavismayaḥ
dātukāmastadārājātayācavinivāritaḥ
vairāgyaṃmanasāgatvāvārāṇasyāmupāgatā
oṃkāraṃdṛṣṭavāndevaṃpaṃcāyatanavāsinam
maṃḍukīcāpitatraiva siddhicaivamupāgatā
āsītpratāpa mukuṭorājāparamadhārmikaḥ
kālenagacchatāśaśvadrājāputraṃ tamuktavān
dārasaṃgrahaṇaṃ putratva yākāryaṃcaśāśvatam
mayānaśakyate kartuṃ tavājñāparipālanam
rājovāca
mā nimajjīḥ kulaṃ matyaṃnarakesatataṃkṣaṇāt
sahitaṃpiturādeśaṃ śrutvānṛpasutobalī
prāhasaṃsmṛtyapaurāṇīṃ saṃsārasyavici tratām
śṛṇutāta va comatyaṃtatvavākyaṃ sahetukam
mayājanmasahasrāṇi jarāmṛtyuśatānica
prāptānidārasaṃyoga viyogānicasarvaśaḥ
tṛṇagulmalatāvallīsarīsṛpammṛgadvijāḥ
paśustrīpuruṣāyāniprāptānigatayomayā
gaṇāḥkiṃnaragaṃdharva bidyādhara mahoragāḥ
yakṣagutyakarakṣāṃsidānavāpsarasastathā
tatreśvareśvaratvaṃ ca prāpnaṃtātapunaḥ punaḥ
sṛṣṭastu bahuśaḥ sṛṣṭau saṃhāre cāpisaṃhṛtaḥ
dārasaṃyogayuktasyajātācaiva viḍaṃbanā
hrākṣarastubhavenmṛtyurasa raṃbrahmaśāśvatam
tarkyamānau bhūtāniyojayetāmasaṃśayaṃ
bhittvāśarīraṃ bhūtānāmahiṃsāṃprati padyate
labdhvāvāpṛthivīṃ sarvāṃsahasthāvarajaṃgamām
mevaniśvinuyāditiśeṣaḥ
tathācābhimānābhāvavatovaiṣayikasukhābhāvādviṣayārjanaṃvyarthamitibhāvaḥ
kāmātmānamiti
kāmenaviṣayecchayākarmaṇā śārīreṇananudhyānena kurvatītiśeṣaḥ amṛto dravyetu mamatāyasya mṛtyorvaśyesavartate
vīkṣāṃtarāṇāṃśatrūṇāṃ svabhāvāyasyame matiḥ
kāmātmānaṃpraśaṃsaṃtilokekāmātmanojanāḥ
tīrthānivedādhyayanaṃ kācidastipravartanā
kecittapa śvakāmenakarmaṇāvāmṭatotsukaḥ
tatohaṃkāmayenityaṃpaṃcāyatanamīśvaraṃ
avimuktesthitadevaṃ oṃ kāraṃ paramaṃ padaṃ
kathayāmisamāsenatīrthamāhātmyamu ttamaṃ
atītyajanmānibaḍūnitāta bhūdevagaṃdharva mahoragāṇāṃ
vidyādharāṇāṃkhagakinnarāṇāṃ jātosmyahaṃ vai śyakulevi śuddhe
tatomamābhūdacalācabhaktiḥ śarveśiveśaṃkaretripuraghne
vratopavāsairvividhaiḥ stavaiśvasaṃtoṣitaḥ śūlaśitāstradhārī
evaṃhisumahatkālaṃbhramatastīrthakāraṇāt
oṃkāraṃdṛṣṭavāṃstatrapaṃcā yatanavāsinaṃ
rudrāvāsakṛtasthānaṃdevadevasyacāgrataḥ
rātrijāgaraṇaṃtatra vaiśākhecakṛtaṃmayā
tatsarvaṃ camayādṛṣṭaṃ devagaṃdharvakiṃnaraiḥ
tenaiva karmaṇājātobhavatohaṃ gṛheśubhe
tatrayāsyāmyahaṃ śīghraṃracitoyaṃmayāṃjaliḥ
oṃkā reśvaradevasyaprasādenamayāpitaḥ
prādurbhūtaṃmahājñānaṃdurlabhaṃyatsurairapi
saṃsārecaprapaśyāmi ātmānaṃprakṛteḥ param
oṃkāraṃniṣkalaṃbrahmapaṃcāyatanavāsinam
drakṣyāmiśaṃkaraṃ devaṃ yaṃ dṛṣṭvāno dbhavaḥ punaḥ
rājovāca
jātismaratvaṃ saṃprāpyau dvignamānasoyahaṃ
saṃsārecasadāpuṃsāṃvairāgyaṃjāyatepunaḥ
priyāpriyāṇi sarvāṇinirmamonirahaṃkṛtiḥ
tyaktakarmāṇisarvāṇi ātmaśuddhānidhārayet
kṛtvāpi kṣetrasaṃnyāsamavimuktamupāsakāḥ
śāṃtādāṃtā jitakrodhāstitikṣāparamāyudhāḥ
ātmanyātmānamādhāya oṃkāreśvara sarvagaṃ
sarvabhūteṣucātmānaṃ paśyaṃtivijiteṃ dviyāḥ
sadbhāvabhāvitāḥ sarveja paṃtiśatarudriyaṃ
viśaṃtiparamaṃdeva moṃkāraṃparamaṃpadaṃ
evamuktastadārājāoṃkāraṃmanasāsmaran
rājyebhiṣecayāmāsaputraṃ caiva kanīyasaṃ
saṃsmaranpūrvaca ritaṃtatonirvedamāgataḥ praṇamyamanasādevaṃ paṃcāyatanavāsinaṃ
oṃkāraṃ paramaṃtrahmavārāṇasyāmupāgataṃ
pradakṣiṇāṃprakurute oṃkāradevamīśvaraṃ
stuvaṃśvaparamaṃ deva moṃkāraṃcastavenataṃ
arādhayaṃtaudeveśaṃpaṃcāyatanamīśvaraṃ
stuvaṃtaupara maṃdeva moṃkāraṃ parameśvaraṃ
vyāsauvāca
kīdṛśaṃcavartanābhyāṃkṛrtadeva syaśūlinaḥ
yasyacoccāramātreṇa ātmāsaṃprakaṭībhavet
śṭaṇuvyāsaparaṃgulyaṃ rahasya yogamuttamaṃ
oṃkārajaṃśivapadama nādimajamavyayaṃ
svayaṃbhuvamanirdeśyaṃ kāraṇaṃ paramaṃ vibhuṃ
paṃcadaivatamoṃkāraṃ
ācāreṇavajita māmakāmatvāt
nirvāṇamokṣaeva nirbhayaṃnirmalaṃnityaṃnirapekṣamanāśrayam
namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ viśuddhaṃjñānanirmalam
śivaṃsarvātmakaṃ sūkṣmamanādipaṃcadaivatam
ātmādhikopaviṣayaṃstutamācāravarjitam
śabdāvakāśarahitaṃbahmanirvāṇakevalam
śaṃkāviśeṣanirmuktaṃ vidyāpatitamocanam
niṣkramyacātmanātmānaṃprakaṭaṃjñānadīpakam
nityāvakāśarahitaṃśabdāśabdādyago caram
sakṛdvistīrṇavipulaṃ devadevaṃ surātmakam
anispaṃdaṃmahātmānaṃnirānaṃdāvalokanam
svabhāvaṃbhāvanāgrātyaṃbhāvātītaṃsulakṣaṇam
vākyāpavādarahitaṃniṣprapaṃcātmakaṃśivam
jñānajñeyāvalokasya hetuṃ paramakāraṇaṃ
anāhataṃ sarvagataṃśabdādiguṇasaṃbhavam
śabdabrahmagataṃśāṃtaṃśabdaśabdāṃta māspadam
anādimacyutaṃdivyaṃ pramāṇātītagocaram
adhaśvordhvagataṃnityaṃ jīvākhyaṃhetusaṃ sthitam
hṛdādidvādaśāṃtasthaṃ prāṇāpānodayāṣṭakam
agrāvyamidriyātmānaṃ niṣkalaṃkātmakaṃ vibhum
svarādivyaṃjanātītaṃvarṇādiparivarjitam
vācāmavācyaviṣayaṃ oṃkārādūrdhvarūpiṇaṃ
niḥśabdaniścalaṃ saumyadehātītaṃ parātparaṃ
bhūtāvagā harahitaṃniḥśabdamekadhāsthitam
aciṃtyaṃ paramaṃsūkṣmaṃpaṃcataṃtrādisaṃvṛtam
aprameyamanaṃtākṣaṃ asayaṃkāmarūpiṇam
prabhavaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃbījāṃkurasamudbhavam
vyāpakaṃsarvakāmākhyamakṣaraṃ paramaṃ mahat
sthūlasūkṣmavibhāgasyaṃvya ktāvyaktaṃsanātanam
mahābhūtaṃ mahākāyaṃ śivaṃ nirvāṇa bhairavam
śaraṇyaṃdevamīśāna moṃkāraṃśivarūpiṇam
devadevaṃ mahādevaṃ paṃcava kaṃṭaṣadhvajam
sadāśivaṃ virūpākṣaṃśūlahastaṃ jaṭādharam
vārāṇasyāṃsthitaṃdeva moṃkāraṃ paramaṃ padam
bhāva kaṃsarvajaṃtūnāṃnamasyāminamo namaḥ
vanhibhāskarasaṃkāśaṃsūryakoṭisamaprabham
stotrāṃta tvatra saṃjātesarājāsastutastadā
ekadauṃkāranirdiṣṭastotraṃśaṃbhoḥ paṭhiṣyati
avimuktemahākṣetre sarvātma nābhisaṃskṛtaḥ
brāhmaṇaḥkṣatriyovaiśyaḥśūdropiya divāpaṭhet
vedāhametaṃ puruṣaṃmahāṃta mādityavarṇatamasaḥ parastāt
tameva viditvānabhavenmṛtyurnānyaḥ paṃthāvidyatehijanānāṃ
tadācoṃkāradevasyaśakyaṃ māhātmyamīrituṃ
itīritaṃtetumayāsamastaṃ māhātmyamoṃkārahataikadeśaṃ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāmoṃkāreśvaravarṇanaṃ nāmadvicatvāriṃśodhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
natṛbhimadhigacchā mioṃkārasyakathāṃparāṃ
śṭaṇuvyāsa kathāṃdivyāṃpaurāṇīṃ vedasaṃmitāṃ
śaṃbhogirimutādevībhāryākālītiviśrutā
tyarthadayitāsādhvīśīlavṛttaguṇānvitā
sadā nitya kriyārthacasopāsteśaṃkarovaśī
saṃdhyāpūrvāpaścimāṃcaoṃkāre saṃsthitoharaḥ
nṛtyamānāḥsthitāḥ sarve gītavāditrasaṃvṛtāḥ
śatavarṣasahasreṇa svedabhūtāgaṇāstathā
pre tabhūtāstathādevātsṛṣṭānanṛturuttamaṃ
tattadvāsaśvamuṃcatiśvalaṃta śvapadepade
taṃtādṛśamathodṛṣṭvā gaurīvacanamabravīt
kiṃvirūpākṣannṛtyoyaṃmamavismayakārakaḥ
anekairbahubhiḥ sthānairdṛṣṭaṃ nṛtyaṃmayāpurā
kailāsenaivasaṃdṛṣṭaṃkadācittumayāpurā
kāraṇaṃkathaṃ yatvadya yadyanugrahabhāgaÉ
asminsthāne oṃkārāyatane
udyamyapāṇinādevaḥ svaṃ gulena mahā tmanā
viśiṣṭaṃkāraṇaṃ metrasthāne girisute śṛṇu
yosauparāvarodevaḥ sākṣikaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
etadatrāyaṃtrahmapaṃcāsyaṃ saṃsthitaṃprabhuṃ
paṃcapaṃcasthi paṃcāyatanavāsinaṃ
tenanṛtyāmyahaṃdeviparamānaṃdamāsthitaḥ
brahmāṃḍodaravartīnitīrthānigiriśodbhave
teṣā matyadhikaṃsthānaṃpaṃcāyatanamuttamaṃ
mamacāpyadhikāprītiryena kāryeṇatacchṛṇu
soyaṃsthāne paredevimaṃtavyonātra saṃśayaḥ
pratyakṣaṃjñātavān bhadrepuruṣasyacaturbhujaḥ

dra kṣyaṃtimānavāḥ pūrvapaṃcāyatanasaṃsthitāḥ
śivalokasya saṃcāraṃ paṃcāyataṃnasaṃsthitaṃ
rahasyaṃ sarvajaṃtūnāṃpaṃcāyatanamutta maṃ
narāṇāmanyabuddhīnāṃviṣayākrāṃtacetasāṃ
aṃtarbhūtaṃtusaṃsthānaṃveda śāstrabahiṣkṛtāḥ
śāṃtādāṃtājitakrodhāḥpaṃcāyatanapūjayā
sadbhāvabhāvitāḥ sarve drakṣyaṃtiparameśvaram
yaistu janmāṃtare devi purāārādhitotyahaṃ
tevidaṃtiparaṃ sthānaṃ avimuktaṃ paraṃ padaṃ
brahmāṃḍodaramadhyecayānitīrthānisuvrate
vārāṇasyāṃgamiṣyaṃtivaiśākhasyacaturdaśīṃ
drakṣaṃtiparamaṃ devaṃ paṃcāyatanavāsinaṃ
pūjayāśamadamādisādhanasaṃpannābhavatītyāha
oṃoṃnamaḥ devāśca ṛṣayaścaiva rudrāḥ pāśupatāśvaye
parivāryasthitāḥ sarve oṃkāreśaṃtu suvrate
yasminakṣetresvayaṃbhūśrvasthitaḥ pūrveṇa keśavaḥ
rudrāṇāṃ caiva koṭistu kāśīpuryeva saṃsthitā
dhyāyamānā caoṃkārasthitātasyaivadakṣiṇe
vāmadevaścasāvarṇiraghoraḥ kapilaḥ pare
dhyāyamānāstuoṃkāraṃ paṃcāyatanavāsinaṃ
saptakoṭyastu maṃtrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tapasādhikaḥ
evaṃ rakṣaṃ titatsthānaṃ madīyaṃśāśvataṃ śubham
eśyo rakṣaṃtisatataṃpaṃcāyatanavāsinaṃ
oṃkāradarśanādeva gatiṃprāpnotidurlabhām
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumā rasaṃhitāyāṃoṃkāranirṇayonāmatrayaścatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
asminsthāne purāvṛttaṃ tadi haikamanāḥ śṛṇu
rathaṃtarepurākalpe rājāsītpuṣpavāhanaḥ
nāmnā lokeṣuvikhyātastejasāsūryasannibhaḥ
tapasātasya tuṣṭena de vadevenaśaṃbhunā
kamalaṃ kāṃcanaṃdattaṃ yathākāmagamaṃmune
īpānisuralokaṃ cayatheṣṭaṃvicaransadā
kalpādau saptadvī peṣutasya puṣkaravāsinaḥ
tasyanāśnātutaddī paṃpuṣkaradvīpa mucyate
puṣpavāhanamityāhustasmāttaṃdevadānavāḥ
patnīcatasyāpratimānarūpānārīsahasrairabhitobhimānyā
በ nāmnācalāvaṇyavatībabhūva sāpārvatīceṣṭatamābhavasya
tasyātmajānāmayutaṃvabhūva dharmātmanāmagyadhanurdharāṇām
sopyāgataṃvīkṣya munipravīraṃ pracetasaṃvākyamidaṃ babhāṣe
kasmā dvibhūtira malāca mamādyapūjājātāca sarvaviditāmamasuṃdarīyam
bhāryāma mālpatapasaiva sutoṣitena dattaṃma māṃbujagṛhaṃcasu dhīradhātrā
yasminpraviṣṭamapikoṭiśataṃnṛpāṇāṃsāmātya kuṃjarasthauvadhanāvatānām
munirapyavocatabhavāṃtaritāṃpṛthivīpatenanu niśamyaka thāṃ
abhūdanāvṛṣṭiratīva raudrākadācidāhāramaviṃdatā
kṣutpīḍitenabhramatāna kiṃcidāsāditaṃvanya phalādisadyaḥ
athābhyapaśyanmahadaṃbujāḍhyaṃ sarovaraṃ paṃkaparītarodhaḥ
tanmūlyalābhāyapuraṃsa mastaṃbhrāṃtaṃtadā'śeṣamabhūttadānīm
upaviṣṭastvamekasminsabhāryā bhavatāṃ'gaṇe
rudrāvāsetu saṃsthāyatvayārātraumahāśrutiḥ
tatradṛṣṭastvayā devo divyāśvarya vibhūtimān
oṃ kāra paramaṃ bahmadevagaṃdharva kiṃnaraiḥ
dhyāyamānaḥ paraṃbrahmaoṃkārākhyaṃ tuīśvaram
tvayādyāvagataṃsarvapaṃcāyatanadarśanāt
bhaktiścaiva tadā jātāsāpatyasya nareśvara
kimebhiḥ kamalaiḥ kāryavaraṃśaṃsuralaṃ kṛtaḥ
niveditāstathāpuṣpāḥpaṃcāyatanavāsine
dīyamānaṃcadevāya suvarṇasyaśataṃ param
nagṛhītaṃtataḥ kṣetre mahāsa tvamahātmanā
prabhātecatvayātasmindṛṣṭaḥ śaṃsuryadṛcchayā
āścaryaṃ paramaṃmatvātasminnāyatanesthitaḥ
karmaṇātenarājeṃdraiyaṃ vyuṣṭistavā gatā
sabhavānlubdhakojātaḥsapatnīkonareśvaraḥ
puṣpānukalpanāttasmācchaṃkarasya capūjanāt
iyaṃ vyuṣṭista thājātāpaṃcāyatanapūjanāt
oṃkāreśvara māhātmyādalpenatapasānṛpa
saṃ tuṣṭastavarājeṃdrabrahmarūpīca īśvaraḥ
tasmādrakṣaskharājeṃdrapuṣkaratvaṃmahītale
avimuktaṃsamāsādya kārraśaraṇaṃtraja
prasādāttasyadevasyadraṣṭāsi padamīśvaram
ityuktaḥ saturājāvaitenaivatumaharṣiṇā
romāṃca sarvagātrastuharpā viṣṭastamabravīt
janmāṃtaraṃtvayākhyātaṃtrahmaṇāṃ kulavardhana
saṃsāretvatsa maiḥsaṃgaḥpuṇyabhārāttujāyate
evaṃprasādyataṃ vipraṃrājātukṛtaniścayaḥ
sapatnīko jagāmāśuvārāṇasyāṃmahāmune
śaṃbhoḥpriyatamedeśepaṃcāyatana mukkiṃde
dakṣiṇāṃmūrtimāsthāya oṃ kārastatra saṃsthitaḥ
durlabhaṃ caparasthānaṃ mānuṣairakṛtātmabhiḥ
akṛtātmabhirakṛtasukṛtasaṃbhāraiḥ
rudrāvāsetivikhyātaṃpuṇyadaṃ sarvadehinām
rudrāvāse kṛtasnānaḥpaṃcāyatanavā sinam
drakṣyāmiīśvaraṃdevaṃ yaṃ dṛṣṭavānodbhavaḥpunaḥ
kalikalmaṣabhūtaistu yeṣāṃ nopagatāmatiḥ teṣāṃdṛśyaṃcagamyaṃcatatsthānaṃśaśimaulinaḥ
tīrthaṃ casthāpitaṃvyā tradaityadānavanāyakaiḥ
aṃtardhyānaśatairnityaṃ pūjyate parameśvaraḥ
tatra gatvāturājarṣiḥ paramaṃ bhāvamāsthitaḥ
ārā dhayānodeveśaṃpaṃcāyatanamīśvaram
śāṃtākāraṃvinirnatyajñānadīpenaīśvaram
dṛṣṭvāvāsaturājarṣiḥ oṃkāraṃ paramaṃ padaṃ
tenavyāptamidaṃviśvaṃgirevaparamātmanā
vārāṇasyāṃtuoṃ kāraṃpaṃcāyatanasaṃsthitam
yaddarśanānnarāloke vijñānaiśvaryabhājanāḥ
dānānāṃ durlabhaṃ dānaṃ vratānāṃdurlabhaṃ param
sarvatradurlabhaṃsthānaṃityāha bhagavānśivaḥ
bha ktyāparamayā yuktāmahādevaṃviśaṃtica
pūjayiṣyaṃtiyetatra sarvabhāvenaśaṃkaram
vijñeyāste gaṇābhadre mānuṣī prakṛti sthitāḥ
vārāṇasyāṃtu ye kecittīrthānyāyatanānica
teṣāṃcaivatu sarveṣāmoṃkāraṃprathamaṃsmṛtam
oṃkāradarśanāddevi sarvedṛṣṭānasaṃśayaḥ
uvācadevi paśyedamudyānaṃnirmitaṃ purā
sahadevyātatovyāsavārāṇasyāṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ
devodyānaṃhididṛkṣurbhagavāṃstatsamaṃtataḥ
pūrvasmiṃstvasi gebhāgedevodevyāḥ parātparaḥ
udyānaṃdarśayāmāsanānākinnaranāditam
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇanānāku sumaśobhitam
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇanānāpakṣivināditam
caṃpakāśokapuṃnāgapriyaṃguśatasaṃkulam
saṃyuktaṃ sarvataḥ śrīmaddanaṃtadrājasaṃnibham
satadudyānamāsādyadevīṃ prāhajagatpatiḥ
paśyadevivimānasthākinnarāṃ śramanorame
pārijātakakhaṃḍānitathākalpadrumāṇica
mamalokecayevṛkṣāviṣṇulokecayeśubhe
iyaṃ vārāṇasīdevīśivalokaṃsamāśritā
tiṣṭhate sarva lokeśobrahmākamalasaṃbhavaḥ
parivāryasthitāḥ sarvāoṃkāraṃcādimuktidam
ūrdhvaṃ golokasaṃsthānaṃgavāṃghāsaḥsvayaṃbhuvaiḥ
gavayatrasaṃvarṇānāṃpayomūrdhnisamāpatat
tatomayordhvato dṛṣṭāgāvastāḥ somapānugāḥ
tatastāvīkṣitāstatra bhītāmāvastadābhavan
tejasāmamanirdagdhānaikavarṇāmṛpāditāḥ
gāvaḥ pūrvamimādevi āsa nūkapilavaṃśajāḥ
naikavarṇāstathābhūtāyadetāprekṣitāmayā

prasādayitvātāgāvobrahmāmāmabravīttataḥ

goprekṣakeśvaraṃ gatvādṛṣṭvācābhyarcyamānavaḥ
tatastāvī kṣyamāṇāstuprasanne suvratemayi
nhadesiṃcitumārebheśāṃtāḥsthiracarāstataḥ
yathābhaktāhitāḥsarvābrahmaṇāpi mahātmanā
dhanyāḥpūjyāścamānyāścabhaviṣyathamamājñayā

atrāpi svayamevāhaṃ vṛpadhvajaitismṛtaḥ
sāṃnidhyaṃkṛtavāndevi satāṃ vaidṛśyatāṃgataḥ
kapilākadavikhyātaṃ devānāmapi durlabhaṃ

āsāṃkṣīreṇa saṃ jātaṃ idametanmanoharam

evaṃdevitatoviṣṇu brahmālokapitāmahaḥ
aśakyāsāgatistasyayogināṃcaivaśāśvatī
asminnapisthitādaityāḥsarvetedeva kaṃṭakāḥ
vyāghrarūpaṃsamāsthāyanirdagdhāstejasāmayā
vyāghreśvarastataḥ khyāto nityaṃtatrāhamāsthitaḥ
napunardurgatiṃyāṃtidṛṣṭvemaṃvyāghramīśvaram

ādāvatrāhamāsāgraprasthitogaṇapaiḥ saha
jyeṣṭhasthānamidaṃtasmādeta nmepuṇyadarśanam
dṛṣṭvā tadamalaṃliṃgaṃjyeṣṭhasthānesamāsthitam
āsamaṃtāttudeveśiliṃgānisthāpitānica
dṛṣṭvātanniyatāmayadeihabhedguṇobhavet
mahādeveti tesarvedhyāyamānāḥ surottamāḥ
vārāṇasyāṃta todevidevānāṃmānitobhavaṃ
kṣetraṃ vārāṇasī puṇyāmuktidāsābhaviṣyati
avimukteśvaraṃmāṃvaiyotradrakṣyati mānavaḥ
prāṇā nihatusaṃnyasyayāsyaṃtigatimuttamāṃ
mamapriyamidaṃsthānaṃjñātvāliṃgaṃprati ṣṭhitaṃ
śaileśvaramitikhyātaṃ dṛśyatāmidamāsthitaṃ
dṛṣṭvaivaśailajaṃdevimamalokamavāpnuyāt
purāvārāṇasī ceyaṃ puṇyabhāgāpramodinī
kṣetrāgatamalaṃkṛtyajānhavyā sahasaṃgatā
varaṇānāmatatraiva gaṃgāsiśvasaridvarā
sthāpi taṃsaṃgametābhyāṃbrahmaṇāliṃgamuttamaṃ
saṃgameśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvaivastrātvācamanujaḥśu triḥ
arcayetsaṃgameśānaṃtasyajanmagataṃpunaḥ

daṇḍeti

namaste'paśave nityaṃ kṣetrajñāyaviṭāyaca

pulahāyapulastyāyakatvāvhānāyatāpine
bhūtāya bhūtanāthāya kūṣmāṃḍapatayenamaḥ
avaśyāyāpyavadhyāya ajarāyāmarāyaca
akṣayāyāvyayāyaivatathā'pratihatāyaca
anāthasyāya sarveṣāṃ tathaiva puṇyarūpiṇe
sūkṣmebhyaśvātisūkṣmāya sarvagā yamahātmane

icchāmyahaṃ viśvanāthasaṃsārādvinivartanaṃ
draṣṭumicchāmi yogena eṣa me dīyatāṃvaraḥ

anyāṃgatiṃnapaśyāmipaśyāmyātyaṃtikaṃsukhaṃ

pratīcchamāṃmahādeva epamedīyatāṃvaraḥ
yaidaṃprātarutthāyapaṭhedavimanānaraḥ
caturdaśyāṃviśeṣeṇabrāhmaṇovāyatistathā
yastvimaṃśṛṇuyānnityaṃ śrāvayedvādvijottamaḥ
mahīyate pūjāṃlabhate
itipaṃcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya nandīśaghoratapasāsaṃ so'śvamedhaphalaṃprāpyarudraloke mahīyate
śrutvāsarudapityenaṃ stavaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam
eṣamaṃtrajapaścaiva saṃsāravinivartakaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃpaṃcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
aśrupūrṇakṣaṇaṃdīnaṃ pādayoḥ śirasānatam
karābhyāṃsaṃmukhābhyāṃtusaṃgṛtyabhuvane śvaraḥ
uvācajagatāṃnāthovacasātoṣayaṃśvatam
nirīkṣyagaṇapānsarvānma hādevo'vadatpunaḥ
akṣayaścā vyayaścaivasapitāsasuhṛjjanaḥ
ye catvāṃsaha saṃdṛṣṭāḥ snigdhabhāvaṃ gatāśvaye
mameṣṭogaṇapaścaivamadvīryomatparākramaḥ
iṣṭomamasadācaiva mamapārśvagataḥ sadā
madrūpa ścaiva bhavitāmahāyogabalānvi taḥ
ṛddhiyuktaṃsahaddīpaṃkṣīrodamamṛtākaram
kuśeśayamayīṃmālāṃsvayaṃbhūrā tmanaḥ śubhām
āvabandhamahādevānaṃ dinedevarūpiṇe
satayāmālayānandīya bhaukaṃṭhāvasaktayā
