kṛtvāśvāṃścaturovedānyetasminnayojayan
viṣṇuḥ pitāmahoniśvapraṇamyaparameśvaraṃ
rathaṃsajjamitiprāhurvināśāya suradviṣāṃ
tataḥ sabhagavāna śaṃbhuḥ stūyamānaḥsurā suraiḥ
adhaścordhvaṃ ca saṃprekṣyatvaśeṣabhuvaneśvaraḥ
devatāstharūpatāṃgatāḥ
pitāmahaṃtatovīkṣyaprovācavacasāṃpatim
dagdhavyaṃ tripuraṃyenatamipuṃśī dhamānaya
tataḥ provācataṃbrahmāpraṇamyaṭaṣabhadhvajam
tataḥpārśvasthitodṛṣṭvāśaṃbhurviṣṇu hutāśanī
dṛṣṭipātenataudavausamājhyadariṃdamau
dvau tāvaṃjalimādhāya sureśānamupasthitau
svayameva tataścakreśaṃbhurviṣṇuṃśarottamaṃ
oṣadhīnāṃpartisomaṃmukhetasyanyaḥ yojayat
śalyaṃcapāvakaṃcakre sabrahmāṇaṃtatobravīt
tamuvācatatobrahmā prāṃjalirjagatāṃpatim
matyaṃdadāsiyayājñāṃ svayameva hisārathiḥ
prāptakimadhikaṃdevasārathyāddhikaṃtataḥ
rudrasya pārṣadāyeva naṃdīśvarapuroga māḥ
śaṃkukarṇapurogāśvaye cacaṃḍeśvarādayaḥ
gaṇeśvarāmahāyogāruyakṣāḥ paṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ
nānāśastrapraharaṇānānā yuddhaviśāradāḥ
vādayaṃtastathāvādyaṃbherīśaṃkhakharānbahūn
ājagmurgaṇa mukhyāste sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
nānā vidhānāṃ puṣpāṇāmupariṣṭātsahasraśaḥ
nipeturdaṣṭayo mūrdhnidevadevasyaśūlinaḥ
aśaktābhāra muddoḍhuṃ mumuhurdevatābhṛśa
tatastāndevadeveśojñātvāyuktādivaukasaḥ
sahanīyaṃvapuścakresurāḥ sarvaividudruvuḥ
brahmāṇaṃsārathiṃ kṛtvāsvayamāyātiśaṃkaraḥ
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā satadādānavādhipaḥ
tārakākṣaṃ samāhūyavidyunmālinamevaca
tathānyānanujān bhṛtyāndānavopipuraḥsarān
nāradenayathākhyātaṃ sarva mākhyātavāṃstadā
tataḥ śrutvādaityarājastārakākhyobravīdidam
durbalaḥ kurute bhedaṃdānaṃ sāṃtvamathāpivā
pramāṇaṃyaśasaḥ saṃtovīryatubalinaḥ sadā
durbalasyariporṭa ḍobalināviji gīṣayā
kartavyāvikrameṇedaṃprāha śukrastathāguruḥ
jitvādaṃḍenatānsarvā nsthāsyāmonirvṛtāḥsukhaṃ
tārakākṣavacaḥ śrutvāvidyunmālī mahābalaḥ
saṃmānyatadatīveṣṭaṃrājño syavacanaṃ śubhaṃ
naśaktāyoddhumasmābhirdevatācalavarjitāḥ
tecedyotsyatisaṃmūḍhāḥ prayāsyaṃtitataḥ kṣayaṃ
anyonyaṃtuvayaṃ budhyāupā bhūtvāiṃdrobhavasiviśvakṛt
saptalokeśvaraṃtyayapaśyāmatvāṃpuraṃdaraṃ
hiraṇyakaśipuṃkṛtvā hiraṇyākṣaṃcadaityapaṃ
tataḥ śrutvāmayovyāsavidyunmālivibhāṣitaṃ
tairdevaiḥ sārdhamasmākaṃyuktaṃsāmādiyojanaṃ
yaeṣabhaga vānīśaḥ sarvabhūteśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
asmākaṃdevatānāṃcasraṣṭāhartācasaprabhuḥ
sahaṃtuṃsvayamāyātiupāyastasya kīdṛśaḥ
praṇāmaḥsaṃśrayaścaivaguṇopāyaiḥ kapardinaḥ
yadikārkaśyamāsthāyayodha yāmapinākinam
tasyājihmekṣaṇenaiva nihatāḥ sthatatāsurāḥ
brahmādyāḥ śaraṇaṃ saṃtamarditāyatiśāṃtaye
abhidhyānāt kṣaṇenaivapraṇaśyetabhavedapi
kīdṛśaṃtenayuddhaṃ nādevadevenaśaṃbhunā
kiṃtapoṣiviśuddhaṃnonaṣṭaṃkiyada naṃtaraṃ
bhavaṃtoloṣṭavobhūtvāgirikalpasamāśinaḥ
icchaṃtisahitāyoddhuṃkālapāśenacoditāḥ
ahaṃbhaktomahādevaṃ jānetasya canāṃtaraṃ
sapraṇāmaḥsvayaṃsyāsyenayo tsyeśaṃbhunāsaha
yadiyūyamapiprājñāmamaśuśrūṣavoyadi
mānudhvaṃśaṃbhunāyuddhaṃ gacchadhvaṃśaraṇaṃśivaṃ
tamevaṃvādinaṃ śrutvāviśvakarmāṇamūrjitam
nārado bhagavānāhadānavāṃtakaraṃ vacaḥ
sarvaṃyuktamidaṃ kiṃtu kāloyaṃnāsyasaṃprati
bhavatāṃtutapaḥkṣīṇamaiśvaryamuktamevaca
klīvatāmapikurvatoyūyaṃnaśpathadā navāḥ
vṛtaḥsarvāmaraiḥśaṃbhurvadhārthaibhavatāmiha
praṇatānapyasauyuṣmāṃstaspriyārthaihaniṣyati
kathaṃdanusutābhūtvārā jānobalagarvitāḥ
bhītāmṛtyuṃjigīṣadhvaṃrupaṇāivadānavāḥ
athaprāpsyathavidhvaṃsaṃdevadevena śūlinā
pramayeṃdrāstatoyūyaṃ bhavitāro nasaṃśayaḥ
śauryeṇa bhavatāṃtrī taḥkadācidvṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
kariṣyāmicarakṣāṃvaḥśastraghātanivāriṇīm
uttiṣṭhatadanoḥputrāvijayāyayuyutsayā
nāradasyavacaḥ śrutvātārakākṣomahābalaḥ
vidyunmālī ca daityeṃdrobāṇādyā śvamahāsurāḥ
kālenanoditāmūḍhāḥ kṣīṇapuṇyāgatāyuṣaḥ
mayopitadva cobudhvājñātvānāśamupasthitaṃ
nāradopitatotsṛṣṭorakṣāṃbadhvātumāyayā
yuyutsūnasurānkṛtvāyayauśrvarathaṃ prati
tatastedānavāḥ sarve yuddhāya kṛtaniścayāḥ
nānāpraharaṇopetābabhūvu yuddhalālasāḥ
tārakākṣocalobāṇovidyunmālīcadānavaḥ
dhāyaśivarathābhimukhamājagāmetisaṃkṣepaḥ
itiekapaṃcāśattamodhyāyaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya mayādidānaveṃdrā ṇāṃmaṃtraṇanāradenatu
avādyaṃtatataḥśaṃkhāstūryāṇi ca sahasraśaḥ
dānavānāṃbaleghorekātarāṇāṃbha yaprade
sarathaḥ sahasāyātiayaṃketuścadṛśyate
praharaṇavara hastāstadrathaṃvīkṣamāṇāḥ paśavaiva yathāgneranvagacchan samī pam
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyāṃ tripuropākhyāneekapaṃcāśattamo'dhyāyaḥ
tevīkṣya durgaṃtripuraṃ gaṇeśānaṃdīśvarādyāḥpramathāḥsapatnāḥ
nādaṃpracakruḥ sahitāḥ pravīrāyuyutsavodānava siṃhamukhyāḥ
caṃḍeśvaraścaṃḍavapurmahātmājvalatmadīpograkuṭhārapāṇiḥ
vyādāyava kaṃpurataḥ sthitobhūddevasyaśaṃbhoḥ pramatheṃ dravīraḥ
dīmaṃtriśūlaṃparigṛtyanaṃdīdhyakṣaḥ pratasthe haratulyadharmā
pārśvasthito bhūtsacaśaṃkukarṇaḥ pragṛtyadīptaṃmuśalaṃga ṇeṃdraḥ
bhṛṃgīmahātmāsacavīrabhadrastathāgaṇeṃdrāḥ śataśaḥ pravīrāḥ
vajjatriśūlāsigadaṣṭihastāḥ pratasthirete vijayāttaha stāḥ
samāgataṃtaṃrathamīkṣya daityāyuddhāyate jagmurupetamohāḥ
tetārakākṣapramukhāḥ suvīrāḥ saṃnatyanānāyudhadīptahastāḥ
tasyausahāsaṃkṛtavānsvanaṃ capaśyanaraṇaṃtagaṇa daityapānām
tataḥ sanaṃdīgaṇapaiḥ pravīrairacī karayuddhamahīnasattvaiḥ
vivyādhabhṛṃgīdaśabhiḥpṛṣatkairvidyutprabhaṃkopasaṃraktanetraḥ
bhṛṃgisamāsādyaśilāyudhāstenāśaknuva stasya rujaṃprakartum
vidyutprabhaṃbhṛṃgiriṭistato sauśūlenadīmenajaghānapṛṣṭhe
śitenaśūlena hatosyapūrṇa phūtkāra bhṛṃgīprayayaubhayārtaḥ
bhagna stadāsauditijādhipena bhṛṃgīsamutsṛjyagaṇeṃdramukhyān
vivyādhatīkṣṇairniśitaiḥ pṛṣatkairvināyakaṃsa nabhiraṃsadeśe
punastriṣaṣṭyādaśabhiśvabhūyo vidyutprabhastaṃ gajarājavatram
jaghāna marmasvavilakṣarūpaṃ tataśvakopāsyavināyakeṃdraḥ
sa puṣkarāgreṇa gajeṃdrasiṃhogrīvāṃtadādaityapatervipiṣya
utpāṭayāmāsaśiraḥśarīrātpadmaṃ yathānāgaiva dvipeṃdraḥ
daityasya kṛttaṃśuśubheśirastudaṃtāvaleṃdra pratibhāccharīrāt
mahotsavebhṛṃgava ropa gītaṃdra dātotkhātamivāśupadmaṃ
kruddhāvupāgamyacaśaṃkukarṇaśilīmukhairvivyadhaturgaṇeṃdram
tauśaṃkukarṇaḥ prasabhaṃnipātyachinnadhvajāśvauvirathaucakāra
taṃ jaghnatu naikavidhaiḥpṛṣatkairvajñābhighātapratimaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ
dī naha tvāmuśalena vīrausaṃpreṣayāmāsapuraṃyamasya
anyecadaityāstripurādhivāsāḥ kruddhāviniṣkramyagaṇeṃdramukhyaiḥ
nārāca vajjāsikuṭhārahastāghoraṃmahāyuddhamatīva cakruḥ
daityeśvarāstairharakalpa tulyai gaṇeśvaraiḥ prāmaśivaprasādaiḥ
praśraṣṭanānāyudhava vadhārāśchinnairbhujaiḥ śoṇitamuddamaṃtaḥ
vātyāhatāstetupa yodharāivapetuḥ samudregiriśṛṃgakalpāḥ
purādviniṣkramya satā rakākṣaḥ kruddhogaṇeṃdrasvayamabhyadhāvat
taṃśaṃkukarṇoditijādhikalpaṃjaghāna mūrddhiprasabhaṃgaṇeṃdraḥ
protthāyatūrṇa sahitāra kāsaḥ cikṣepatasmai gaṇapāyacakram
kruddhastataḥ sobhiha togaṇeṃdrastaṃtārakākṣaṃ satuśaṃkukarṇaḥ
nipatyamuṣṭyānijaghāna mūrdhnisamāhataḥ sopijagāmakṛcchraṃ
mumocaroṣaṃvirarājatīvraṃ mamāra paśvādasuraḥprasaktaḥ dṛṣṭvāvipannaṃditijādhipeṃ
tatomayastān rudato'sureśānāśvāsayanprāhava cosureṃdraḥ
sajīvaṃhiyathāpurāṇaṃma yaṃtraṇemuśvamuduḥśirobhiḥ
satārakākṣastata āśubhūyo yuyutsayāyuddhapathaṃ jagāma
ā yāṃtamālakṣya pitāmahastaṃ pūrvaṃ smṛtaṃjīvitamāśubhūyaḥ
provācavākyaṃ sasurāsureśaṃnivedayan vāma kareṇa daityam
hato pyayaṃśaṃkaratārakākṣaḥ kṛtoma yenāśusajīva eva
asyāstidevāmṛtamuttamaṃ hitenāsurān jīvayate sureṃdraḥ
devomahā nepasureṃdra kenamṛtāntān jīvayatesaढāsau
tatomṭataṃ tanmaya saṃsthamāśu prahāramātreṇaharāsyaśaṃbho
śrutvāvacasta syapitāmahasya prahāramātreṇajahārasayaḥ
tadāmṛtaṃtadgamitaṃtadāstu gṛhāṇadeveśaśirovyayastadā
pitāmahastatpunare vahṛṣṭaḥpinākinaṃprāhavacaḥpraṇamya
dṛṣṭaṃmayāyuddhamidaṃgaṇānāṃdaityādhipaiḥ sārdha mahīnasatvaiḥ
divyaṃ sahasraṃhigataṃsamā stamabhūtsureśa
saṃkalpamātrādapi nāśametidaityādhivāsaṃtripuraṃ tadeva
vijñaptaevaṃ caturānanenapralīḍhamālīḍhamanaṃgahaṃtā
kṛtvādha nustaddalavannikṛṣyaprāyojayaddīptamiṣupināke
saṃkalpamātreṇatadāsamānipurāṇidaityaiḥ sahitānitāni
cakrejaga tsṛṣṭivināśakartājagacca nippaṃdamabhūttadāśu
viśvātmakaṃpāvakasomapuṃkhaṃ trailokyasaṃhāramipuṃpradīptam
cikṣepa devastamiṣutayograṃkṣitvāca kaṣṭaṃdhigatīti cāha
'naṃdī samāgamyatataḥ sureśaṃprovācavākyaṃkimitipraṇamya
naṃdīśvarastaṃbhagavānuvācamayasyabhaktasyaśubhaṃcikīrṣuḥ
tathānalaṃsomaharaṃ cadeva śīghraṃsamāgacchanivārayasva
naṃdīpragṛ tyāthasureśvarājñāṃtūrṇayayauviśvakṛtaḥ puraṃtat
dṛṣṭvā mayaṃtatra sadānaveṃdramūrdhānatāṃgaṃvṛṣabhadhvajāya
mṛtyorbhayāttaṃśaraṇārthinaṃca naṃdīsamāśvāsayadīśabhaktaṃ
naṃdīśvaraṃdānavarāṭsadṛṣṭvā śrutvāmayastaṃśivasaṃprasādaṃ
athāgnirogātripuraṃdidhakṣuḥpradīpayitvāsa kalaṃsamaṃtāt
tamāgataṃviśvakṛtonivāsaṃviśveṃdrayuktaṃjvalanaṃsanaṃdī
naṃdī hutāśaṃsatatotyuvāca mayotratiṣṭhatyamareśabhaktaḥ
taṃva nhirāhāsurarājamāśupurādvinirgacchamayetivākyam
hai maṃgṛhītvāsamaheśaliṃgaṃpurā dviniṣkramyamayosureṃdraḥ
pātālamārtaḥ sahasāpraviṣṭaḥkurvannamaskāra mumāpriyāya
naṃdīśvaraḥ sopisureśapārśvamāga myacākhyāyacasaṃsthitobhūt
tataḥ pradīmaṃtripuraṃbabhūvavissṛṣṭanaṣṭākula vediveśma
vātāyane harmya vimāna saṃsthāśrcaṃdrānanāḥ pīnapayodharāḍhyāḥ
paryaikasuptāmadavivhalākṣyomānaṃ priyānāṃsahavīkṣamāṇāḥ
vilocanaistāmranitāṃtarāgaiḥśyāmāvadātānayanairviśālaiḥ
daityāṃganāstaṃ dadṛśuḥ pradīptamā liṃgyamānāḥśarapāvakena
prasādasaṃsthāḥ prayayurbhayārtāstrāsenakiṃnaryaivācalasthāḥ
priyāstathodvīkṣyasamāgatāṃ stānmohaṃsamāliṃgyabhṛśaṃsmajagmuḥ
priyāgṛhītāditijāstataste praṇaṣṭakāmāstarasābhijagmuḥ
samānaḥ
amareśabhaktaḥ śivabhaktaḥ
ārtaḥ pīḍitaḥ
tāmetitānonitāṃtarāgoyeṣāṃtaiḥ
āliṃgyamānādahyamānāḥ śarapāvakena śaraevapāvakastena
tīvrāśvanakrāmakarāśvaghorāḥ saṃjagrasurnaṣṭabalānvinaṣṭān
jalecarāstāstvapare mahāṃtaḥ saṃcchinnahārāḥ patitāḥ striya stāḥ
hīnāḥ parairbhakṣayituṃ pravṛttāḥ karāladaṃṣṭrāvikṛtānanāstāḥ
tābhakṣyamāṇāḥ patitāstaruṇyaḥ priyāntsaroṣaṃva huśoni rīkṣya
rujāhatānyāḥ paribhidyamānāḥ saṃcukruśurdīnataraṃyuvānaḥ
tāsāṃtadādaityavilāsinīnarijebhṛśaṃ krodhanirīkṣi taṃtat
ratāvasāneparikheditānāṃpriyairivāsāmabhigaṃtukāmaiḥ
sarvetatodaityavṛṣāḥ sabhāryāḥ pradatyamānākhipurānale na
śaraśvasomnīṃdu janārdanātmāpradatyanṛtsnaṃtripuraṃtatomum yathādivyaśarīradhārīcakārassṛṣṭipralayādihetuḥ
daityāhatā statripuraṃ pradagdhaṃśāṃtiḥ kṛtānaśvasurāsureśa
namostu sarvatra sadāsthi tāyasraṣṭrasurāṇāṃpramayeśatubhyaṃ
tānāhadevaḥ satadāsureṃ dvānbrahmārkaviṣṇvidrayameśvarādīn
sadaivayūyaṃ paripālanīyārakṣyāśvadevāḥ sutavatsadaiva
pūrṇābhilāpāhatavidvi paścaprayātadṛṣṭāścaniveśanāni
devāstatodevavaraṃ praṇamyajagmuḥ svakīyāniniveśanāni
devopi sādhyairabhinaṃya mānaḥ kailāsaśṛṃgesa hitogaṇeṃdraiḥ
caṃḍīśanaṃdīśvaravīrabhadrairjagāma kartājagatastrinetraḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ tripuradahane dvipaṃcāśattamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
gatvāhimavataḥ śṛṃgaṃpārvatyāsahitoharaḥ
babhāṣegirijādevaṃ praṇamya parameśvaraṃ
uṃchavatte hiraṇyasyanaimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ
svayamevaprayātāhaṃdvijātpūjāṃpratīcchitum
māhātmyaṃ tasya taddṛṣṭvābrāhmaṇa syatapasvinaḥ
gatārhavismayaṃ devadvijāḥ śreṣṭhatamāiti
devebhyopi garīyāṃsobrāhmaṇāiti me matiḥ
satvaṃnāśayate mohaṃsacāgnau saṃpravartate
vanhitejaḥ sāmātyete mahā tmānodvijātayaḥ
sarvataḥ prabhavaṃtastenāsti teṣāṃnivāraṇam
tapovidyāsa māyuktādārjavaṃtuviśiṣyate
asādhyaṃhaṃtipāpānisamatāmohabaṃdhanam
purābhāgīrathītīreddijaḥparamadharmavit
nāmnādānarucirnāmauṃchavṛttirbabhūvaha
sarvavidyāvinītātmāsarva bhūtābhayapradaḥ
ṣaṣṭhekāletato śnātitasyedaṃvratamutamam
babhūvātyarthamaciṣmānarkānyorapitejasā
tasyaivaṃtapasāvanhiḥ prītastuṣṭimagātparām
gurutuṣṭirbabhūvāsyasamīhitaphalapradaḥ
kadācidathakālena ṣaṣṭhekāle samāgate
nāpaśyadatithiṃkaṃcittapasācasakheditaḥ
yadānāsāditastenadināṃtepyatithiḥkvacit
aprāpyaivatutaṃkaṃcidupavāsaparāyaṇaḥ
patnīcāsya mahābhāgāpatibhaktivratesthitā
yathācāsyāḥ patiścakratathaivāpyakarotsadā
śītavātāditamāṃgonaika dvaṃdvasamāvṛtaḥ
tathāgnistasya taṃ jñātvāniścayaṃ paramaṃ mahat
śvapākasadṛśaṃrūpaṃvikṛtaṃ kutsitaṃ vahiḥ
kṣudhārtoyasa vipreṃdraḥ paryaṭan atithīpsayā
apaśyadṛkṣamūlasthaṃ ghoraṃ vikṛtarūpiṇam
śvapākaśīta saṃkṣubdhaṃnaikatra ṇaśatārditam
vikrośataṃcatātetisacāpaśyadvijottamaḥ
kṛpaṇaṃ taṃ sadādṛṣṭvā svapaṃ tadvijasattamaḥ
śītāpanayanārthacava nhiprajvālayandvijaḥ
viśītaṃvanhisaṃsargātsamāśvastamuvācasaḥ
tamuvācatatodīnaḥ śvapākastapasāṃnidhim
śvapākohaṃdvijaśreṣṭhamatyamannamiva hi
nāhaṃ saṃskṛtamāhartuyogyonnamiticātravīt
tamevaṃvādinaṃdhyānātjñātvāvahnimupasthitam
provācadvijaśārdūlaidaṃva canakovidaḥ
nāhaṃjātiṃ tavārcābhiḥ pūjayāmitavānagha
ātmāvai sarvatojyeṣṭhaḥ sarvaprāṇiṣvayaṃsthitaḥ
ā tmānaṃtamahaṃ bhadrapūjayāmiparaṃśivam
kṛmikīṭādi sarpeṣuśvapākeṣu dvijātiṣu
yadāsarvagatotdyātmātadākutsākathaṃcana
atraśloke eka śvaraṇonopala bhuktvāsaṃskṛtamannaṃtvaṃpāvayāsmānanugrahāt
evamuktodvijeṃdreṇaśvapākaḥ prītimāṃstadā
gṛhaṃgataḥ saviprasyaviprāḥ nugraha lipsayā
vimuktaḥsahapatnyātuprāptavānamṛtaṃ padam
evamārjavasaṃpannobā hmaṇaḥkṛtalakṣaṇaḥ
nakiṃcitprāpnuyāddeviśubhāśubhaparaṃ padam
evaṃ kathitaṃnageṃdratanayemāhātmyamatyuttamaṃ śṛṇvan nityamidaṃpaṭhaṃśvavidhivatsiddhaḥ śucirmānavaḥ
puṇyaṃsaukhya mathāpyabhīpsitaphalaṃtejovalaṃprāpnuyāt
ākhyāna me tatkathitaṃyathāvanmahāmahīdheṃdrasute dvijānām
dṛṣṭaprabhāvāmamatedvijeṃdrā mahāmunīnāṃ padamadhyavātsuḥ
dvijamāhātmyamullikhyapārvatīparameśayoḥ
babhūva caivaṃ saṃvādaḥ puṇyaḥ pāpabhayāvahaḥ
yaccānyadaṃbudaśyāmapā rāśaryatapodhana
śrotavyaṃmanyase mattastatśṭaṇuṣvasamāhitaḥ
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyatripaṃcā śattamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
prāpyapāśupataṃjñā naṃbrahmādyāstesurottamāḥ
lebhireparamaṃtatvaṃjñānaṃcāpimahādyute
kīdṛśaṃ vābhavetyogaṃjñānaṃpāśupataṃśubham
brahmādyā devatāvyāsa dakṣayajñamukhepurā
śaṃkaraṃśaraṇaṃjagmu vīrabhadrabhayārditāḥ
gaṇeṃdrairabhiyuktāstebhasmakūṭājiresthitaiḥ
abhayaṃte tathāraudrāḥpaśavadīkṣitāiva
bhasmarūṣitagātrāṇāṃśaṃkaravratadhāriṇāṃ
svayogaṃcadadau teṣāṃtadādeva umāpatiḥ
sarvāsāṃmokṣavidyānāṃyatratvamitihocyate
dīkṣāṃpāśupatīṃprā pyapraviśaṃtimaheśvaram
nādharme ṇavinādharmonadharmeṇavināśubham
dahetsomakkṛtaṃvanhiriṃ dhanaṃcānalaṃviduḥ
kṛtākṛtaṃdahatyagnirbhūyaḥ somasamāhṛtaḥ
bhasmanāsaṃcitāḥ sarve brahmādyāabhimāninaḥ
bhasmanastejasāvīryayasmātpāvanamīśvaram
ātmānaṃśaṃkaraṃ nyasya yatusnānaṃ bhasmanācaret
prabhavaṃtisurāḥ somātpitarovanhisaṃbhavāḥ
agnīṣomātmakaṃtasmātjaga tsarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
tejasātasya saṃsṛṣṭomucyate bhasmanādvijaḥ
sāṃkhyaṃvi dyāṃtapaścaivatyaktvādharmāśvavaidikān
śīghramevaparaṃyogaṃprāpyamucyatibaṃdhanāt
evaṃtra taṃ mahatprāpyaśū raḥ pāśupatomuniḥ
bhāvaḥ
trīṇiambakāninetrāṇiyasyetivigrahaḥ
tamasāśūnyam
omitye idaṃmāheśvaraṃjñānaṃ gutyaṃparamamabhyaset
jñeyaṃjñānaṃtathājñātātrayaṃdehetathāsthitam
ātmāyaśvayathāvāsosthānatraya samanvitaḥ
nāḍīṣucayathātdyātmāātmanyevāvatiṣṭhati
sarvataḥ sarvabhūteṣunigūḍhastiṣṭhatetathā
nasevituṃvinājñānaṃsamyagātmākathaṃcana
rūpaśabdarasātītaṃ kastaṃ vettimaheśvaram
ta thātyahaṃmahābhāgaprasādātryaṃbakasyatu
ātmajñāneparopāyakathayāmitavānagha
nadevānāsurācaivanadyaḥ sūryaśca caṃdramāḥ
śuddhaṃ mahacca vimala makṣaraṃparamīśvaram
sarvamātraguṇātītaṃ nirvikāraṃniraṃjanam
bahiraṃtaścaraṃdīnamavikāraṃ paraṃ dhruvam
vijñānaṃ paramaṃyattadakṣaraṃbrahmatatśṛṇu
omityekākṣaraṃpūrvākṣaraṃtasmādvinirgatam
yakṣaraśvatrimātraśca oṃkārobrahmaśasya te
akāretatraviṣṇuḥsyātukāretupitāmahaḥ
makāro bhagavānīśomātrāyāṃprakṛtiḥsmṛtā
patnīrūpeṇasāśaṃbhuṃbhuṃ jateprakṛtiṃpunaḥ
brahmaviṣṇū sthitau taucadevāvīśvarasaṃjñitau
saṃpadvirūpaṃ prakṛtiḥ sarvaviṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ
tāvā kramyamaheśastaṃprakṛtistauguṇātmakau
mahāvalovibhurbhūtvānaktaṃsaṃhārameva hi
oṃkāraṃdhyāyatoyenaatītyaprakṛtiṃmune
satamāditya muktātmānṛtārthojāyatemuniḥ
naivaṃjanāvimārgasthāḥ śuddhahetu parāyaṇāḥ
bhoktāraṃprakṛterīśaṃ paraṃtatveṣusaṃsthitam
oṃkāraṃprakṛternityaṃ tanmadhye bhāsvaraṃ svayam
īśvarosaudadātīśaḥsamuktaḥ paśubaṃdhanaiḥ
neśvarāprakṛtiḥkhyātāguṇakarmādibhedinī
bṛhattvāgṛhatīśyāmāviṣṇutvādvibhavāsmṛtā
sābhimānābhavetsṛṣṭirbho ktāṃtasyāmaheśvaraḥ
aṣṭabāhu tripādāca paṃcadehamukhītathā
jaganmātā smṛtātyeṣāguṇatrayavikārajā
ubhe śubhāśubhe tasyāṃ vidyāvidyetathā dyubhe
ubhayārthapramāyāgaḥ kriyānuṣṭhānamevaca
nimittaṃ bhavaneyānetārāḥ saṃkṣepatastvamī
īśvarājjāta oṃkāraḥ sacatasminpratiṣṭhitaḥ
ataḥ kṛtvā mahāyo gaṃyoginaḥkapilādayaḥ
saeva sarvayogātmākāraṇaṃsacaeva tu
īśabhojyauguṇātmānaurutvāviṣṇupitāmahau
saṃsā ratāḍanaumūḍhausarvanityasamāvubhau
īśvaretubhavedvidvānadhyānayogaparāyaṇaḥ
yenāsāvīśvarobhinnoyogenātmanisaṃsthitaḥ
itiśrīśivama hāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃvibhūtiyogonāmacatuṣpaṃcāśattamo'dhyāyaḥ
ātmā sūkṣmo manobuddhirahaṃkāroguṇāstathā
bhūtānīṃdriyasaṃbhārastanmātrāṇidaśānilāḥ
ātmātatrasajīvastusumanaḥsupratiṣṭhitaḥ
tatsvapnasthamitiprāhuḥ saṃsiddhāḥ śivayoginaḥ
jvālinīstimitācosrāvidyāvidyāviśālinī
mālinīśaṃkarī caiva sumitrābodhinītathā
etādaśamahānāḍyo jīvesmiṃstāḥpratiṣṭhitāḥ
śayānaṃpraticohuddhobhāvairbhāṣaiḥ samāhitaḥ
śabdādiviṣayebhyastu ātmasarvagatāstrayaḥ
sadbhi pūrvasaṃyuktaujīvaīkṣayatepunaḥ
ahaṃkāro manobuddhirbhāvaśvatasrodehajāḥ
sahanaiva na tiṣṭhativārayaṃtiśarīriṇaṃ
ta evaṃ vihitāḥ sarve jīvaścaiva tupaṃcamaḥ
kaṇikāyāṃtativyognisaṃsthitaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ
cetaḥ saeva saṃproktaṃsa evapuruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
ahaṃkāropya jāraṃbhabhūtobhāskarasaṃcaraḥ
rasamātmāmahauṣadhyaḥ sānugobhāvavistaraḥ
ahaṃkārogatāśaśvamṭatyuduḥkhamanāmayaṃ
kāmaroṣaja vāduṣṭāḥsudharmāśrābhitāḥsamāḥ
viṣṇurbuddhiryathākāryakāraṇaṃ bhūmirevaca
jñānavairāgyamākāśaṃrāja saṃbhāvavista raṃ
jīvamadhye sthitāsūkṣmāvidhūmāpāvakaṃśikhā
amṭataṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ gatiścaiva hisāparā
madhyetasyāgnisaṃkāśo jīvaḥprotonadṛśyate
sarasālohitāmukhyāprotārasavatītathā
vidhūmācāmṭatācaivanaṃdinībaśnuvistarā
etāḥsūkṣmatarānāḍyaḥsaṃbhidyadaśapāvakaṃ
paryaṭatisadāsomaṃ bhūtādhāraṃpayovataṃ
satābhistarpitaḥ somaḥ sarvāṃtarasa mīpataḥ
śabdāpayativṛddhastāṃjīva madhyāṃgatāṃśivāṃ
tadevāmṛtamākhyātaṃyaccaivātmadamuttamaṃ
tayāyadāhisomasya śikhayākalpitāplavaḥ
jāgartopipunaḥ prājñaḥ sarvayogasanvitaḥ
yābhūteṣusurānāḍīsāsuṣumnā pratiṣṭhitā
bhāvāḥkriyāḥ
ghṛṇāparajugupsā
kuśalaṃmokṣaḥ
kathaṃyogaḥsādhanīyaityāhasa hīti
gamanādyāśvayebhāvāmanasaścaivayāghṛṇā
yatvaṃ kuryādahaṃkārastatjñātvāmaraṇaṃtyajet
nikṣipya cakutaḥ karmatadvinākuśalaṃkutaḥ
yaimeviṣayāḥ kiṃcidvidyāḥ somasyasaṃbhavāḥ
bhoktāvanhiḥsmṛtasteṣāṃtvacā nālpenabādhyate
itijñātvātya jevitāṃ sarvayogarataḥ sadā
dharmavādakṣayaṃ lokānicchāmāṃbadhyatekathaṃ
kriyayāyogaviduṣaḥ śaṃkaraṃ vratamāsthitāḥ
gacchaṃtisvatanuṃtyaktvābhitvāmāyāṃ paraṃpadaṃ
idamanyatparaṃjñānamasyasūkṣmataraṃsphuṭaṃ
yoginoyaṃnajānaṃtiya tasūkṣmaṃparamottamaṃ
muktvāpāśupatānśuddhānyannabhūteṣuvidyate
manobuddhirahaṃkāraiṃdriyāṇiguṇaḥkṣayaṃ
naspṛśaṃti sadātmānaṃvikārāstasyatebahiḥ
sadṛśyate ca bhagavānnatuprāyaḥ kathaṃcana
sarvabhāvaguṇānāṃtamacityaṃ parameśvaraṃ
jñānenayeprapaśyaṃtiyoginasteparāmatāḥ
chāyaiṣāṃ dṛśyateyātu cakṣurviṣayasaṃ gatā
kanīnyaṃtasthitirvyāsa hetuḥ sarvaśarīriṇāṃ
atrāstesasarojñātvāsūkṣmomadhyagatonayaḥ
sahasrakaṇikārya tināḍyojīvecasaṃsthitāḥ
gāṃdhārīvijayācaiva etāḥ prāṇavahāḥ smṛtāḥ
pāṇinātālagaṃdhāyānāḍyaunābhaucasaṃ yute
yogādayodaśoṣmāṃtānāḍyonāgenasaṃbhṛtāḥ
saprāṇobahiraṃtaścatarpayanhavyavāhanaḥ
vṛddhasyavārayeddā yuṃvahan puṃsābalenaca
nāḍītvanyāsuṣumnītisomavanhisvavasthitā
nābhinibaddhāyāṃnābhideśatatāyām
kūrmaḥ pūrvoktovāyuḥ
tasmiṃśvāturake dehe kumārecānalaṃsthitāḥ
śudhyate vātavāsannānityavātatra sāriṇī
samānadhyānasaṃyuktāraktamātmātrapūryate
tadāvāyoḥ parovāyuḥ sacakūrmaihocyate
nāḍyāṃ nābhinibaddhāyāṃ natāyāṃtaupratiṣṭhitau
adharāva dhare nāḍyāṃvāyuralpāstadūrdhvataḥ
adhastātpādasanaddhaḥkūrmaḥśirasicasthitaḥ
yovāyurdevadattākhyaḥ kṛtakāryāyabodhinaḥ
devadattamahānāgalaka kūrmadhanaṃjayāḥ
prāṇāstemayivikhyātāścakrayogābhipālinaḥ
hutaśeṣaṃpradiṣṭaṃvā somaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhati
somaṃvidhitsateyajñānnateṣāṃmuktilakṣaṇam
dīptiragniḥsmṛtāyāṃtusravitaścātrayatrasā
tarpaṇaṃ parvaṇātasya kaṇikāyāṃtadāsmṛtam
netrepaśyatiyajjyotistārārūpaṃprakāśakam
sajīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃā tmānaṃcasamāsthitaḥ
jyotiṣaścakṣuṣaḥ sūkṣmaṃtatvaṃtatparamaṃsmṛtam
taccāmṛtaṃ samākhyātaṃ jñāna labhyaṃtaducyate
tasmā tparataraṃ nāstiyoga vijñānadāgatiḥ
jñātvaivaṃ saṃtyajenmohaṃguṇatrayavikārajam
vimohaṃtyaja saṃsargākriyāḥ kāryāvivarjitāḥ
taṃ viśaṃtimaheśānamīśvaraṃkṛtakāriṇī
ititatvaṃ samākhyātaṃvyāsa māheśvaraṃ tava
tabrahmaparipūrṇatunāmarūpaṃcanāstite
itiśrīśiva mahāpurāṇesanatkumārasaṃhitāyapiṃcapaṃcāśattamo'dhyāyaḥ
vyāsauvāca
ahojñānaṃtvayākhyātamajñānavinivarttanam
adyāhaṃgata saṃde homahādevaṃ paraṃprati
śaṃkarātprakṛtirjātāvahmaviṣṇuśivātmakau
jñātvāṣaḍīśamīśānaṃmucyatesarvabaṃdhanāt
itipaṃcapaṃcāśattamodhyāyaḥ
niṣkalaṃsakalaṃjñātvāsayaeva prakāśate
tvatprasādādahaṃtātaprāptajñānogatā śubhaḥ
niḥsaṃdeho'bhavaṃśāṃtaḥ praṣṭavyaṃ nānyadasti me
tathāpijñāpayāmīdaṃtatvamākhyātumarhasi
evaṃ vijñānasaṃpannaḥprāptayo gomunirmuniṃ
vinākleśaṃtanuṃ tyaktvāyogīyogabalānvitaḥ
īśvara dhyānasaṃprāptamupāyaṃyogalakṣaṇam
kathayasva muniśreṣṭhapraṣṭavyaṃ nānyadasti me
evamuktaḥ saśiṣyeṇavyāsenasumahātmanā
śṛṇuvyāsa paraṃjñānamīśvaradhyānakāraṇam
svecchayā yenamucyaṃteyoginojñānatatparāḥ
svadehaṃvighnavacyatktvāṣaḍūiṃśenayamānu yāt
yānāḍyovāyusaṃrabdhāḥ saṃcaraṃtiśarīriṇaḥ
setustāsāṃtatānāṃtukaṇikāmadhyamāśritāḥ
tamāśri tyatusānāḍībāhyapādeṣusaṃsthitā
smṛtābhūyastuyānāḍyastāekakaramāśritāḥ
niḥsamāne sahasrāṇināḍīnāṃpara mātmani
tāsāmekaikaśobhedaḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmataraḥ smṛtaḥ
tāsusaṃcarateprāṇaḥ karṇikāmadhyasaṃbhavaḥ
tatrātmāsūkṣma saṃ lakṣyaḥ prāguktastiṣṭhatidvija
vidyayādiśipaśyaṃstāstaṃ paśyedyogamāsthitaḥ
tattejaḥ sarvanāḍīṣuvibhaktaṃ sarvadehinā
tāścanāḍyomanaḥsaṃgānmanaḥ kurvativiṣṭutam
tattejaścakṣurāhatya sarvanāḍīsamāśritam
vāyurvarṇajayonāmayothṛdī hasphuretsadā
trīṇitasya mukhānyāhuḥ śironābhirtṛdeva hi
yepramāṇāstavākhyātāvāyavaḥ kīrtitāmayā
mukhānisthānāni
prayogādabhyāsāt
yoginojīvāitisaṃbaṃdhaḥ
śārīraṃśarīrajamityarthaḥ
dhanaṃjayasya te sarve vaśagātannibaṃdhanāḥ
navaśāgaṃtumanyatratasmiṃstiṣṭhatisaṃsthitāḥ
nābhibaṃdhanamāsādyanāḍīcakraṃ samāśritāḥ
dvitīyaṃkarṇikāyāṃtu tṛtīyaṃ tālusaṃsthitam
vikāraparaṃśūlaṃtrividhotkrāṃtirucyate
hṛdiśūlaṃpa raṃnāḍyāṃtālaparaśurāsthitaḥ
tāsu kehadibaddhaśvapadmanāḍyāṃniyojitaḥ
bhānauviyojitaṃ sarvaṃ prāṇamevavimuṃcati
ākṣipyatritayaṃnāḍyāṃkaṇikāyāṃniyojanam
yayājīvānabādhyaṃ yoginastadidaṃśṭaṇu bālyaḥśarīrajaścetismṛtyurdvividhaucyate
vātyomṭatyuritikhyātaḥśārīraṃ tunibodhame
kālajojarayāyuktorogajovyādhisaṃjñitaḥ
yogopāyarutoyaśvayaścakālakṛtaḥkṣayaḥ
tayorbhedādhikārauvābhṭaṇuvyāsa samāsataḥ
yogamākrāmataḥśabdaḥ śrūyate śrotrasaṃdhijaḥ
śabdasparśoguṇātītorūpayogaṃvimuṃca ti
udānonāmasaṃyujya karṇikāyāṃviśaṃtihi
iṃdri yāṇimanoyāṃtimanaḥprāṇavinirgatam
teṣu sarveṣulīneṣuprāṇavāyuṃnipīḍayet
pīḍyamānāstataḥ sarve bhavatyekaśa tānilāḥ
susaṃyuktaṃtataḥ sthānaṃtataḥ karmayadātmakam
ekasthāvāyavaḥ sarve pūrayaṃtidhanaṃjayam
śeṣastadīya kūrmādyājīvaṃtyaktvāsatiṣṭhati
ekakālakṛtātyeṣāsarvabhūtaguṇasthitiḥ
samāsataḥ saṃkṣepataḥ
yogamākrāmatoyogābhyāsinaḥ
śa bdayogātśabdasaṃbaṃdhāt
anitājīvitāḥ
karaṇaiḥ kriyābhiḥsaha
sukhaṃkalyāṇam
brahmabhiḥ sadyojātādibhiḥ
niṣkalaṃnirguṇam
churikāṃparaśvāpiśūlaṃvādhārayenmuniḥ
tataḥ sarvevilīyaṃtevikārāḥ karaṇaiḥ saha
yadānapaṃcavijñāyaddaṣṭvātupariniṣṭhitaḥ
paṃcabhirbrahmabhiḥpūtobhasmanādīkṣitodvijaḥ
śaṃkaraikamanāyogījñānametadavāpnute
māheśvarabhimaṃyogaṃniṣkalaṃmukti kāraṇam
yajñādapinamuṃcativratamaprāpyaśāṃkaraṃ
mahādevaparobhūtvā sarvajñānamavāpnuhi
naivāmatyāparaṃbrahma anyeviṃdaṃtiyoginaḥ
mahādevaprasādenanamuktāḥ śivayoginaḥ
mahādevasyavakṣyāmitadbhaktyāyenayāṃti hi
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃyogadhyāne ṣaṭpaṃcāśattamo'dhyāyaḥ
tkumārauvāca
bhūtabhavyabhavānāṃcasaptānāmūrdhvataḥsthitāḥ
lokābhagava taḥśaṃbhoryatrāstesatataṃśivaḥ
nāsautarkavinirdeśyolokāsta sminpratiṣṭhitāḥ
brahmāṃḍaṃsakalaṃtasmiṃcchivaloke pratiṣṭhitam
nāsaunaśyatisaṃhāredhruvasthānaṃsurālayaḥ
yatrāhaṃsanakādyāśca brahmācaivapitāmahaḥ
oṃnamaḥ śivāya yeṣulokeṣu bhagavānsaṃsthitogirijāpatiḥ
yakṛtoyaścakālakṣayāgataḥ
tayorbhedavikārāṇiśṭaṇuvyāsasamāhitaḥ
yoyamātheṣajaḥśabdanupeta vālakhilyapurogāśvasiddhāśvakāpilādayaḥ
śivayogaṃpariprāptāḥ satvādiguṇavarjitāḥ
niṣkāmāniṣṭhitāvyāsa se vamānāśvaīśvaram
paramātmācabhāvosaupara mosaumanīṣiṇām
kṣamāsatyaṃ dhṛtiścaivatapovairāgyamevaca
viṣṇutvaṃcavidhātṛtvamādyabodhomaheśatā
ataḥparaṃparodivyeparamāṇoḥpadesthitaḥ
manasaḥprākṛtasyādautattejaḥ saṃprakāśanaḥ
mahāṃtaḥsarvatonityāīśvarāttadabhūttadā
tasmāddijasyanirbhedaḥkṣatrataḥ savibhuḥ smṛtaḥ
prakṛtirvaiṣṇavīpro ktāsācatasmādvinirgatā
amuṣyapuratobrahmābrahmaṇaḥ śaṃkarātmanaḥ
yatsthānaṃvigraheśasya īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ
nāmnāśivapuraṃvyāsa gatirīśvarayogināṃ
śataṃśatasahasrāṇāṃ yojanānāṃ taducyate
mahāmaṃḍalasaṃsthānaṃ tanmadhyevimalaṃ śubham
mahatājātarūpeṇaprākāreṇasaveṣṭitaḥ
śataṃśatasahasrāṇāṃ yojanānāṃyathādiśam
divyā marāvatī bhūmiḥsparśamātra sukhāvahā
vimaleṃduvikāśānivālārkasadṛśāni ca
mahākradapramāṇāninānāvaidūryasannibhāḥ
gaṃdhavaṃti mahārhāṇivinyastāni mahītale
iṃdranī lanikāśāni mahāmaṇinibhānica
kvacitkṛṣṇāniraktānidivyagaṃdhavahānica
kāṃtānirejiretatra utpatrāṇisamaṃta taḥ
purebhagavataḥśaṃbhoḥ parivāryanivodhatāḥ
varadācavareṇyācavareśā varavarṇini
varāhavāribhadrācavarācaiva mahāpagā
nānākusumasaṃmiśra bahutānijalāmṛtam
nadevānamunīṃdrāśva nāsurāḥpaśavonaca
aṃtarbhāvaviśuddhāyesarvatobhaktibhāvitāḥ
meruśṛṃgapratīkāśodṛśyatecapunaḥ punaḥ
prāsādonakṣapādistukāmadaḥ kanakāmayaḥ
anirīkṣyomahālubdhaiḥ samaṃtātpariśobhitaḥ
vaiḍūryavyomasaṃkā śaiḥ sphaṭikaiścaṃdrasaprabhaiḥ
pravālairarkasaṃkāśairiṃdranīlamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ
śikhirasmiprakāśābhiḥkvacidarkasvarūpibhiḥ
śobhitaṃtupatākābhirvirarājasukhānilam
śuśubhetatpuraṃdivyaṃpādapaiḥ kā madaiśvitam
yathaivakāṃcanomeruḥ sarveṣāṃpravaromahān
tatraviśveśvaraḥsā kṣānmahābhūtaparigrahaḥ
sadāstesahitaḥ patyāṣaḍūiṃśaḥ saparigrahaḥ
lakṣmīrmedhādhṛtiścaiva śrīḥ kīrtiśvasarasvatī
umayāmahitāstatra modate lokamātaraḥ tāstāmunīśvarādivyārūpiṇyoyogasaṃyutāḥ
gaṇānāmadhipāstatrakunavāmanarūpiṇaḥ
kāmarūpāmahāveśāmahāyogaparāyaṇāḥ
pramathānāṃmahātmāna statratiṣṭhaṃtisuvratāḥ
mahākāleśvarastatranaṃdīśvaragaṇeśvarau
gṛhītapaṭṭiśaudivyausadevaudevapārśvagau
devyāḥ pārśvesthitenityaṃ asihaste mahābale
kakudmīca mahānādomahā nīśvaravāhanaḥ
tatrāstemeghasaṃkāśogopatiḥ kāmarūpadhṛk
ghaṃṭāśaktidharaḥ śrīmānpitṛpārśvevyavasthitaḥ
śākha ścaivaviśākhaśvanaigamīcaivasuvrata
kumārāśvasthitāpārśvalokānugrahahetavaḥ
daśasūryasahasrāṇirathesūkṣme jagatpa teḥ
śārdūlāḥkāṃcanāstatra siṃhāśvarajataprabhāḥ
prājñānāṃmaṇitulyānāṃmahāyogabalaujasāṃ
asaṃkhyātāḥ ttamaḥ
sakalāṃkogṛheśasya de vadevajagatsṛjaḥ
sarvabhāvārpitātmānoyeyogārudratatparāḥ
yatrata tramṭatāvatsateṣāṃtatrāspadaṃ smṛtaṃ
yecamāheśvarāvyāsatiṣṭhateśaṃkarālaye
anyeyeśaṃkarebhaktāstāncchṛṇuṣvasamāhi taḥ
ahaṃsanaṃdanaścaivasanakaśvasanātanaḥ
dhātābrahmāsatu jyeṣṭhonaranārāyaṇāvapi
munirhayaśirāyaśvayājñavalkyādayastathā
ṛṣayaḥ śukadharmāṇaḥ paramaiśvaryasaṃyutāḥ
tiṣṭhatīśvaramūletuguṇātītā didṛkṣavaḥ
īśvaraṃtesa māviśyaprāpnuvaṃtyāparāhnikaṃ
yaiśvadṛṣṭānivipreṃdrahara syāyatanānitu
mahākāleśvaraścaiva gokarṇaśvatathāśubhau
vaikarṇa śveśvarodevaḥśrīgirauvāmaheśvaraḥ
kārohane cadeveśomahākālecaśaṃkaraḥ
bhadreśaśvamahādevaḥśabdakarṇeśvarastathā
mahākāleśvaraścaivagokarṇecatathāśubhau
avimukteca oṃkāraṃyaiśvadṛṣṭaṃmahāmune
tepiyāṃtiṣṭatāḥ kāle purecagiri jāpateḥ
yogaḥpāśupatoyasya mayāte parikīrtitaḥ
bhaktiryeṣāṃ bhaveni tyaṃkṛtārthāstenarottamāḥ
mṛtāḥ śivapurevyāsabhikṣāpaṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ
naṃdīśaskaṃdasaṃkāśāyogaiśvaryabalānvitāḥ
rudrābhavaṃtivipreṃdrasadāśaṃkarapārśvagāḥ
sakalaṃcaivajñātvaivaṃvijñāyaparame śvaraṃ
bhaviṣyasicayogīcajñānasyāsya prabhāvataḥ
jñānasitdhyāsmṛtiṃprāpyabrahmāṃḍodbhavakāraṇe
sthitidharmanirodhānāṃ purāṇaṃcakari ṣyasi
vijñānārthamanusmṛtyacaturdhāvikariṣyasi
tvatkṛtāḥ prakariṣyaṃtitīrthakṛttvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
tasmādrataṃcasaṃprāpyapaśupā śavimocanaṃ
śaṃkarajñānasaṃpannaīśvarelayamāpsyasi
tatkṣaṇāccāsyayogosau prādurbhūto mahāmuneḥ
abhivādyaguruṃcyāsobrahmaputraṃ mahātapāḥ
savāyatenadīkṣārthaṃ viveśacamahītalaṃ
evaṃ sanatkumārastupṛṣṭovyāsena dhīmatā
munīṃdrakathayāmāsapurāṇaṃśivasaṃbha vaṃ
śivayogadharaṃ dhīraṃ sarvajñānārṇavaṃ mahat
tasmādyūyamapiprāpyavrataṃpāśu pataṃdvijāḥ
vedārtha smṛtisaṃpannaścitāścakre mahādyutiḥ
purāṇaṃprathamaṃ prāha ślāghyaṃnaṃdīśvaroddi jaḥ
kṛtsnasyajagatovidyāsvādi kartāyathāharaḥ
tathāsarva purāṇānāṃ purāṇoyaṃparaḥ smṛtaḥ
mṛtyukālamanuprāpyanateśocaṃtijanminaḥ
śravaṇāddevadevasyasāyujyaṃdhā raṇādvibhoḥ
ślāghyātpuṇyamumāpaterhijagatāṃstotrānuvādaṃ paraṃ devyāśvā vitaṃ
śaṃbhāvarpitasarvabhāva hṛdayaiyaiyaira yaṃsevitaḥ sarvetejvaladarkavanhivapuṣaruyakṣāḥśaśāṃkatviṣaḥ
devasyānucarāścatu daśavarānirmuktasarvāśubhāḥ sarve harṣasamanvitāḥśrutadhiyonānāguṇairanvitāḥ
tataihaparamaṃprāpyayogaṃmunīṃdrāḥ parama paramanaṃtaṃprāpyadevādhivāsaṃ
tripuraharamimaṃ yejñātavaṃtaḥprayatnādgatakaluṣacayāsteprāpnuvatecamokṣaṃ
idaṃ purāṇaṃ paramaṃ pavitraṃśuciḥpaṭhedyaḥśṛṇuyāccayonaraḥ
pitṝṇāṃ tidaṃśrāddhepaṭhyamānamidaṃbhavet
duṣṭasvapnādiduṣkarma kalikalmaṣanāśanaṃ
adhītecāsyayaḥ ślokaṃślokārthaivāsa māhitaḥ
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyāṃ saptapaṃcāśa ttamo'dhyāyaḥ
samāpteyaṃsaṃhitā
bhāvanaikavaśaṃdevaṃbhavānīsahitaṃbhavam
iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitā samāptā
